### [1] [Next-to-next-to-leading QCD corrections to the $\mathbf{B^+}$-$\mathbf{B_d^0}$, $\mathbf{D^+}$-$\mathbf{D^0}$, and $\mathbf{D_s^+}$-$\mathbf{D^0}$ lifetime ratios](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24841)
*Francesco Moretti,Ulrich Nierste,Pascal Reeck,Matthias Steinhauser*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper calculates the three-loop contributions of order $\alpha_s^2/m_Q^3$ to the lifetime ratios of heavy mesons, and presents new $\alpha_s/m_Q^3$ corrections. The results are in good agreement with experimental data, providing a successful test of the calculations of hadronic matrix elements and allowing for estimates of unknown higher-order terms.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to systematically calculate the total decay widths of heavy mesons using an expansion in the parameters $1/m_Q$ and $\alpha_s(m_Q)$. The focus is on the dominant contributions to meson lifetime splittings, which are suppressed by $1/m_Q^3$ relative to the leading universal contribution. The aim is to provide precise theoretical predictions that can be compared with experimental data to test the validity of the theoretical framework and to estimate higher-order contributions.

Method: The method involves calculating three-loop contributions of order $\alpha_s^2/m_Q^3$ to the lifetime ratios $\tau(B^+)/\tau(B_d^0)$, $\tau(D^+)/\tau(D^0)$, and $\tau(D_s^+)/\tau(D^0)$ in the limit of exact isospin and V-spin symmetry. Additionally, new $\alpha_s/m_Q^3$ corrections to the Cabibbo-suppressed terms in $\tau(B^+)/\tau(B_d^0)$ are presented. The perturbative coefficients are combined with hadronic matrix elements calculated from Heavy Quark Effective Theory (HQET) sum rules and lattice QCD calculations.

Result: The results include the following lifetime ratios: $\tau(B^+)/\tau(B_d^0) = 1.072 \pm 0.024$, $\tau(D^+)/\tau(D^0) = 2.344 \pm 0.170$, and $\tau(D_s^+)/\tau(D^0) = 1.289 \pm 0.042$. These predictions are in good agreement with experimental data, validating the theoretical calculations and allowing for estimates of the unknown $1/m_Q^4$ contributions and V-spin breaking terms in $\tau(D_s^+)/\tau(D^0)$.

Conclusion: The study successfully calculates the three-loop contributions and new corrections to the lifetime ratios of heavy mesons, which are in good agreement with experimental data. This provides a strong validation of the theoretical framework used, including the HQET sum rules and lattice QCD calculations. The results also allow for the estimation of higher-order contributions, such as $1/m_Q^4$ terms and V-spin breaking effects.

Abstract: The total decay widths of heavy mesons can be systematically calculated in terms of an expansion in the two parameters $1/m_Q$ and $α_s(m_Q)$, where $Q=c,b$ denotes the heavy quark. The dominant contributions to meson lifetime splittings stem from terms which are suppressed by $1/m_Q^3$ with respect to the leading universal contribution to the total decay width. We calculate three-loop contributions of order $α_s^2/m_q^3$ to the lifetime ratios $τ(B^+)/τ(B_d^0)$, $τ(D^+)/τ(D^0)$, and $τ(D_s^+)/τ(D^0)$ in the limit of exact isospin and V-spin symmetry, respectively. Furthermore, we present new $α_s/m_q^3$ corrections to the Cabibbo-suppressed terms in $τ(B^+)/τ(B_d^0)$. Combining our perturbative coefficients with hadronic matrix elements calculated from Heavy Quark Effective Theory sum rules, we find $τ(B^+)/τ(B_d^0)= {1.072 \pm 0.024 }$. Using hadronic matrix elements from a recent lattice QCD calculation we find $τ(D^+)/τ(D^0)={2.344 \pm 0.170} $ and $τ(D_s^+)/τ(D^0)={1.289 \pm 0.042}$. We find good agreement of our predictions with experimental data, which constitutes a successful probe of the calculations of hadronic matrix elements and permits estimates of the unknown $1/m_Q^4$ contributions as well as the V-spin breaking terms in $τ(D_s^+)/τ(D^0)$.

</details>


### [2] [Accidental Peccei-Quinn Symmetry from Chiral Gauge Symmetry and Mirror QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24849)
*Hajime Fukuda,Keisuke Harigaya*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper proposes a solution to the strong CP problem using a chiral U(1) gauge symmetry, which leads to an accidental Peccei-Quinn symmetry. This framework avoids massless fermions and a light QCD axion, and it allows for a high reheating temperature suitable for leptogenesis. The model also predicts gravitational waves and a WIMP dark matter candidate, with the chiral U(1) gauge boson serving as a vector portal to the Standard Model.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The strong CP problem is addressed by introducing a chiral U(1) gauge symmetry that results in an accidental Peccei-Quinn symmetry. This approach aims to resolve the issue without invoking massless fermions or a light QCD axion, while also avoiding stable domain walls and colored relics. The model is designed to be compatible with a high reheating temperature, necessary for leptogenesis, and to provide a viable WIMP dark matter candidate. Additionally, the model predicts the existence of metastable domain walls and a first-order mirror QCD phase transition, which can generate primordial gravitational waves.\n\n强CP问题通过引入一个手征U(1)规范对称性来解决，这导致了一个偶然的Peccei-Quinn对称性。这种方法旨在不引入无质量费米子或轻QCD轴子的情况下解决问题，同时避免稳定的畴壁和有色遗迹。该模型设计为与高重加热温度兼容，这是轻子生成所必需的，并提供一个可行的WIMP暗物质候选者。此外，该模型预测了亚稳态畴壁和一阶镜像QCD相变的存在，这可以产生原初引力波。

Method: The method involves constructing a theoretical framework based on a chiral U(1) gauge symmetry, which accidentally gives rise to a Peccei-Quinn symmetry. This symmetry is both explicitly and spontaneously broken by mirror QCD dynamics. The breaking of the symmetry leads to the absence of massless fermions and a light QCD axion. The model also includes a mechanism for generating a stochastic background of primordial gravitational waves through metastable domain walls and a first-order mirror QCD phase transition. A pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone boson (pNGB) serves as a WIMP dark matter candidate, and the chiral U(1) gauge boson provides a vector portal to the Standard Model.\n\n方法涉及构建基于手征U(1)规范对称性的理论框架，该对称性偶然地产生了Peccei-Quinn对称性。这种对称性通过镜像QCD动力学被显式和自发地破坏。对称性的破坏导致没有无质量费米子和轻QCD轴子。该模型还包括通过亚稳态畴壁和一阶镜像QCD相变产生原初引力波随机背景的机制。伪Nambu-Goldstone玻色子（pNGB）作为WIMP暗物质候选者，而手征U(1)规范玻色子提供了到标准模型的矢量门户。

Result: The result is a consistent theoretical framework that resolves the strong CP problem without the need for massless fermions or a light QCD axion. The model accommodates a high reheating temperature, making it compatible with leptogenesis. It also predicts the existence of metastable domain walls and a first-order mirror QCD phase transition, leading to a stochastic background of primordial gravitational waves. One of the pNGBs in the model serves as a WIMP dark matter candidate, and the chiral U(1) gauge boson acts as a vector portal to the Standard Model.\n\n结果是一个一致的理论框架，解决了强CP问题，而不需要无质量费米子或轻QCD轴子。该模型容纳了高重加热温度，使其与轻子生成兼容。它还预测了亚稳态畴壁和一阶镜像QCD相变的存在，导致原初引力波的随机背景。模型中的一个pNGB充当WIMP暗物质候选者，而手征U(1)规范玻色子充当到标准模型的矢量门户。

Conclusion: The proposed model successfully addresses the strong CP problem and provides a framework that is free from massless fermions and a light QCD axion. It is consistent with a high reheating temperature, allowing for leptogenesis, and predicts a stochastic background of primordial gravitational waves. The model also offers a viable WIMP dark matter candidate and a vector portal to the Standard Model via the chiral U(1) gauge boson.\n\n提出的模型成功地解决了强CP问题，并提供了一个没有无质量费米子和轻QCD轴子的框架。它与高重加热温度一致，允许轻子生成，并预测了原初引力波的随机背景。该模型还提供了一个可行的WIMP暗物质候选者，并通过手征U(1)规范玻色子提供了到标准模型的矢量门户。

Abstract: We present a solution to the strong CP problem in which a simple chiral U(1) gauge symmetry gives rise to an accidental Peccei-Quinn symmetry that is both explicitly and spontaneously broken by mirror QCD dynamics, yielding a framework without massless fermions or a light QCD axion. The model contains no stable domain walls or colored relics, and it accommodates a sufficiently high reheating temperature to account for the baryon asymmetry of the Universe via leptogenesis. Metastable domain walls and first-order mirror QCD phase transition generate a stochastic background of primordial gravitational waves. Additionally, one of the pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone bosons serves as a viable WIMP dark matter candidate. The gauge boson associated with the chiral U(1) gauge symmetry, which kinetically mixes with the Standard Model hypercharge gauge boson, provides a vector portal connecting dark matter to the Standard Model and plays a central role in the dark-matter phenomenology. Colored pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone bosons can be probed at the LHC through searches for dijet resonances, jets plus missing energy, multijet events with leptons, and displaced vertices.

</details>


### [3] [The Angular Observables of $Λ_b \to Λ_c(\to Λ^0 π^+) \, τ^-(\to π^- ν_τ)\, \barν_τ$ within the Paradigm of FCCC Anomalies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24922)
*Muhammad Arslan,Ishtiaq Ahmed,Muhammad Jamil Aslam*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper analyzes the $B$-meson flavor anomalies and extends the study to baryonic decays, particularly $Λ_b^0 \to Λ_c^+ τ^- \barν_τ$. The analysis reveals significant deviations from SM predictions, with the $(C_{V_L}, C_{S_R})$ scenario being the most favored NP solution. Angular observables in the five-fold $Λ_b$ decay show high sensitivity to NP effects, and specific scenarios exhibit correlations that suggest CP-violating or CP-conserving dynamics.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to investigate the lepton flavor universality (LFU) ratios $R_{τ/(μ,e)}(D^{(*)})$ which show a combined $3.8σ$ deviation from Standard Model (SM) predictions. By extending the analysis to the baryonic sector, specifically the decay $Λ_b^0 \to Λ_c^+ τ^- \barν_τ$, the authors aim to explore new physics (NP) solutions and their impact on angular observables.

动机是研究轻子味普适性（Lepton Flavor Universality, LFU）比值 $R_{τ/(μ,e)}(D^{(*)})$，这些比值与标准模型（Standard Model, SM）预测相比显示出联合的 $3.8σ$ 偏差。通过将分析扩展到重子部门，特别是衰变 $Λ_b^0 \to Λ_c^+ τ^- \barν_τ$，作者旨在探索新物理（New Physics, NP）解及其对角分布可观测的影响。

Method: The method involves a global analysis of the current $B$-meson flavor anomalies using the latest HFLAV averages and $B_c$-lifetime constraints. The authors extend this analysis to the baryonic sector through the cascade decay $Λ_b^0 \to Λ_c^+ τ^- \barν_τ$. They use Lattice-QCD form factors to study the impact of NP operators on a complete set of angular observables in the five-fold $Λ_b$ decay. Correlation analysis is performed to identify patterns in the NP scenarios.

方法涉及使用最新的HFLAV平均值和$B_c$寿命约束对当前$B$介子味异常进行全局分析。作者通过级联衰变 $Λ_b^0 \to Λ_c^+ τ^- \barν_τ$ 将这种分析扩展到重子部门。他们使用格点QCD形式因子来研究NP算符对五重$Λ_b$衰变中完整角可观测量集的影响。还进行了相关性分析以识别NP场景中的模式。

Result: The results indicate that the $(C_{V_L}, C_{S_R})$ scenario is the most favored NP solution, showing the largest deviation from the SM and insensitivity to branching-ratio constraints. The angular observables $\mathcal{K}_{1c}$, $\mathcal{K}_{2ss}$, $\mathcal{K}_{2cc}$, and $\mathcal{K}_{4s}$ are highly sensitive to NP effects. The correlation analysis shows inverse and direct correlations among these observables, suggesting possible CP-violating or CP-conserving dynamics.

结果表明，$(C_{V_L}, C_{S_R})$ 场景是最受青睐的新物理解，显示出与标准模型最大的偏差，并且对分支比约束不敏感。角可观测量 $\mathcal{K}_{1c}$, $\mathcal{K}_{2ss}$, $\mathcal{K}_{2cc}$ 和 $\mathcal{K}_{4s}$ 对新物理效应高度敏感。相关性分析显示这些可观测量之间存在反向和正向相关性，表明可能存在CP破坏或CP守恒动力学。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that baryonic semileptonic decays, such as $Λ_b^0 \to Λ_c^+ τ^- \barν_τ$, provide a powerful and independent probe of the $R_{τ/(μ,e)}(D^{(*)})$ anomalies. The identified NP scenarios, particularly $(C_{V_L}, C_{S_R})$ and $(\Re[C_{S_L}=4C_T], \Im[C_{S_L}=4C_T])$, generate significant deviations from the SM predictions and exhibit distinct correlation patterns. Future measurements will be crucial for testing the underlying NP structure.

结论是，如 $Λ_b^0 \to Λ_c^+ τ^- \barν_τ$ 的重子半轻子衰变为 $R_{τ/(μ,e)}(D^{(*)})$ 异常提供了有力且独立的探针。已确定的新物理场景，特别是 $(C_{V_L}, C_{S_R})$ 和 $(\Re[C_{S_L}=4C_T], \Im[C_{S_L}=4C_T])$，产生了与标准模型预测显著的偏差，并表现出独特的相关模式。未来的测量对于测试潜在的新物理结构至关重要。

Abstract: We present a global analysis of the current $B$-meson flavor anomalies and extend it to the baryonic sector through the decay $Λ_b^0 \to Λ_c^+(\to Λ^0 π^+) τ^-(\to π^- ν_τ)\barν_τ$. The lepton flavor universality ratios $R_{τ/(μ,e)}(D^{(*)})$, measured by BaBar, Belle, and LHCb, exhibit a combined $3.8σ$ deviation from Standard Model (SM) predictions. Using the latest HFLAV averages and $B_c$-lifetime constraints, $\mathcal{B}(B_c \to τν) < 60\%, 30\%, 10\%$, found new physics (NP) solutions to the cascade decay $Λ_b^0 \to Λ_c^+(\to Λ^0 π^+) τ^-(\to π^- ν_τ)\barν_τ$. The scenario $(C_{V_L},C_{S_R})$ emerges as the most favored NP solution, largest pull from the SM and insensitive to branching-ratio constraints; followed by $C_{V_L}$ case. We study the impact of NP operators on a complete set of angular observables on the five-fold $Λ_b$ decay using Lattice-QCD form factors and find that the scenarios $(\Re[C_{S_L}=4C_T],\Im[C_{S_L}=4C_T])$ and $(C_{S_L},C_{S_R})$ generate the largest deviations from the SM predictions. In particular, the observables $\mathcal{K}_{1c}$, $\mathcal{K}_{2ss}$, $\mathcal{K}_{2cc}$, and $\mathcal{K}_{4s}$ show the highest sensitivity to NP effects. The correlation analysis reveals the $(\Re[C_{S_L}=4C_T],\Im[C_{S_L}=4C_T])$ scenario exhibits inverse correlations among $\mathcal{K}_{1c}$ and $\mathcal{K}_{2ss,2cc,4s}$ and direct correlations between $\mathcal{K}_{2ss}$ and $\mathcal{K}_{2cc,4s}$, pointing to a possible CP-violating phase, while the $(C_{S_L},C_{S_R})$ scenario displays complementary behavior consistent with CP-conserving dynamics. These results establish baryonic semileptonic decays as a powerful and independent probe of the $R_{τ/(μ,e)}(D^{(*)})$ anomalies, with future measurements providing critical tests of the underlying NP structure.

</details>


### [4] [Forward backward CP asymmetry in $τ^- \to K πν_τ$ in the Left-Right Inverse seesaw model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24924)
*David Delepine,Shaaban Khalil*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper investigates CP-violating effects in $\tau \to K\pi\nu_\tau$ decays within the Left--Right Inverse Seesaw (LRIS) model. While the integrated CP asymmetry is too small to explain the BaBar result, a significant signal in the differential forward--backward CP asymmetry, $A_{\rm CP}^{\rm FB}(s)$, is predicted. The dominant non-decoupling scalar operator, $g_S$, enhances $A_{\rm CP}^{\rm FB}(s)$ through interference with the SM vector current, leading to distinctive kinematic features near the $K^*(892)$ and $K_0^*(1430)$ resonances.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Recent measurements by the BaBar collaboration of the integrated CP asymmetry in $\tau \to K\pi\nu_\tau$ decays show a $2.8\sigma$ deviation from the Standard Model (SM) prediction. This deviation motivates the investigation of new physics models, such as the Left--Right Inverse Seesaw (LRIS) model, to understand the observed anomaly and to predict new observables that could be tested in future experiments.

Method: The authors derive the effective $|\Delta S| = 1$ Hamiltonian relevant for $\tau \to K\pi\nu_\tau$ decays in the LRIS model. They identify a dominant non-decoupling scalar operator, $g_S$, generated by a top-quark flavor-changing neutral current box diagram involving heavy neutrinos and scalar exchange. The numerical analysis includes the interference between the SM vector current and the new scalar operator, focusing on the differential forward--backward CP asymmetry, $A_{\rm CP}^{\rm FB}(s)$. The analysis also examines the kinematic features near the $K^*(892)$ and $K_0^*(1430)$ resonances.

Result: The results show that while the integrated CP asymmetry remains too small to account for the BaBar result, the differential forward--backward CP asymmetry, $A_{\rm CP}^{\rm FB}(s)$, is significantly enhanced due to the interference between the SM vector current and the new scalar operator, $g_S$. This leads to distinctive kinematic features near the $K^*(892)$ and $K_0^*(1430)$ resonances, providing a sensitive probe of the LRIS scalar sector.

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that the LRIS model predicts a pronounced signal in the differential forward--backward CP asymmetry, $A_{\rm CP}^{\rm FB}(s)$, which could be tested in current and future flavor experiments, particularly at Belle~II. Although the integrated CP asymmetry is not large enough to explain the BaBar result, the differential observables provide a promising avenue to explore new physics beyond the SM.

Abstract: Recent measurements of the integrated CP asymmetry in $τ\to Kπν_τ$ decays by the BaBar collaboration exhibit a $2.8σ$ deviation from the Standard Model (SM) prediction. In this work, we investigate CP-violating effects in $τ\to Kπν_τ$ within the model of the Left--Right Inverse Seesaw (LRIS) model. We show that, although the integrated asymmetry remains too small to account for the BaBar result, the model nevertheless predicts a pronounced signal in the \emph{differential} forward--backward CP asymmetry, $A_{\rm CP}^{\rm FB}(s)$. We derive the effective $|ΔS| = 1$ Hamiltonian relevant for these decays and identify a dominant non-decoupling scalar operator, $g_S$, generated by a top-quark flavor-changing neutral current box diagram involving heavy neutrinos and scalar exchange. Our numerical analysis demonstrates that, while this contribution largely cancels in the integrated $A_{\rm CP}$, it significantly enhances $A_{\rm CP}^{\rm FB}(s)$ through interference with the SM vector current, leading to distinctive kinematic features near the $K^*(892)$ and $K_0^*(1430)$ resonances. These angular and differential observables provide a sensitive probe of the LRIS scalar sector at current and future flavor experiments, in particular Belle~II.

</details>


### [5] [Muon $g$$-$$2$: correlation-induced uncertainties in precision data combinations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25004)
*Alexander Keshavarzi,Daisuke Nomura,Thomas Teubner,Aidan Wright*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: A systematic framework is introduced to quantify uncertainties from imperfectly known systematic correlations in combined data. Applied to $e^+e^- \rightarrow \mathrm{hadrons}$ cross section data, it provides robust estimates of correlation-induced uncertainties, which are found to be subdominant but non-negligible. The method is applicable to precision measurements and will be part of the upcoming KNTW data combination for $a_\mu^\mathrm{HVP}$.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to develop a general and systematic approach to handle uncertainties arising from imperfectly known systematic correlations in combined datasets. This is crucial for precision measurements, such as the determination of the hadronic vacuum polarization (HVP) contribution to the muon anomalous magnetic moment, $a_\mu^\mathrm{HVP}$. Accurate quantification of these uncertainties is necessary to ensure the reliability of the results.

动机是开发一种通用且系统的方法来处理组合数据集中由于系统相关性不完全已知而产生的不确定性。这对于精密测量非常重要，例如确定强子真空极化（HVP）对μ子反常磁矩$a_\mu^\mathrm{HVP}$的贡献。准确量化这些不确定性对于确保结果的可靠性是必要的。

Method: The method is formulated at the level of the combined data, allowing for controlled variation of the correlation structure. This leads to the construction of covariance matrices directly on the resulting combination, providing a robust and systematic estimate of correlation-induced uncertainties. The method is applied to $e^+e^- \rightarrow \mathrm{hadrons}$ cross section data, and the resulting covariance matrices are propagated to derived observables, including dispersive determinations of the HVP contribution to $a_\mu^\mathrm{HVP}$.

该方法是在组合数据的层面上制定的，允许对相关结构进行受控的变化。这导致了直接在组合结果上构建协方差矩阵，从而提供了相关性引起的不确定性的稳健和系统的估计。该方法应用于$e^+e^- \rightarrow \mathrm{hadrons}$截面数据，并将所得协方差矩阵传播到导出的可观测值，包括HVP对$a_\mu^\mathrm{HVP}$的色散确定。

Result: The application of the method to $e^+e^- \rightarrow \mathrm{hadrons}$ cross section data reveals that uncertainties from systematic correlation assumptions are generally subdominant but non-negligible. These uncertainties do not fully account for differences between existing $e^+e^- \rightarrow \mathrm{hadrons}$ data combinations. The method is shown to be broadly applicable to correlated data combinations in precision measurements.

将该方法应用于$e^+e^- \rightarrow \mathrm{hadrons}$截面数据表明，系统相关性假设带来的不确定性通常是次要的但不可忽略。这些不确定性并不能完全解释现有$e^+e^- \rightarrow \mathrm{hadrons}$数据组合之间的差异。该方法被证明广泛适用于精密测量中的相关数据组合。

Conclusion: The proposed framework provides a robust and systematic way to quantify uncertainties from imperfectly known systematic correlations in combined data. It is particularly useful for precision measurements like the determination of $a_\mu^\mathrm{HVP}$. The method is applicable to a wide range of correlated data combinations and will be an important component of the upcoming KNTW data combination for $a_\mu^\mathrm{HVP}$.

提出的框架提供了一种稳健且系统的方法来量化组合数据中由于系统相关性不完全已知而产生的不确定性。它特别适用于像$a_\mu^\mathrm{HVP}$的确定这样的精密测量。该方法适用于广泛的相关数据组合，并将成为即将进行的KNTW数据组合中$a_\mu^\mathrm{HVP}$的重要组成部分。

Abstract: We present a general and systematic framework to quantify uncertainties arising from imperfectly known systematic correlations in data combinations. Formulated at the level of the combined data, the method enables controlled variation of the correlation structure, leading to the construction of covariance matrices directly on the resulting combination and thus providing a robust and systematic estimate of correlation-induced uncertainties. We apply the method to $e^+e^- \rightarrow \mathrm{hadrons}$ cross section data, with the resulting covariance matrices propagated to derived observables, including dispersive determinations of the hadronic vacuum polarization (HVP) contribution to the muon anomalous magnetic moment, $a_μ^\mathrm{HVP}$. We find that uncertainties from systematic correlation assumptions are generally subdominant but non-negligible, and do not fully account for differences between existing $e^+e^- \rightarrow \mathrm{hadrons}$ data combinations. The framework is broadly applicable to correlated data combinations in precision measurements and constitutes a new component of the upcoming KNTW data combination for $a_μ^\mathrm{HVP}$.

</details>


### [6] [NMSSMScanner: Efficient Scans in the NMSSM Parameter Space Proof of Concept](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25009)
*Rafael Boto,Thi Nhung Dao,Felix Egle,Karim Elyaouti,Martin Gabelmann,Margarete Mühlleitner,Johann Plotnikov*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper introduces NMSSMScanner, a new tool for efficient scanning of the NMSSM parameter space, and applies it to find configurations that maximize Higgs boson pair production through resonant scalar or pseudoscalar production.

本文介绍了 NMSSMScanner，这是一种用于高效扫描NMSSM参数空间的新工具，并将其应用于寻找通过共振标量或伪标量产生最大化希格斯玻色子对产生的参数配置。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to develop a tool that can efficiently scan the complex multi-parameter space of the NMSSM and identify parameter configurations that are consistent with experimental data and theoretical expectations, particularly focusing on enhancing Higgs boson pair production rates.

动机是开发一种能够有效扫描NMSSM复杂多参数空间并识别与实验数据和理论预期一致的参数配置的工具，特别关注提高希格斯玻色子对产生率。

Method: A new scanning tool, NMSSMScanner, is developed to efficiently explore the multi-parameter space of the Next-to-Minimal Supersymmetric Standard Model (NMSSM) while considering all relevant constraints. The tool is applied to search for NMSSM parameter configurations that maximize Higgs boson pair production via resonant scalar or pseudoscalar production in various final states.

开发了一个新的扫描工具 NMSSMScanner，用于高效地探索考虑所有相关约束条件的次最小超对称标准模型 (NMSSM) 的多参数空间。该工具被应用于寻找通过各种最终态的共振标量或伪标量产生的最大化希格斯玻色子对产生的NMSSM参数配置。

Result: The NMSSMScanner successfully identifies parameter configurations within the NMSSM that lead to enhanced Higgs boson pair production through resonant scalar or pseudoscalar production. This demonstrates the tool's capability to navigate the NMSSM parameter space and find regions of interest.

NMSSMScanner 成功地识别了导致通过共振标量或伪标量产生增强希格斯玻色子对产生的NMSSM参数配置。这展示了该工具导航NMSSM参数空间并找到感兴趣区域的能力。

Conclusion: The NMSSMScanner tool is effective in identifying parameter configurations that maximize Higgs boson pair production through resonant scalar or pseudoscalar production, demonstrating its utility for exploring the NMSSM parameter space.

NMSSMScanner 工具在识别最大化希格斯玻色子对产生（通过共振标量或伪标量产生）的参数配置方面是有效的，展示了其在探索NMSSM参数空间中的实用性。

Abstract: We present the first version of the new scanning tool NMSSMScanner that allows to perform efficient scans in the complex multi-parameter space of the Next-to-Minimal Supersymmetric extension of the Standard Model (NMSSM) while taking into account all relevant constraints. As a proof of concept we apply it to the search for NMSSM parameter configurations that maximize Higgs boson pair production from resonant scalar or pseudoscalar production in various final states.

### [7] [Can LLP detectors probe the reheating temperature? A case study of vector dark matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25090)

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper explores an extended Higgs portal model with a dark vector and a real scalar, focusing on dark matter production via freeze-in, and the interplay between cosmological constraints and long-lived particle searches at colliders.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to extend the standard singlet-scalar Higgs portal model by including a dark vector $V_\mu$ and a real scalar $\phi$, where $V_\mu$ acts as a dark matter candidate and $\phi$ is a long-lived particle. 作者采用了一个理论框架，该框架通过引入一个暗向量$V_\mu$和一个实标量$\phi$来扩展单标量希格斯门模型。他们分析了在低和高重加热温度下的暗物质（DM）通过冻结机制产生的过程。对于对撞机特征，他们重点关注$\phi \to Z + V$的衰变，这导致了独特的长寿命粒子（LLP）特征。分析包括宇宙学约束与LHC和FCC-hh上LLP搜索之间的相互作用，强调了远端探测器在探测其他无法访问的参数空间以及设定新的重加热温度界限方面的作用。

Result: The results show that the freeze-in mechanism can produce the correct relic abundance of dark matter for a wide range of parameters. The decay $\phi \to Z + V$ yields distinctive LLP signatures at colliders, which can be probed by far detectors. The interplay between cosmological constraints and collider searches reveals that far detectors can access previously unexplored regions of the parameter space and place novel bounds on the reheating temperature, thus providing new insights into the early universe and dark matter physics.

结果表明，冻结机制可以在广泛的参数范围内产生正确的暗物质遗迹丰度。$\phi \to Z + V$的衰变在对撞机中产生了独特的LLP特征，这些特征可以通过远端探测器进行探测。宇宙学约束与对撞机搜索之间的相互作用揭示了远端探测器可以访问以前未探索的参数空间区域，并设定新的重加热温度界限，从而为早期宇宙和暗物质物理提供了新的见解。

带有暗向量和实标量的扩展希格斯门模型为研究暗物质和长寿命粒子提供了一个丰富的框架。冻结机制成功地产生了观测到的暗物质遗迹丰度，而来自$\phi \to Z + V$衰变的LLP特征可以被远端探测器有效探测。这种宇宙学约束与对撞机搜索之间的相互作用为探测新物理并设定重加热温度界限提供了一条有前景的途径。

Abstract: We study an extension of the singlet-scalar Higgs portal featuring a dark vector $V_μ$ and a real scalar $φ$. The vector is a dark matter (DM) candidate, while $φ$ is long-lived and decays via higher-dimensional operators. We explore the DM production via freeze-in at low and high reheating temperatures. At colliders, the decay $φ\to Z+V$ yields distinctive long-lived particle (LLP) signatures. We explore the interplay between cosmological constraints and LLP searches at the LHC and FCC-hh, showing that far detectors can probe otherwise inaccessible parameter space and place novel bounds on the reheating temperature.

Abstract: We present a minimal basis for non-derivative baryon-number-violating operators in the Standard Model Effective Field Theory up to mass dimension 11, as well as for the $(ΔB,ΔL) = (2,2)$ and $(2,-2)$ operators at dimension 12. ### [9] [On the Role of Prompt Photons in the Anisotropic Emission of Direct Photons -- Direct Photons from Au+Au collisions at $\sqrt{s_{NN}}=200$ GeV with IP-Glasma Initial Condition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25165)
*Fu-Ming Liu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The study calculates the anisotropic emission of direct photons from Au+Au collisions using a (3+1)-dimensional viscous hydrodynamic model with Glasma initial conditions. The transverse momentum spectra and flow harmonics $v_2$ and $v_3$ are compared with experimental data, showing good agreement in some centrality bins but discrepancies in others. Adjusting for prompt photon contributions improves the agreement for $v_2$.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand the anisotropic emission of direct photons in heavy-ion collisions at RHIC energies. This is important for probing the properties of the quark-gluon plasma and the dynamics of the collision. 

动机是理解RHIC能量下重离子碰撞中直接光子的各向异性发射。这对于探测夸克-胶子等离子体的性质和碰撞动力学非常重要。

Method: The method involves using a (3+1)-dimensional viscous hydrodynamic model with impact parameter Glasma initial conditions to calculate the anisotropic emission of direct photons. The transverse momentum spectra and flow harmonics $v_2$ and $v_3$ are then compared with experimental data from RHIC. 

方法涉及使用具有冲击参数Glasma初始条件的(3+1)维粘滞流体动力学模型来计算直接光子的各向异性发射。然后将横向动量谱和流动谐波$v_2$和$v_3$与RHIC的实验数据进行比较。

Result: The results show that the transverse momentum spectra of direct photons in different centrality bins (0-20%, 20-40%, and 40-60%) agree well with experimental data. For the elliptic flow $v_2$ and triangular flow $v_3$, the agreement is centrality dependent, with good correspondence for the 20-40% bin but underprediction for the 0-20% bin and overprediction for the 40-60% bin. After accounting for prompt photon contributions, the measured $v_2$ of direct photons can be better explained. 

结果显示，不同中心度区间（0-20%，20-40%，以及40-60%）的直接光子横向动量谱与实验数据吻合良好。对于椭圆流$v_2$和三角流$v_3$，一致性依赖于中心度，在20-40%区间内一致性较好，但在0-20%区间内低估，在40-60%区间内高估。在考虑了瞬时光子贡献后，直接光子的测量$v_2$可以得到更好的解释。

Conclusion: The study concludes that the (3+1)-dimensional viscous hydrodynamic model with Glasma initial conditions provides a good description of the anisotropic emission of direct photons, especially in the 20-40% centrality bin. Discrepancies in $v_2$ and $v_3$ for other centrality bins can be attributed to the contribution from prompt photons, which, when properly accounted for, can improve the agreement with experimental data. 

研究得出结论，具有Glasma初始条件的(3+1)维粘滞流体动力学模型对直接光子的各向异性发射提供了良好的描述，特别是在20-40%中心度区间。其他中心度区间的$v_2$和$v_3$的差异可归因于瞬时光子的贡献，当适当地考虑这些贡献时，可以提高与实验数据的一致性。

Abstract: The anisotropic emission of direct photons from Au+Au collisions at $\sqrt{s_{NN}}$=200 GeV was calculated using a (3+1)-dimensional viscous hydrodynamic model with the impact parameter Glasma initial condition. The transverse momentum spectra of direct photons in different centrality bins (0-20\%, 20-40\%, and 40-60\%) are in good agreement with experimental data measured at RHIC. For the elliptic flow $v_{2}$ and triangular flow $v_{3}$, the agreement is centrality dependent, showing good correspondence for the 20-40\% bin but underprediction for the 0-20\% bin and overprediction for the 40-60\% bin. After carefully accounting for the contribution from prompt photons, the measured $v_{2}$ of direct photons is no longer too large to explain. An overestimation of the prompt photon yield can suppress the $v_2$ and $v_3$ of direct photons to values lower than those observed in the experimental data.

### [10] [Big Dipper, Help Me Find A Way -- Dip-hunting at hadron colliders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25407)
*Diego A. Baron Moreno,Christoph Englert,Yvonne Peters*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper addresses the challenge of detecting top-philic scalar resonances due to destructive interference, proposing a parametric neural network approach to learn likelihood ratios and perform inference on BSM parameters, thus extending traditional bump-hunting with a dip-hunting strategy.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Destructive interference between signal and background processes in searches for top-philic scalar resonances significantly reduces experimental sensitivity. Traditional bump-hunting strategies fail because interference effects invalidate the narrow-width approximation across large regions of the BSM parameter space. Detailed simulations are typically required to model these effects, but this work proposes a new method using parametric neural networks to address the inverse problem.

在寻找顶夸克偏好标量共振的过程中，信号和背景过程之间的破坏性干涉显著降低了实验灵敏度。传统的寻找峰策略由于干涉效应在整个超出标准模型参数空间的大部分区域使窄宽度近似失效而失败。通常需要详细的模拟来建模这些效应，但本文提出了一种使用参数化神经网络解决逆问题的新方法。

Method: The authors employ parametric neural networks to learn the likelihood ratio as a function of both background and key BSM parameters, based on a ratio-of-signed-mixtures framework. The method involves performing inference by testing the compatibility of observed data with a scan over the parameter space of a minimal scalar extension of the Standard Model.

作者基于带符号混合比框架，使用参数化神经网络学习作为背景和关键BSM参数函数的似然比。该方法包括通过测试观测数据与最小标量扩展的标准模型参数空间扫描的兼容性来进行推理。

Result: The proposed method provides a robust diagnostic tool in perturbative regimes and motivates a complementary `dip-hunting' strategy, which extends traditional bump-hunting and could guide future discoveries.

所提出的方法在微扰机制中提供了一个强大的诊断工具，并激发了互补的“凹陷搜索”策略，这扩展了传统的峰搜索，并可能指导未来的发现。

Conclusion: This work demonstrates a novel approach to addressing the challenge of destructive interference in top-philic scalar resonance searches, providing a robust diagnostic tool and a complementary dip-hunting strategy that can enhance the search for BSM physics.

这项工作展示了一种解决顶夸克偏好标量共振搜索中破坏性干涉挑战的新方法，提供了一个强大的诊断工具和一个互补的凹陷搜索策略，可以增强对超出标准模型物理的搜索。

Abstract: Destructive interference between signal and background processes poses a fundamental challenge in searches for top-philic scalar resonances, significantly reducing experimental sensitivity to well-motivated extensions of the Higgs sector. Traditional bump-hunting strategies fail in this instance because interference effects invalidate the narrow-width approximation across large regions of the BSM parameter space. As a result, experimental analyses typically rely on detailed simulations to accurately model these effects throughout the full analysis chain. In this work, we consider the inverse problem in a proof-of-principle study: given an observed pattern in a discriminating distribution, what is the likelihood that it originates from a BSM scalar? To address this, we employ parametric neural networks to learn the likelihood ratio as a function of both background and key BSM parameters, based on a ratio-of-signed-mixtures framework. We perform inference by testing the compatibility of observed data with a scan over the parameter space of a minimal scalar extension of the Standard Model. While BSM parameter extraction remains inherently model-dependent, our approach provides a robust diagnostic in perturbative regimes and motivates a complementary strategy of `dip-hunting'. This strategy extends traditional bump-hunts and could point the way as we navigate towards future discoveries.

### [11] [A study of $J/ψ$ mass shift and bound states: Impact of $D D$ and $DD^*$ meson loops](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25449)
*Manpreet Kaur,Arvind Kumar*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper investigates the mass modification of $J/ψ$ mesons in asymmetric nuclear matter at zero and finite temperatures using an effective Lagrangian approach. It finds that an increase in baryonic density leads to a negative mass shift, suggesting the attraction of $J/ψ$ mesons to nuclear mean fields, which may form meson-nucleus bound states. The binding energy and absorption decay width for $J/ψ$ mesons in various nuclei are also calculated, contributing to the understanding of future experimental data.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand the behavior of $J/ψ$ mesons in asymmetric nuclear matter, which can provide insights into the formation of meson-nucleus bound states and contribute to the interpretation of experimental data from upcoming studies at Jefferson Lab and the Facility for Antiproton and Ion Research (FAIR). [English Text]

研究动机是为了理解$J/ψ$介子在非对称核物质中的行为，这可以为介子-原子核束缚态的形成提供见解，并有助于解释即将在Jefferson实验室和反质子与离子研究设施（FAIR）进行的研究的实验数据。

Method: The method involves an effective Lagrangian approach that includes the contributions of $DD$ and $DD^*$ meson loops. The medium dependence of $D$ meson masses is determined using the hadronic chiral SU(3) model, where scalar condensates are calculated and used in the QCD sum rules approach. [English Text]

方法涉及有效拉格朗日方法，包括$DD$和$DD^*$介子环的贡献。使用手征SU(3)模型确定$D$介子质量的介质依赖性，在该模型中计算标量凝聚物并用于QCD求和规则方法。

Result: The results show that an increase in baryonic density causes a negative mass shift of the $J/ψ$ meson, indicating its attraction to nuclear mean fields. Additionally, the binding energy and absorption decay width of the $J/ψ$ meson for both ground and excited states of specific nuclei are determined. [English Text]

结果表明，重子密度的增加导致$J/ψ$介子的质量负移，表明其被吸引到核平均场。此外，还确定了特定原子核基态和激发态的$J/ψ$介子的结合能和吸收衰减宽度。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the $J/ψ$ meson experiences a negative mass shift in asymmetric nuclear matter, suggesting the possibility of forming meson-nucleus bound states. The calculated binding energies and decay widths provide valuable information for future experimental studies. [English Text]

结论是$J/ψ$介子在非对称核物质中经历质量负移，表明可能形成介子-原子核束缚态。计算出的结合能和衰减宽度为未来实验研究提供了宝贵的信息。

Abstract: We investigate the modification of the $J/ψ$ meson mass in asymmetric nuclear matter at zero and finite temperatures employing an effective Lagrangian approach that considers the contributions of $DD$ and $DD^*$ meson loops. The medium dependence of $D$ meson masses is determined using the hadronic chiral SU(3) model, where scalar condensates are calculated and subsequently utilized in the QCD sum rules approach. Our findings indicate that an increase in baryonic density results in a negative mass shift of the $J/ψ$ meson. This suggests that the $J/ψ$ meson is attracted to nuclear mean fields indicating the possibility of the formation of meson-nucleus bound states. Moreover, we have also determined the binding energy and absorption decay width of the $J/ψ$ meson for both the ground and excited states of $\text{O}^{16}$, $\text{Ca}^{40}$, $\text{Zr}^{90}$, and $\text{Pb}^{208}$ nuclei. These results are expected to contribute to the understanding of experimental data from upcoming studies at Jefferson lab and the facility for antiproton and ion research, where low-momentum charmed mesons can be produced and examined within nuclei.

### [12] [Les Houches study on inclusive jet production at NNLO+NNLL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25490)
*Terry Generet,Joey Huston,Kyle Lee,Ian Moult,Rene Poncelet,Xiaoyuan Zhang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper reassesses the scale variation method in the context of inclusive jet production at the LHC, using NNLO QCD calculations and NNLL resummation. It finds that NNLL resummation can significantly affect the scale uncertainty and central cross section, suggesting that scale variations alone may not reliably estimate the impact of higher orders.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to critically assess the remaining uncertainties in jet production data at the LHC, particularly those arising from non-perturbative effects and missing higher orders. The authors aim to evaluate the reliability of scale variation as a method for estimating these uncertainties and to highlight the importance of going beyond this method in jet and jet substructure calculations.

动机是严格评估LHC上喷流产生数据中剩余的不确定性，特别是那些由非微扰效应和缺失高阶项引起的不确定性。作者旨在评估尺度变化方法在估计这些不确定性方面的可靠性，并强调在喷流和喷流子结构计算中超越该方法的重要性。

Method: The authors perform NNLO QCD calculations supplemented by small-jet-radius resummation through next-to-next-to-leading-logarithmic accuracy (NNLL) for inclusive jet production. They use this approach to reassess the scale variation method, which is commonly used to determine the effects of missing higher orders.

作者进行了通过次次对数精度（NNLL）补充的小喷流半径重求和的NNLO QCD计算，用于全包含喷流产生。他们使用这种方法重新评估了尺度变化方法，该方法通常用于确定缺失高阶项的影响。

Result: The results show that NNLL resummation can have a significant impact on the scale uncertainty for inclusive jet cross sections. For some scale choices, it can also lead to substantial shifts in the central cross section. This suggests that scale variations in fixed-order and resummed calculations may drastically underestimate the impact of higher orders for commonly used jet radius parameters.

结果表明，NNLL重求和可以对全包含喷流截面的尺度不确定性产生显著影响。对于某些尺度选择，它还可能导致中心截面发生实质性偏移。这表明，在固定阶和重求和计算中，尺度变化可能会严重低估常用喷流半径参数下高阶项的影响。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that scale variations in fixed-order and resummed calculations can drastically underestimate the impact of higher orders for commonly used jet radius parameters. The authors recommend that missing higher-order estimates obtained via scale variations should be considered unreliable, and emphasize the importance of going beyond scale variations in jet and jet substructure calculations.

结论是，在固定阶和重求和计算中，尺度变化可能会严重低估常用喷流半径参数下高阶项的影响。作者建议，通过尺度变化获得的缺失高阶项估计应被视为不可靠，并强调在喷流和喷流子结构计算中超越尺度变化方法的重要性。

Abstract: Jet production at the LHC is a powerful probe of QCD, making it ideal for precision tests and determinations of QCD parameters such as parton distribution functions and the strong coupling constant. To make the most of the abundant jet production data collected at the LHC, precise calculations are required. While state-of-the-art calculations reach next-to-next-to-leading order (NNLO) QCD accuracy, a critical assessment of the remaining uncertainties arising from non-perturbative effects and missing higher orders remains crucial for correctly interpreting comparisons between theory and data. Scale variation is nearly always used to determine effects from missing higher orders. In this article, we reassess this method in the context of inclusive jet production by performing NNLO QCD calculations supplemented by small-jet-radius resummation through next-to-next-to-leading-logarithmic accuracy (NNLL). We find that NNLL resummation can have an appreciable impact on the scale uncertainty for inclusive jet cross sections, and, for some scale choices, can lead to sizeable shifts of the central cross section. We conclude that scale variations in fixed-order and resummed calculations can drastically underestimate the impact of higher orders for commonly used jet radius parameters, and that missing higher-order estimates obtained via scale variations should be considered unreliable. Our findings add further evidence to the importance of going beyond scale variations in jet and jet substructure calculations.

### [13] [The EDM inverse problem: Identifying the sources of CP violation and PQ breaking with electric dipole moments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25516)

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper explores the impact of CP-violating effective operators near the QCD scale on electric dipole moments (EDMs) and how these EDMs can be used to distinguish between different sources of CP violation, including the QCD $\theta$-term and the QCD axion's vacuum expectation value.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to identify and classify CP-violating effective operators near the QCD scale that are relevant for low-energy EDMs. The authors aim to use the distinct patterns of EDMs in different systems to discern the underlying ultraviolet origin of CP violation, which could provide insights into physics beyond the Standard Model (SM). Additionally, the paper seeks to explore the connection between EDM measurements and the origin of the QCD axion's vacuum expectation value, particularly in distinguishing between high-scale Peccei--Quinn symmetry-breaking effects and the interplay between beyond-the-SM CP violation and the QCD anomaly.

Method: The method involves identifying six representative classes of CP-violating effective operators near the QCD scale, including the QCD $\theta$-term, that are relevant for low-energy EDMs. The authors then analyze the distinct EDM patterns that arise from these operator classes across different systems, such as nuclei, atoms, and molecules. By comparing the predicted EDM patterns with experimental measurements, the authors aim to discriminate among the different CP-violating sources and infer their ultraviolet origins. The analysis also considers the implications of these EDM measurements for the QCD axion's vacuum expectation value, particularly in the context of Peccei-Quinn symmetry breaking and the QCD anomaly.

该方法包括识别六类代表性的在QCD尺度附近的CP破坏有效算符，其中包括QCD $\theta$-项，这些算符与低能EDMs相关。然后，作者分析了这些算符类在不同系统（如核、原子和分子）中产生的独特EDMs模式。通过将预测的EDMs模式与实验测量结果进行比较，作者旨在区分不同的CP破坏源并推断其紫外起源。该分析还考虑了这些EDMs测量对QCD轴子真空期望值的影响，特别是在Peccei-Quinn对称性破缺和QCD反常的背景下。

Result: The results show that the six identified classes of CP-violating effective operators lead to distinct EDM patterns across different systems. These patterns can be used to discriminate among the different CP-violating sources, thereby providing a way to infer the underlying ultraviolet origin of CP violation. The study also highlights that EDM measurements can provide insights into the origin of the QCD axion's vacuum expectation value, helping to distinguish between high-scale Peccei--Quinn symmetry-breaking effects and the interplay between beyond-the-SM CP violation and the QCD anomaly.

结果表明，所识别的六类CP破坏有效算符在不同系统中导致了独特的EDMs模式。这些模式可以用来区分不同的CP破坏源，从而提供了一种推断CP破坏基本紫外起源的方法。研究还强调，EDMs测量可以为QCD轴子真空期望值的起源提供见解，有助于区分高尺度Peccei-Quinn对称性破缺效应与超出SM的CP破坏和QCD反常之间的相互作用。

Conclusion: The conclusion of the paper is that by analyzing the distinct EDM patterns induced by different CP-violating effective operators, it is possible to distinguish between various sources of CP violation and potentially uncover the underlying ultraviolet physics. Furthermore, the study suggests that EDM measurements can shed light on the origin of the QCD axion's vacuum expectation value, which has implications for understanding the nature of Peccei--Quinn symmetry breaking and the role of the QCD anomaly in this context.

本文的结论是，通过分析由不同CP破坏有效算符引起的独特EDMs模式，可以区分各种CP破坏源，并有可能揭示其基本紫外物理。此外，研究表明，EDMs测量可以为QCD轴子真空期望值的起源提供见解，这对理解Peccei-Quinn对称性破缺的本质以及QCD反常在这种背景下的作用具有重要意义。

Abstract: Many extensions of the Standard Model (SM) generically introduce new sources of CP violation, which can induce observable $P$-odd and $T$-odd permanent electric dipole moments (EDMs) of nuclei, atoms, and molecules. A future observation of nonvanishing EDMs would therefore provide a sensitive probe of physics beyond the SM, while also posing a nontrivial inverse problem: identifying their underlying ultraviolet origin. In this work, we identify six representative classes of CP-violating effective operators near the QCD scale, including the QCD $θ$-term, that are particularly relevant for low-energy EDMs and can arise in a broad range of SM extensions. We show that these operator classes lead to distinct EDM patterns across different systems, thereby enabling discrimination among them through experimentally measured EDMs. We further emphasize that EDM measurements can shed light on the origin of the vacuum expectation value of the QCD axion. In particular, they may help distinguish whether a nonzero axion vacuum expectation value is predominantly induced by high-scale Peccei--Quinn symmetry-breaking effects, such as those associated with quantum gravity, or by the interplay between beyond-the-SM CP violation and the QCD anomaly.

### [14] [A Speculative Benchmark for the AMS-02 Electron and Positron Spectra from a Time-Symmetric Transport Hypothesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25542)
*Yi Yang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper explores the time-symmetric interpretation of antiparticles, particularly in the context of AMS-02 electron and positron data. It uses a standard high-energy energy-loss form and introduces a time-symmetric hypothesis for the propagation response. The study identifies preferred benchmark regions by analyzing the spectral morphology, especially the breadth of the turnover region. A minimal phenomenological framework is used to capture the lepton spectra, with the advanced branch experiencing reduced effective radiative exposure.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore whether the time-symmetric interpretation of antiparticles can be connected to the distinct spectral structures observed in the AMS-02 electron and positron data. The authors aim to introduce the time-symmetric hypothesis at the level of the effective propagation response, treating the electron sector as purely retarded and the positron sector as an admixture of retarded and advanced components.

Method: The method involves using the standard high-energy energy-loss form for Galactic leptons, $b(E) = b_0 E^2$, and introducing the time-symmetric hypothesis for the propagation response. A 2D scan of the parameter space is performed to analyze the macroscopic admixture fraction and the exposure reduction. The authors adopt a representative, order-of-magnitude benchmark where the advanced-associated component dominates but experiences a ten-fold reduction in effective radiative exposure. The analysis omits complex spatial diffusion and solar modulation.

Result: The results show that while the characteristic peak position is degenerate, the spectral morphology, particularly the breadth of the turnover region, helps identify physically preferred benchmark regions. The minimal phenomenological framework captures the widely separated energy scales of the lepton spectra, isolating the reduced effective radiative exposure of the advanced branch as a key ingredient.

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the time-symmetric hypothesis, when applied to the effective propagation response, can naturally capture the lepton spectra and the distinct features observed in the AMS-02 data. The advanced-associated component, with reduced effective radiative exposure, is identified as a key postulated ingredient requiring deeper theoretical justification.

Abstract: We revisit the time-symmetric interpretation of antiparticles and explore whether it can be connected, as a speculative benchmark, to the distinct spectral structures observed in the AMS-02 electron and positron data. Rather than modifying the local radiative loss law, we adopt the standard high-energy energy-loss form for Galactic leptons, $b(E)=b_0E^2$, and introduce the time-symmetric hypothesis at the level of the effective propagation response. In this framework, the electron sector is treated as purely retarded, while the positron sector is modeled as an effective admixture of retarded and advanced-associated components. We perform a systematic 2D scan of the parameter space governing the macroscopic admixture fraction and the exposure reduction, and demonstrate that while the characteristic peak position is degenerate, the spectral morphology, especially the breadth of the turnover region, helps identify physically preferred benchmark regions. Based on this, we adopt a representative, order-of-magnitude benchmark, in which the advanced-associated component dominates the effective admixture but experiences a ten-fold reduction in effective radiative exposure, to dissect the underlying spectral components and verify the results against AMS-02 data. While omitting complex spatial diffusion and solar modulation, this minimal phenomenological framework naturally captures the widely separated energy scales of the lepton spectra, explicitly isolating the reduced effective radiative exposure of the advanced branch as a postulated ingredient requiring deeper theoretical justification.

Conclusion: The paper concludes by demonstrating the effectiveness of Jarvis-HEP through synthetic and phenomenological examples, highlighting its potential to streamline high-energy physics research workflows and parameter scans. 

该论文通过合成和现象学示例展示了Jarvis-HEP的有效性，强调了其在简化高能物理研究工作流程和参数扫描方面的潜力。

Abstract: High-energy physics phenomenology often requires linking multiple computational tools to evaluate observables, likelihoods, and experimental constraints across nontrivial parameter spaces. ### [16] [Determination of the $Z_c(3900)$ and the $Z_{cs}(3985)$ states from joint analysis of experimental and lattice data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25607)
*Yun-Hua Chen,Meng-Lin Du,Feng-Kun Guo*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper presents a unified analysis of the $Z_c(3900)$ and $Z_{cs}(3985)$ states, incorporating experimental and lattice data. It includes various processes and interactions, concluding that these states are SU(3) flavor partners within the same octet multiplet and are resonance states with specific pole masses and half-widths. A compositeness analysis suggests additional components are needed beyond the $D\bar{D}^* (D_s\bar{D}^\ast+D\bar{D}_s^\ast)$ component to form these exotic states.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to provide a comprehensive understanding of the nature of the $Z_c(3900)$ and $Z_{cs}(3985)$ states by integrating both experimental and lattice QCD data. The study aims to clarify whether these states can be interpreted as SU(3) flavor partners and to determine their physical properties, such as pole masses and half-widths, as well as their composition.

动机是通过整合实验和格点QCD数据，全面理解$Z_c(3900)$和$Z_{cs}(3985)$态的性质。研究旨在明确这些态是否可以被解释为SU(3)味伙伴，并确定它们的物理属性，如极点质量和半宽度，以及它们的组成。

Method: The method involves a simultaneous analysis of multiple processes including $e^+e^- \rightarrow J/ψπ^+π^-, J/ψK^+ K^-, D^0 D^{\ast-} π^+, (D^{\ast 0} D_s^{-}+D^0 D_s^{\ast -}) K^+$, and finite-volume energy levels from recent lattice QCD simulations. The analysis accounts for open-charm meson loops with triangle singularities, coupled-channel interactions, and final-state interactions. Theoretical frameworks such as the Bethe-Salpeter equation and effective field theory are used to model these interactions.

方法包括同时分析多个过程，包括$e^+e^- \rightarrow J/ψπ^+π^-, J/ψK^+ K^-, D^0 D^{\ast-} π^+, (D^{\ast 0} D_s^{-}+D^0 D_s^{\ast -}) K^+$，以及最近的格点QCD模拟中的有限体积能级。分析考虑了具有三角奇点的开粲介子环、耦合道相互作用和末态相互作用。使用诸如Bethe-Salpeter方程和有效场论等理论框架来建模这些相互作用。

Result: The results show that pole contributions associated with the $Z_c(3900)$ and $Z_{cs}(3985)$ are essential for describing the data. The extracted pole masses and half-widths are $(3879.6 \pm 4.8)$ MeV and $(32.2 \pm 4.7)$ MeV for the $Z_c(3900)$, and $(3976.9 \pm 5.1)$ MeV and $(28.8 \pm 5.9)$ MeV for the $Z_{cs}(3985)$. The ratios of the couplings to different channels are also determined. The compositeness analysis indicates that while the $D\bar{D}^* (D_s\bar{D}^\ast+D\bar{D}_s^\ast)$ component is significant, additional components are necessary to fully describe these states.

结果表明，与$Z_c(3900)$和$Z_{cs}(3985)$相关的极点贡献对于描述数据是必不可少的。提取的极点质量和半宽度分别为$(3879.6 \pm 4.8)$ MeV 和 $(32.2 \pm 4.7)$ MeV（$Z_c(3900)$），以及$(3976.9 \pm 5.1)$ MeV 和 $(28.8 \pm 5.9)$ MeV（$Z_{cs}(3985)$）。还确定了不同通道的耦合比。组合性分析表明，虽然$D\bar{D}^* (D_s\bar{D}^\ast+D\bar{D}_s^\ast)$成分显著，但需要额外的成分来完全描述这些态。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the $Z_c(3900)$ and $Z_{cs}(3985)$ states are SU(3) flavor partners within the same octet multiplet and are resonance states. The joint description of experimental and lattice data supports this interpretation. The extracted pole masses and half-widths, along with the coupling ratios, provide a detailed understanding of the internal structure of these states. The compositeness analysis suggests that while the $D\bar{D}^* (D_s\bar{D}^\ast+D\bar{D}_s^\ast)$ component is important, additional components are still required to fully explain the nature of these exotic states.

结论是$Z_c(3900)$和$Z_{cs}(3985)$态是同一八重态内的SU(3)味伙伴，并且是共振态。实验和格点数据的联合描述支持这一解释。提取的极点质量和半宽度以及耦合比提供了对这些态内部结构的详细理解。组合性分析表明，虽然$D\bar{D}^* (D_s\bar{D}^\ast+D\bar{D}_s^\ast)$成分重要，但还需要额外的成分来完全解释这些奇异态的性质。

Abstract: We present a unified analysis of the $Z_c(3900)$ and $Z_{cs}(3985)$ states considering both experimental and lattice data. The study simultaneously includes the processes $e^+e^- \rightarrow J/ψπ^+π^-, J/ψK^+ K^-, D^0 D^{\ast-} π^+, (D^{\ast 0} D_s^{-}+D^0 D_s^{\ast -}) K^+$, together with finite-volume energy levels from recent lattice QCD simulations. Open-charm meson loops with triangle singularities, the $J/ψπ(J/ψ\bar{K})$-$\bar{D}D^*(\bar{D}D^*_s)$ coupled-channel interactions, and the $ππ$-$K\bar K$ final-state interaction are all taken into account. We find that pole contributions associated with the $Z_c(3900)$ and $Z_{cs}(3985)$ are indispensable for describing the data. The successful joint description of the experimental and lattice data supports the interpretation that the $Z_c(3900)$ and $Z_{cs}(3985)$ are SU(3) flavor partners within the same octet multiplet and indicates that both are resonance states. The extracted pole masses and half-widths of the $Z_c(3900)$ and the $Z_{cs}(3985)$ are $(3879.6 \pm 4.8)$ MeV and $(32.2 \pm 4.7)$ MeV, and $(3976.9 \pm 5.1)$ MeV and $(28.8 \pm 5.9)$ MeV, respectively. The ratios of the $Z_c(Z_{cs})$ couplings to the $D\bar D^*(D_s\bar{D}^\ast+D\bar{D}_s^\ast)$ and $J/ψπ(J/ψK)$ channels are also determined. A compositeness analysis indicates that, although the $D\bar D^* (D_s\bar{D}^\ast+D\bar{D}_s^\ast)$ component in the $Z_c(3900) (Z_{cs}(3985))$ state is sizable, additional components are still needed to form these exotic states.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: The method involves using chiral effective field theory to describe the interactions of the $\pi^0$-$\eta$-$\eta'$-$a$ system, incorporating next-to-leading-order corrections and linear isospin-breaking effects. The hadronic form factors relevant to the $\tau$ decays are calculated using this framework. Resonance parameters are determined by fitting the form factors to experimental data from $\tau^- \to \pi^- \pi^0 \nu_\tau$, $\tau^- \to K_S \pi^- \nu_\tau$, and $\tau^- \to K^- \eta \nu_\tau$ decays. The predictions for the branching ratios, invariant-mass distributions, and forward-backward asymmetries offer a clear path for future experimental searches. Abstract: In this work we explore the semileptonic $τ$ decays into the axion-like particle ($a$)-meson final states within chiral effective field theory. The next-to-leading-order mixing matrix for the $π^0$-$η$-$η'$-$a$ system with the linear isospin-breaking effects, is exploited and then implemented to calculate the hadronic form factors relevant to the $τ$ decays. TL;DR: This paper studies deeply virtual Compton scattering on a helium-4 target, incorporating kinematic twist-3 and twist-4 corrections, and NLO corrections to the twist-2 amplitude. It results in the first tomographic image of the helium-4 nucleus at the quark-gluon level.

本文研究了氦-4靶上的深度虚拟康普顿散射，包括动量扭曲-3和扭曲-4修正，以及次领头阶修正。这得到了第一个在夸克-胶子层次上的氦-4原子核的断层图像。

Method: The method involves studying deeply virtual Compton scattering (DVCS) on a helium-4 target. Result: The result is the first tomographic image of the helium-4 nucleus at the quark-gluon level, obtained through a precise description of the data using DVCS with comprehensive corrections. This image provides a new perspective on the internal structure of the helium-4 nucleus.

结果是通过使用包含全面修正的深度虚拟康普顿散射（DVCS）精确描述数据，得到了第一个在夸克-胶子层次上的氦-4原子核的断层图像。这个图像提供了关于氦-4原子核内部结构的新视角。

Conclusion: The study of deeply virtual Compton scattering on a helium-4 target, including kinematic twist-3 and twist-4 corrections, as well as next-to-leading-order corrections to the twist-2 amplitude in the strong coupling $\alpha_s$, is crucial for achieving a precise description of the data. This work results in the first tomographic image of the helium-4 nucleus at the quark-gluon level.

对氦-4靶进行深度虚拟康普顿散射的研究，包括动量扭曲-3和扭曲-4修正，以及强耦合$\alpha_s$中的次领头阶修正对于精确描述数据至关重要。这项工作得到了第一个在夸克-胶子层次上的氦-4原子核的断层图像。

Abstract: Coherent hard exclusive reactions on light nuclei provide access to their quark and gluon structure and enable three-dimensional tomography of these complex systems. We study deeply virtual Compton scattering on a helium-4 target, including both kinematic twist-3 and twist-4 corrections, as well as next-to-leading-order corrections to the twist-2 amplitude in the strong coupling $α_s$. We show that these contributions are crucial for achieving a precise description of the data and, as a result, obtain the first tomographic image of the helium-4 nucleus at the quark-gluon level.

### [20] [Collective neutrino-antineutrino pair oscillations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25687)
*Shih-Jie Huang,Meng-Ru Wu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper investigates the conditions for collective neutrino-antineutrino ($\nu\bar{\nu}$) pairing instabilities in a dense neutrino gas using simplified toy models. The instability growth rate is comparable to that of fast flavor instabilities, and the results suggest further studies in realistic astrophysical and cosmological settings.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to explore the conditions under which collective $\nu\bar{\nu}$ pairing instabilities can occur in a dense neutrino gas. This is motivated by the potential significance of such instabilities in astrophysical and cosmological environments, where dense neutrino gases are common. Understanding these instabilities could provide new insights into the behavior of neutrinos in extreme conditions.

本文的动机是探索在密集的中微子气体中集体$\nu\bar{\nu}$配对不稳定性发生的条件。这是由于这种不稳定性在天体物理和宇宙学环境中可能具有重要意义，这些环境中密集的中微子气体很常见。理解这些不稳定性可以为极端条件下中微子的行为提供新的见解。

Method: The authors use simplified toy models consisting of discretized $\nu\bar{\nu}$ pairs in a homogeneous neutrino gas to study the conditions for the emergence of $\nu\bar{\nu}$ pairing instabilities. They analyze the phase space distribution of the excessive pair-occupation number, defined as the sum of the neutrino and antineutrino occupation numbers of a pair minus 1, and find that the sign change of this distribution is a key indicator of the onset of instabilities. The instability growth rate is determined by the forward scattering potential and is compared to the growth rate of fast flavor instabilities.

作者使用由均匀中微子气体中的离散$\nu\bar{\nu}$对组成的简化玩具模型来研究$\nu\bar{\nu}$配对不稳定性出现的条件。他们分析了过量对占据数的相空间分布，该分布定义为一对中微子和反中微子的占据数之和减去1，并发现该分布符号的变化是不稳定性开始的关键指标。不稳定性增长率由前向散射势决定，并与快速味不稳定性增长率进行比较。

Result: The results show that in anisotropic systems, $\nu\bar{\nu}$ pairing instabilities generally emerge when the phase space distribution of the excessive pair-occupation number changes signs. The associated instability growth rate is set by the forward scattering potential and is comparable to that of collective fast neutrino flavor instabilities. These instabilities can lead to the conversion of $\nu\bar{\nu}$ occupation numbers between different momentum modes.

结果表明，在各向异性系统中，当过量对占据数的相空间分布符号变化时，$\nu\bar{\nu}$配对不稳定性通常会出现。相关的不稳定性增长率由前向散射势决定，并且与集体快速中微子味不稳定性增长率相当。这些不稳定性可以导致不同动量模式之间的$\nu\bar{\nu}$占据数转换。

Conclusion: The study concludes that $\nu\bar{\nu}$ pairing instabilities can occur in dense neutrino gases under certain conditions, and their growth rates are comparable to those of fast flavor instabilities. The findings motivate further investigations into the relevance of $\nu\bar{\nu}$ pairing effects in realistic astrophysical and cosmological environments, potentially leading to a better understanding of neutrino behavior in such settings.

研究得出结论，$\nu\bar{\nu}$配对不稳定性在一定条件下可以在密集的中微子气体中发生，其增长率与快速味不稳定性增长率相当。这些发现激发了进一步研究$\nu\bar{\nu}$配对效应在实际天体物理和宇宙学环境中的相关性，从而可能更好地理解在这种环境下的中微子行为。

Abstract: In dense neutrino gas, pairing correlations between neutrinos and antineutrinos with opposite momenta can be nonzero in generalized neutrino quantum kinetic equations at the mean-field level. In this Letter, we investigate for the first time the condition under which collective neutrino-antineutrino ($ν\barν$) pairing instabilities can occur, using simplified toy models consisting of discretized $ν\barν$ pairs in a homogeneous neutrino gas. We find that, in ansiotropic systems, $ν\barν$ pairing instabilities generally emerge when the phase space distribution of the excessive pair-occupation number, defined as the sum of the neutrino and antineutrino occupation numbers of a pair minus 1, changes signs. The associated instability growth rate is set by the forward scattering potential and is comparable to that of collective fast neutrino flavor instabilities. The instabilities can result in pair conversions of $ν\barν$ occupation numbers between different momentum modes. Our results motivate further studies to assess the relevance of $ν\barν$ pairing effects in realistic astrophysical and cosmological environments.

### [21] [Imprint of domain wall annihilation on induced gravitational waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25726)
*Rishav Roshan*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper discusses the impact of domain wall annihilation on the gravitational wave spectrum, particularly focusing on how an early matter-dominated phase, driven by the decay of a long-lived scalar field, can amplify induced gravitational waves, leading to a spectrum with two detectable peaks.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand the distinctive imprint left by domain wall annihilation on the gravitational wave spectrum and how this can be used to probe early universe symmetry breaking. The focus is on the transformation of domain wall energy into a scalar field and the subsequent amplification of gravitational waves due to an early matter-dominated phase.

Method: The method involves theoretical analysis and modeling of the gravitational wave spectrum produced during and after domain wall annihilation. This includes considering the transition from an early matter-dominated phase to radiation domination and its effect on the gravitational wave spectrum. The authors explore the parameter space that can be observed and how multi-band detection can be used to probe these phenomena.

Result: The result is the identification of a gravitational wave spectrum with two distinct peaks, one from the initial domain wall annihilation and another from the amplified induced gravitational waves during the early matter-dominated phase. These peaks are detectable across complementary frequency bands, providing a unique signature of early universe processes.

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the distinctive gravitational wave spectrum resulting from domain wall annihilation and the subsequent early matter-dominated phase can provide valuable insights into early universe symmetry breaking. Multi-band detection of these gravitational waves could offer a new way to probe the physics of the early universe.

Abstract: Domain wall annihilation can leave a distinctive imprint on the induced gravitational wave spectrum. During annihilation, most of the domain wall energy transforms into the scalar field responsible for the initial $\mathbb{Z}_2$ symmetry breaking that created the walls, along with any coupled species. If the produced scalar is sufficiently long-lived, its delayed decay drives an early matter-dominated phase following domain wall annihilation, significantly amplifying induced gravitational waves from primordial perturbations. The subsequent transition to radiation domination dilutes the domain wall contribution through entropy injection while preserving the enhanced induced signal. This creates a gravitational wave spectrum with two distinct peaks detectable across complementary frequency bands. We explore the observable parameter space and demonstrate how multi-band detection can probe early universe symmetry breaking.

### [22] [Covariant Construction of Generalized Form Factors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25771)
*Hao Sun,Tuo Tan,Jiang-Hao Yu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper introduces a systematic method to construct Lorentz-covariant structures for hadronic matrix elements of local operators using spinor Young tableaux. It provides form factor bases for scalar, vector, and rank-2 tensor operators for particles with various spins, including the first presentation of general $P$ and $T$ form factors for spin-$\frac{3}{2}$ and spin-$2$ particles. The results are cross-checked by non-relativistic counting and Hilbert Series methods, revealing an overcount in the literature for spin-2 particles. The method can be applied to decompose matrix elements of nonlocal operators.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to develop a comprehensive and systematic technique for constructing all possible Lorentz-covariant structures of hadronic matrix elements of local operators, which is essential for understanding the behavior of particles with arbitrary spins. This includes the derivation of form factor bases that have not been fully explored, particularly for higher spin particles such as spin-$\frac{3}{2}$ and spin-$2$. [English Text]
The motivation is to develop a comprehensive and systematic technique for constructing all possible Lorentz-covariant structures of hadronic matrix elements of local operators, which is essential for understanding the behavior of particles with arbitrary spins. This includes the derivation of form factor bases that have not been fully explored, particularly for higher spin particles such as spin-$\frac{3}{2}$ and spin-$2$.

[Chinese Text]
动机是开发一种全面且系统的技术，用于构建局部算符的强子矩阵元的所有可能的洛伦兹协变结构，这对于理解任意自旋粒子的行为至关重要。这包括推导尚未完全探索的形式因子基，特别是对于高自旋粒子，如自旋-$\frac{3}{2}$和自旋-$2$。

Method: The method involves the use of spinor Young tableaux of the Lorentz group to construct all possible covariant structures for the matrix elements of arbitrary operators. The relativistic wave functions and momenta of the initial and final state particles, with arbitrary spin, serve as building blocks. The form factor bases for scalar, vector, and rank-2 tensor operators are obtained for particles with spin-$\frac{1}{2}$, $1$, $\frac{3}{2}$, and $2$. The independent form factor structures are cross-verified using non-relativistic counting and the Hilbert Series method. [English Text]
The method involves the use of spinor Young tableaux of the Lorentz group to construct all possible covariant structures for the matrix elements of arbitrary operators. The relativistic wave functions and momenta of the initial and final state particles, with arbitrary spin, serve as building blocks. The form factor bases for scalar, vector, and rank-2 tensor operators are obtained for particles with spin-$\frac{1}{2}$, $1$, $\frac{3}{2}$, and $2$. The independent form factor structures are cross-verified using non-relativistic counting and the Hilbert Series method.

[Chinese Text]
该方法利用洛伦兹群的旋量杨表来构造任意算符的矩阵元的所有可能的协变结构。初始态和末态粒子的相对论波函数和动量，具有任意自旋，作为构建块。对于自旋为$\frac{1}{2}$, $1$, $\frac{3}{2}$ 和 $2$ 的粒子，获得了标量、矢量和秩-2张量算符的形式因子基。独立的形式因子结构通过非相对论计数和希尔伯特级数方法进行了交叉验证。

Result: The result is the construction of form factor bases for scalar, vector, and rank-2 tensor operators for particles with spins $\frac{1}{2}$, $1$, $\frac{3}{2}$, and $2$. For the first time, the general $P$ and $T$ form factors for spin-$\frac{3}{2}$ and spin-$2$ particles are presented. Additionally, the study reveals that there is a redundant $P$ and $T$ conserved structure for spin-$2$ particles, as reported in the literature. [English Text]
The result is the construction of form factor bases for scalar, vector, and rank-2 tensor operators for particles with spins $\frac{1}{2}$, $1$, $\frac{3}{2}$, and $2$. For the first time, the general $P$ and $T$ form factors for spin-$\frac{3}{2}$ and spin-$2$ particles are presented. Additionally, the study reveals that there is a redundant $P$ and $T$ conserved structure for spin-$2$ particles, as reported in the literature.

[Chinese Text]
结果是为自旋为$\frac{1}{2}$, $1$, $\frac{3}{2}$ 和 $2$ 的粒子构建了标量、矢量和秩-2张量算符的形式因子基。首次展示了自旋-$\frac{3}{2}$ 和自旋-$2$ 粒子的一般 $P$ 和 $T$ 形式因子。此外，研究揭示了文献中报道的自旋-$2$ 粒子存在冗余的 $P$ 和 $T$ 守恒结构。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the proposed method successfully constructs the Lorentz-covariant structures for hadronic matrix elements of local operators, providing a complete set of form factor bases for particles with various spins. The method also identifies and corrects an overcounting issue in the literature for spin-$2$ particles. [English Text]
The conclusion is that the proposed method successfully constructs the Lorentz-covariant structures for hadronic matrix elements of local operators, providing a complete set of form factor bases for particles with various spins. The method also identifies and corrects an overcounting issue in the literature for spin-$2$ particles.

[Chinese Text]
结论是所提出的方法成功地为局部算符的强子矩阵元构建了洛伦兹协变结构，为具有各种自旋的粒子提供了一整套形式因子基。该方法还识别并纠正了文献中关于自旋-$2$ 粒子的过度计数问题。

Abstract: We present a systematic technique for constructing the Lorentz-covariant structures of hadronic matrix elements of local operators. The spinor Young tableaux of the Lorentz group is employed to construct all possible structures for the matrix elements of arbitrary operators, using the relativistic wave functions and momenta of the initial and final state particles of arbitrary spin as building blocks. We obtain the form factor bases for the scalar, vector, and rank-2 tensor operators for particles with spin-$\frac{1}{2}$, $1$, $\frac{3}{2}$, and $2$, among which the general $P$ and $T$ form factors for spin-$\frac{3}{2}$ and spin-$2$ particles are presented for the first time. The independent form factor structures are also cross-checked by the non-relativistic counting and Hilbert Series method and we find there is redundant $P$ and $T$ conserved structure for spin-$2$ particles in literature. As an application, the matrix elements of general nonlocal operators can be expanded by towers of the matrix elements of local operators, and thus can be decomposed by the constructed form factor bases above.

### [23] [Four-Loop Gluon Anomalous Dimension of General Lorentz Spin: Transcendental Part](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25833)
*B. A. Kniehl,S. -O. Moch,V. N. Velizhanin,A. Vogt*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper calculates the $\zeta(3)$-proportional part of the four-loop anomalous dimension $\gamma_{gg}^{(3)}(N)$ for twist-two gluon operators in a general gauge theory, using the Lenstra-Lenstra-Lovász algorithm. It also provides the rational part with color factor $C_F^2n_f^2$. The results contribute to reducing uncertainties in QCD parton distribution functions.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to advance the understanding of the anomalous dimensions of twist-two operators in gauge theories, particularly at four loops. By calculating the $\zeta(3)$-proportional part and the rational part with specific color factors, the authors aim to improve the precision of predictions for scaling violations in QCD parton distribution functions.

动机是推进对规范理论中二扭算子的反常维数的理解，特别是在四环水平。通过计算与$\zeta(3)$成比例的部分和具有特定颜色因子的有理部分，作者旨在提高QCD部分子分布函数标度违背预测的精度。

Method: The authors use the Lenstra-Lenstra-Lovász (LLL) algorithm to analyze the available low-$N$ moments of the anomalous dimension $\gamma_{gg}^{(3)}(N)$. They apply generalized Gribov-Liptov reciprocity and establish new self-tuning relations for the anomalous dimension matrix in the singlet sector. Information from $\mathcal{N}=1,4$ supersymmetric Yang-Mills theories is also utilized. The inverse Mellin transformation is used to derive the contribution to the four-loop splitting function $P_{gg}^{(3)}(x)$.

作者使用Lenstra-Lenstra-Lovász（LLL）算法分析了反常维数$\gamma_{gg}^{(3)}(N)$的可用低$N$矩。他们应用广义Gribov-Liptov互易性，并建立了单态部门反常维数矩阵的新自调谐关系。还利用了来自$\mathcal{N}=1,4$超对称Yang-Mills理论的信息。通过逆Mellin变换推导出对四环分裂函数$P_{gg}^{(3)}(x)$的贡献。

Result: The paper presents the $\zeta(3)$-proportional part of the four-loop anomalous dimension $\gamma_{gg}^{(3)}(N)$ in analytic form. Additionally, the rational part of $\gamma_{gg}^{(3)}(N)$ with the color factor $C_F^2n_f^2$ is provided. These results are then used to determine the exact contributions to the four-loop splitting function $P_{gg}^{(3)}(x)$ via inverse Mellin transformation.

论文以解析形式呈现了四环反常维数$\gamma_{gg}^{(3)}(N)$的$\zeta(3)$-成比例部分。此外，还提供了具有颜色因子$C_F^2n_f^2$的$\gamma_{gg}^{(3)}(N)$的有理部分。这些结果随后用于通过逆Mellin变换确定对四环分裂函数$P_{gg}^{(3)}(x)$的确切贡献。

Conclusion: The calculation of the $\zeta(3)$-proportional part and the rational part of the four-loop anomalous dimension $\gamma_{gg}^{(3)}(N)$, along with the derived contributions to the four-loop splitting function, significantly reduces theoretical uncertainties in the scaling violations of parton distribution functions in QCD. This work advances the precision of perturbative QCD calculations and provides a deeper understanding of the structure of anomalous dimensions in gauge theories.

计算四环反常维数$\gamma_{gg}^{(3)}(N)$的$\zeta(3)$-成比例部分和有理部分，以及对四环分裂函数的贡献，显著减少了QCD部分子分布函数标度违背中的理论不确定性。这项工作提高了微扰QCD计算的精度，并提供了对规范理论中反常维数结构的更深入理解。

Abstract: We consider the anomalous dimension $γ_{gg}^{(3)}(N)$ of the twist-two gluon operator of arbitrary Lorentz spin $N$ in the quark flavor singlet sector of a general gauge theory at four loops and construct its contribution proportional to $ζ(3)$ in analytic form by applying the Lenstra-Lenstra-Lovász algorithm to the available low-$N$ moments. We exploit generalized Gribov-Liptov reciprocity, establish new self-tuning relations for the anomalous dimension matrix of the singlet sector, and inject information from $\mathcal{N}=1,4$ supersymmetric Yang-Mills theories. We also present the contribution to the rational part of $γ_{gg}^{(3)}(N)$ with color factor $C_F^2n_f^2$. Exact contributions to the four-loop splitting function $P_{gg}^{(3)}(x)$ hence resulting via inverse Mellin transformation help us to reduce theoretical uncertainties in scaling violations of parton distribution functions in QCD.
