### [24] [Analysis of quarkonium polarization in proton-proton (p-p) collisions at LHC using PYTHIA model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25838)
*Deekshit Kumar,Ekata Nandy,Biswarup Paul,Subikash Choudhury,Tinku Sinha,Partha Pratim Bhaduri*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper investigates the polarization of charmonia ($J/\psi$) and bottomonia ($\Upsilon(1S)$) in proton-proton collisions at LHC energies, using the PYTHIA8 Monte Carlo event generator. The study includes the effects of detector inefficiencies and muon momentum smearing on the polarization parameters, which are estimated in Helicity and Collins-Sooper reference frames. The results are compared with recent ALICE measurements.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The measurement of quarkonia polarization provides insights into the production mechanisms of heavy quark-antiquark bound states in hadronic collisions. By studying the angular distribution of decay muons, one can infer the polarization state of the quarkonia. This work aims to model these phenomena using a perturbative QCD-based Monte Carlo event generator, PYTHIA8, and to account for experimental conditions such as detector inefficiencies and muon momentum resolution.

重夸克偶素的极化测量为研究强子碰撞中重夸克-反夸克束缚态的产生机制提供了重要线索。通过分析来自夸克偶素衰变的缪子角分布，可以推断出夸克偶素的极化状态。本工作旨在使用基于微扰QCD的蒙特卡洛事件生成器PYTHIA8来模拟这些现象，并考虑实验条件，如探测器效率和缪子动量分辨率。

Method: The study employs the PYTHIA8 Monte Carlo event generator to simulate $J/\psi$ and $\Upsilon(1S)$ production in p-p collisions at $\sqrt{s} = 7$ and 13 TeV. The transverse momentum ($p_T$) differential distributions are calculated at forward rapidity ($2.5 < y_{\mu\mu} < 4.0$). Polarization parameters are estimated in both the Helicity and Collins-Sooper reference frames. To mimic realistic experimental conditions, detector inefficiencies and muon momentum smearing are incorporated into the simulations.

本研究使用PYTHIA8蒙特卡洛事件生成器模拟在$\sqrt{s} = 7$和13 TeV质子-质子碰撞中$J/\psi$和$\Upsilon(1S)$的产生。计算了前向快度区（$2.5 < y_{\mu\mu} < 4.0$）的横向动量（$p_T$）微分分布。在Helicity和Collins-Sooper参考系中估计了极化参数。为了模拟真实的实验条件，将探测器效率低下和缪子动量平滑效应纳入了模拟中。

Result: The simulation results show that the inclusion of detector inefficiencies and muon momentum smearing significantly affects the polarization parameters. These effects introduce an artificial degree of polarization, which must be corrected for to accurately interpret the data. The simulated polarization parameters are compared with recent ALICE measurements, providing a basis for understanding the impact of experimental conditions on the observed polarization.

模拟结果显示，探测器效率低下和缪子动量平滑效应显著影响极化参数。这些效应引入了一定程度的人为极化，必须进行校正才能准确解释数据。将模拟的极化参数与最近的ALICE测量结果进行了比较，为理解实验条件对观测到的极化的影响提供了基础。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates the importance of accounting for detector inefficiencies and muon momentum smearing in the analysis of quarkonia polarization. The comparison with ALICE measurements highlights the need for careful consideration of experimental conditions to accurately determine the polarization of $J/\psi$ and $\Upsilon(1S)$ in p-p collisions at LHC energies. Further refinements in the simulation and analysis methods could lead to a better understanding of the underlying physics of quarkonium production and polarization.

研究表明，在夸克偶素极化的分析中考虑探测器效率低下和缪子动量平滑效应的重要性。与ALICE测量结果的比较突显了准确确定LHC能量下质子-质子碰撞中$J/\psi$和$\Upsilon(1S)$极化时仔细考虑实验条件的必要性。进一步改进模拟和分析方法可能会更好地理解夸克偶素产生和极化的基本物理。

Abstract: The measurement of polarization serves as an important probe to investigate the production mechanism of quarkonia, the bound state of heavy quark anti-quark (charm or bottom) pairs, in hadronic collisions. In experimental invesigations, the polarization is usually measured by analyzing the anisotropies in the angular distribution of the muons originating from the decay of the quarkonium state. In the present article, we study the charmonia ($J/ψ$) and bottomonia ($Υ(1S)$) polarization at $\sqrt{s} =7 $ and 13 TeV in proton-proton(p-p) collisions at LHC using Monte Carlo (MC) event generator model PYTHIA8, which is based on perturbative QCD. The transverse momentum ($p_{T}$) differential distribution has been calculated at forward rapidity ($2.5 < y_{μμ} < 4.0$) and the polarization parameters are estimated in Helicity and Collins-Sooper reference frames. In addition, to mimic realistic experimental conditions, we have incorporated, in PYTHIA simulations, effects like detector inefficiencies and muon momentum smearing. These contributions alter the polarization parameters, introducing an artificial degree of polarization, if not properly corrected for. The simulation results have been compared with the recent ALICE measurements for quarkonia polarization in p-p collisions at LHC energy regime.

Conclusion: The summary highlights the importance of precise calculations for trilinear scalar couplings and Higgs pair production in BSM models, which are essential for reconstructing the Higgs potential and exploring new physics. The advancements in these areas will significantly contribute to our understanding of the electroweak phase transition and BSM physics.

总结强调了在BSM模型中对三重标量耦合和希格斯对产生的精确计算的重要性，这对于重建希格斯势和探索新物理至关重要。这些领域的进展将显著促进我们对电弱相变和BSM物理的理解。

Abstract: Reconstructing the shape of the Higgs potential realised in Nature is one of the most pressing tasks of current and future colliders. This will offer deep insights into the dynamics of the electroweak phase transition and provide a unique opportunity to probe physics beyond the Standard Model (BSM). In this context, it is essential to have precise theory predictions for trilinear scalar couplings, which control the form of the potential, and for Higgs pair production processes, which are the observables that allow accessing the trilinear couplings. I summarise in these proceedings recent progress in precision calculations of both trilinear scalar couplings and Higgs pair production at the (HL-)LHC in BSM models with extended scalar sectors.

</details>


### [26] [$CP$ violation in singly Cabibbo suppressed $D\to πa_0(980)$ decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25875)
*Yu-Kuo Hsiao,Shu-Ting Cai,Yan-Li Wang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper discusses the measurements of branching-fraction ratios for the SCS decays $D \to \pi a_0$ and finds significant deviations from short-distance expectations, indicating the need to consider long-distance rescattering effects. These effects lead to direct $CP$ asymmetries at the ${\cal O}(10^{-3})$ level, suggesting a new way to probe $CP$ violation.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand the discrepancies between the measured branching-fraction ratios $r^{+/-}_{\rm ex}$ and $r^{+/0}_{\rm ex}$ for the SCS decays $D \to \pi a_0$ and the short-distance theoretical expectations. The large deviations indicate the importance of long-distance rescattering effects, which are essential for understanding $CP$ violation in these decays.

动机是理解SCS衰变$D \to \pi a_0$的测量分支比$r^{+/-}_{\rm ex}$和$r^{+/0}_{\rm ex}$与短程理论预期之间的差异。这些显著的偏差表明长程重散射效应的重要性，这对于理解这些衰变中的$CP$破坏至关重要。

Method: The method involves analyzing the measured branching-fraction ratios $r^{+/-}_{\rm ex}$ and $r^{+/0}_{\rm ex}$ for the SCS decays $D \to \pi a_0$. The authors highlight the necessity of considering long-distance rescattering effects, specifically the process $D \to K^*K \to a_0\pi$, which generates amplitudes ${\cal M}_s$ comparable in magnitude to ${\cal M}_d$. The strong phases associated with these amplitudes are crucial for $CP$ violation.

方法包括分析SCS衰变$D \to \pi a_0$的测量分支比$r^{+/-}_{\rm ex}$和$r^{+/0}_{\rm ex}$。作者强调了考虑长程重散射效应的必要性，特别是过程$D \to K^*K \to a_0\pi$，该过程生成的振幅${\cal M}_s$在大小上与${\cal M}_d$相当。与此振幅相关的强相位对于$CP$破坏至关重要。

Result: The results show that the direct $CP$ asymmetries in the SCS decays $D \to \pi a_0$ naturally arise at the ${\cal O}(10^{-3})$ level due to the nontrivial strong phases from long-distance rescattering effects. Specific values for the $CP$ asymmetries are given as ${\cal A}_{CP}(D^0 \to \pi^- a_0^+) = (-0.7 \pm 0.1 \pm 0.1 \pm 0.1) \times 10^{-3}$, ${\cal A}_{CP}(D^+ \to \pi^0 a_0^+) = (-1.4 \pm 0.1 \pm 0.1 \pm 0.1) \times 10^{-3}$, and ${\cal A}_{CP}(D^0 \to \pi^+ a_0^-) = (-2.1 \pm 0.9 \pm 1.1 \pm 0.4) \times 10^{-3}$.

结果表明，由于长程重散射效应带来的非平凡强相位，SCS衰变$D \to \pi a_0$中的直接$CP$不对称性自然出现在${\cal O}(10^{-3})$水平。具体的$CP$不对称性值为${\cal A}_{CP}(D^0 \to \pi^- a_0^+) = (-0.7 \pm 0.1 \pm 0.1 \pm 0.1) \times 10^{-3}$，${\cal A}_{CP}(D^+ \to \pi^0 a_0^+) = (-1.4 \pm 0.1 \pm 0.1 \pm 0.1) \times 10^{-3}$，以及${\cal A}_{CP}(D^0 \to \pi^+ a_0^-) = (-2.1 \pm 0.9 \pm 1.1 \pm 0.4) \times 10^{-3}$。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the SCS decays $D \to \pi a_0$ provide a new avenue for probing $CP$ violation, with the observed direct $CP$ asymmetries at the ${\cal O}(10^{-3})$ level. The significant deviations from short-distance expectations and the necessity of long-distance rescattering effects suggest that these decays are sensitive to subtle strong phase differences, making them a promising tool for future studies.

结论是，SCS衰变$D \to \pi a_0$为探测$CP$破坏提供了一条新的途径，观察到的直接$CP$不对称性在${\cal O}(10^{-3})$水平。与短程预期的显著偏差以及长程重散射效应的必要性表明，这些衰变对微妙的强相位差非常敏感，使其成为未来研究的有力工具。

Abstract: The singly Cabibbo suppressed (SCS) decays $D\to πa_0$, with $a_0\equiv a_0(980)$, have been measured with the branching-fraction ratios $r^{+/-}_{\rm ex}\equiv {\cal B}(D^0\toπ^- a_0^+)/{\cal B}(D^0\toπ^+ a_0^-)=7.5^{+2.5}_{-0.8}\pm 1.7$ and $r^{+/0}_{\rm ex}\equiv {\cal B}(D^+\toπ^0 a_0^+)/{\cal B}(D^+\toπ^+ a_0^0)=2.6\pm 0.6\pm 0.3$, deviating significantly from the short-distance expectations $(r^{+/-},r^{+/0})\simeq (0.07,0.2)$. This discrepancy indicates the necessity of long-distance rescattering effects. In particular, the process $D\to K^*K\to a_0π$ generates ${\cal M}_s$ comparable in magnitude to ${\cal M}_d$ in the amplitude ${\cal M}=λ_d{\cal M}_d+λ_s{\cal M}_s$, with $λ_q\equiv V_{cq}^*V_{uq}$, accompanied by nontrivial strong phases essential for $CP$ violation. Consequently, the direct $CP$ asymmetries naturally arise at the ${\cal O}(10^{-3})$ level, for example, ${\cal A}_{CP}(D^0\toπ^- a_0^+)=(-0.7\pm 0.1\pm 0.1\pm 0.1)\times 10^{-3}$, ${\cal A}_{CP}(D^+\toπ^0 a_0^+)=(-1.4\pm 0.1\pm 0.1\pm 0.1)\times 10^{-3}$, and ${\cal A}_{CP}(D^0\toπ^+ a_0^-)=(-2.1\pm 0.9\pm 1.1\pm 0.4)\times 10^{-3}$. These results establish SCS $D\to πa_0$ decays as a new avenue for probing $CP$ violation.

*Sven Bjarke Gudnason,Paul Leask*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper introduces cuSkyrmion, a 3D Skyrme model software for fast computation and visualization using CUDA C. It allows interactive construction of Skyrmions and is modular, with a Python version available.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to provide a powerful, user-friendly, and efficient tool for the study of Skyrmions in the Skyrme model, enabling both rapid computation and interactive visualization. This can facilitate research and education in the field of theoretical physics, particularly in the study of solitons and topological structures.

动机是提供一个强大、用户友好且高效的工具，用于研究Skyrme模型中的Skyrmions，实现快速计算和交互式可视化。这可以促进理论物理学领域，特别是孤子和拓扑结构研究中的研究和教育。

Method: The method involves developing a software named cuSkyrmion, which is written in CUDA C for GPU acceleration. The software consists of three main modules: a computational module, a rendering/visualization module, and a main program. Users can interactively construct Skyrmions using configuration files or through real-time input via keyboard and mouse. The software also supports the insertion of rational map ansatz Skyrmions and random initial configurations.

方法涉及开发一个名为cuSkyrmion的软件，该软件使用CUDA C编写以实现GPU加速。该软件由三个主要模块组成：计算模块、渲染/可视化模块和主程序。用户可以通过配置文件或通过键盘和鼠标实时输入来交互地构建Skyrmions。该软件还支持插入有理映射假设Skyrmions和随机初始配置。

Result: The result is a fully functional, interactive, and efficient 3D Skyrme model software that can be used for both research and educational purposes. The software, cuSkyrmion, provides a flexible and user-friendly interface for constructing and visualizing Skyrmions, and it is designed to be modular and reusable, with a Python fork available for broader use.

结果是一个完全功能、交互且高效的3D Skyrme模型软件，可用于研究和教育目的。该软件cuSkyrmion提供了灵活且用户友好的界面，用于构建和可视化Skyrmions，并设计为模块化和可重用，提供了一个Python版本以供更广泛使用。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that cuSkyrmion offers a significant advancement in the computational and visualization capabilities for studying Skyrmions. Its modular design, GPU acceleration, and interactive features make it a valuable tool for researchers and educators in the field of theoretical physics.

cuSkyrmion在研究Skyrmions的计算和可视化能力方面提供了显著的进步。其模块化设计、GPU加速和交互特性使其成为理论物理学领域的研究人员和教育工作者的宝贵工具。

Abstract: We introduce $\texttt{cuSkyrmion}$, a 3-dimensional Skyrme model computation and visualization software, that is written in CUDA C for rapid computation and visualization of especially the arrested Newton flow algorithm. The programme is interactive and lets the user construct Skyrmions either with configuration files, specifying coordinates, or simply in run-time using the keyboard and mouse. Rational map ansatz constituent Skyrmions can be inserted at any time and a random generator can produce a stochastic initial configuration. The software is composed into three main modules being a computational module, a rendering module and a main programme. The rendering/visualization module can readily be used by other computational modules and a Python-fork has been developed demonstrating the re-usability of the code.

### [28] [Explainable AI for Jet Tagging: A Comparative Study of GNNExplainer, GNNShap, and GradCAM for Jet Tagging in the Lund Jet Plane](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25885)
*Pahal D. Patel,Sanmay Ganguly*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper introduces and evaluates different explainability methods (perturbation-based, Shapley-value-based, and gradient-based) for graph neural networks in jet tagging at the LHC. It uses LundNet's Lund-plane graph representation and constructs Monte Carlo truth explanation masks to evaluate the quality of explanations. The analysis is performed in three transverse-momentum bins, and the correlation between explainer-assigned node importance and classical jet substructure observables is quantified, indicating that the model learns some aspects of known QCD features.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to provide a deeper understanding of the physical reasoning behind the predictions made by graph neural networks and transformer-based networks used in jet tagging at the Large Hadron Collider (LHC). Despite their state-of-the-art performance, the underlying mechanisms driving these predictions are not well understood. By introducing and evaluating different explainability methods, the authors aim to shed light on how these models learn and utilize physically meaningful information from the data.

本文的动机是深入理解在大型强子对撞机（LHC）喷流标记中使用的图神经网络和基于Transformer的网络所做出预测背后的物理推理。尽管这些模型具有最先进的性能，但驱动这些预测的基本机制尚不清楚。通过引入和评估不同的可解释性方法，作者旨在揭示这些模型是如何从数据中学习和利用具有物理意义的信息。

Method: The authors employ several explainability methods adapted to operate on LundNet's Lund-plane graph representation, including perturbation-based (GNNExplainer), Shapley-value-based (GNNShap), and gradient-based (GRADCam) approaches. They construct Monte Carlo truth explanation masks and introduce a physics-informed evaluation framework that goes beyond standard fidelity metrics. The analysis is conducted across three transverse-momentum bins: $\mathrm{p_T} \in [500,700]$, $[800,1000]$, and the inclusive region $[500,1000]$ GeV, to reveal how the quality and focus of explanations change between non-perturbative and perturbative regimes. Additionally, they quantify the correlation between explainer-assigned node importance and classical jet substructure observables, such as $N$-subjettiness ratios $\tau_{21}$ and $\tau_{32}$, and energy correlation functions.

作者采用了多种可解释性方法，这些方法适应于LundNet的Lund平面图表示，包括基于扰动的方法（GNNExplainer）、基于Shapley值的方法（GNNShap）和基于梯度的方法（GRADCam）。他们构建了蒙特卡洛真解释掩码，并引入了一个超越标准保真度指标的物理信息评估框架。分析在三个横向动量区间进行：$\mathrm{p_T} \in [500,700]$，$[800,1000]$ 和全包容区域 $[500,1000]$ GeV，以揭示在非微扰和微扰区之间解释的质量和焦点如何变化。此外，他们还量化了解释器分配节点重要性与经典喷流子结构可观测值之间的相关性，例如 $N$-subjettiness 比率 $\tau_{21}$ 和 $\tau_{32}$ 以及能量关联函数。

Result: The results show that the weight assigned by the explainability methods has a correlation with analytic observables, such as $N$-subjettiness ratios $\tau_{21}$ and $\tau_{32}$, and energy correlation functions. This indicates that the trained neural network indeed learns some aspects of known QCD features. The analysis also reveals how the quality and focus of explanations shift between non-perturbative and perturbative regimes across different transverse-momentum bins. The open-source implementation provided by the authors enables reproducible explainability studies for graph-based jet taggers.

结果表明，可解释性方法分配的权重与分析观测值（如 $N$-subjettiness 比率 $\tau_{21}$ 和 $\tau_{32}$ 以及能量关联函数）之间存在相关性。这表明训练好的神经网络确实学到了一些已知的QCD特征。分析还揭示了在不同横向动量区间内，解释的质量和焦点在非微扰和微扰区之间如何变化。作者提供的开源实现使基于图的喷流标记器的可解释性研究能够重现。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that the explainability methods can provide insights into the physical reasoning behind the predictions of graph neural networks used in jet tagging at the LHC. The correlation between the explainer-assigned node importance and classical jet substructure observables suggests that the models have learned some aspects of known QCD features. The work also highlights the importance of considering different phase space regimes when evaluating the quality of explanations. The open-source implementation paves the way for further research and reproducibility in this field.

研究表明，可解释性方法可以提供对用于LHC喷流标记的图神经网络预测背后的物理推理的见解。解释器分配节点重要性与经典喷流子结构可观测值之间的相关性表明，这些模型已经学到了一些已知的QCD特征。该工作还强调了在评估解释质量时考虑不同相空间区域的重要性。开源实现为这一领域的进一步研究和可重复性铺平了道路。

Abstract: Graph neural networks such as ParticleNet and transformer based networks on point clouds such as ParticleTransformer achieve state-of-the-art performance on jet tagging benchmarks at the Large Hadron Collider, yet the physical reasoning behind their predictions remains opaque. We present different methods, i.e. perturbation-based (GNNExplainer), Shapley-value-based (GNNShap), and gradient-based (GRADCam); adapted to operate on LundNet's Lund-plane graph representation. Leveraging the fact that each node in the Lund plane corresponds to a physically meaningful parton splitting, we construct Monte Carlo truth explanation masks and introduce a physics-informed evaluation framework that goes beyond standard fidelity metrics. We perform the analysis in three transverse-momentum bins ($\mathrm{p_T} \in [500,700]$, $[800,1000]$, and the inclusive region $[500,1000]$ GeV), revealing how explanation quality and focus shift between non-perturbative and perturbative regimes. We further quantify the correlation between explainer-assigned node importance and classical jet substructure observables -- $N$-subjettiness ratios $τ_{21}$ and $τ_{32}$ and the energy correlation functions -- establishing the degree to which the model has learned known QCD features. We find that overall the weight assigned by explainability methods has a correlation with analytic observables, with expected shift across different phase space regimes, indicating that a trained neural network indeed learns some aspects of jet-substructure moments. Our open-source implementation enables reproducible explainability studies for graph-based jet taggers.

### [29] [Gauging Axionic Symmetries and Dark Matter: In memory of George Lazarides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25888)
*Claudio Corianò*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper revisits a joint work on the cosmology of a gauged axion and its connection to anomalous gauge symmetries, orientifold effective actions, Stueckelberg fields, and dark matter. It highlights the unique cosmological history of the physical axion-like state that emerges after Higgs-Stueckelberg mixing and sequential electroweak and QCD misalignment, which can contribute to dark matter only if the Stueckelberg scale is large. The work is dedicated to George Lazarides for his contributions to understanding the interplay between particle physics and early universe cosmology.

该论文回顾了关于规范轴子宇宙学的联合工作，并将其与异常规范对称性、定向折叠有效作用量、Stueckelberg场和暗物质联系起来。它强调了在Higgs-Stueckelberg混合和顺序电弱和QCD错位后出现的物理轴子类状态的独特宇宙历史，只有当Stueckelberg尺度足够大时，这种状态才能对暗物质有显著贡献。这篇论文献给George Lazarides，感谢他对粒子物理学和早期宇宙之间相互作用的理解所做出的贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to honor the memory of George Lazarides by revisiting and expanding upon a previous collaboration that explored the cosmology of a gauged axion. The aim is to place this work in a broader context, connecting it with the ideas of anomalous gauge symmetries, orientifold effective actions, Stueckelberg fields, and their implications for dark matter. This perspective emphasizes the importance of understanding the vacuum structure of axion models in conjunction with the gauge structure in which they are embedded, as originally proposed by George Lazarides.

本文的动机是通过回顾和扩展之前的合作研究来纪念George Lazarides，该合作探讨了规范轴子的宇宙学。目的是将这项工作置于更广泛的背景下，将其与异常规范对称性、定向折叠有效作用量、Stueckelberg场及其对暗物质的影响联系起来。这一视角强调了理解轴子模型的真空结构与其嵌入的规范结构相结合的重要性，这是George Lazarides最初提出的观点。

Method: The method involves a theoretical analysis of the cosmological implications of a gauged axion within the framework of an anomalous extra $U(1)$ symmetry. The approach includes the examination of how the Stueckelberg pseudoscalar participates in the restoration of gauge invariance through Wess-Zumino counterterms and the subsequent emergence of a physical axion-like state after electroweak symmetry breaking. The analysis also considers the sequential electroweak and QCD misalignment effects on the axion's cosmological history and its potential contribution to the dark matter relic abundance.

方法涉及在一个异常额外$U(1)$对称性的框架内，对规范轴子的宇宙学意义进行理论分析。这种方法包括考察Stueckelberg伪标量如何通过Wess-Zumino反项参与恢复规范不变性，以及在电弱对称性破缺后物理轴子类状态的出现。分析还考虑了顺序电弱和QCD错位效应对轴子宇宙历史的影响及其对暗物质遗迹丰度的潜在贡献。

Result: The results highlight that the physical axion-like state, which appears after Higgs-Stueckelberg mixing, has a distinct cosmological history compared to an ordinary Peccei-Quinn axion. This state undergoes sequential electroweak and QCD misalignment and can contribute significantly to the dark matter relic abundance only if the Stueckelberg scale is sufficiently large. This finding underscores the importance of the interplay between the gauge structure and the vacuum structure of axion models in determining the properties of dark matter candidates.

结果强调，在Higgs-Stueckelberg混合后出现的物理轴子类状态与普通的Peccei-Quinn轴子相比具有独特的宇宙历史。该状态经历了顺序电弱和QCD错位效应，只有当Stueckelberg尺度足够大时，才能对暗物质遗迹丰度产生显著贡献。这一发现强调了规范结构与轴子模型真空结构之间的相互作用在确定暗物质候选者性质方面的重要性。

Conclusion: The conclusion of the paper is that the cosmological history and dark matter potential of the gauged axion are intimately tied to the Stueckelberg mechanism and the associated gauge structure. The physical axion-like state, which arises from Higgs-Stueckelberg mixing, has a unique evolution that is different from that of an ordinary Peccei-Quinn axion. This work provides a deeper understanding of the role of anomalous gauge symmetries and Stueckelberg fields in the context of axion cosmology and dark matter, honoring the legacy of George Lazarides.

论文的结论是，规范轴子的宇宙历史和暗物质潜力与Stueckelberg机制及其相关的规范结构密切相关。从Higgs-Stueckelberg混合中产生的物理轴子类状态具有与普通Peccei-Quinn轴子不同的独特演化。这项工作提供了对异常规范对称性和Stueckelberg场在轴子宇宙学和暗物质背景下的作用的更深入理解，以纪念George Lazarides的遗产。

Abstract: These notes are written for a memorial Session dedicated to George Lazarides. They revisit a joint work on the cosmology of a gauged axion and place it in a broader line of ideas connecting anomalous gauge symmetries, orientifold effective actions, Stueckelberg fields and dark matter. In models with an anomalous extra $U(1)$ symmetry, the Stueckelberg pseudoscalar participates in the restoration of gauge invariance through Wess-Zumino counterterms and, after electroweak symmetry breaking, may leave a physical axion-like state. Its cosmological history differs from that of an ordinary Peccei-Quinn axion: the physical field appears only after Higgs-Stueckelberg mixing, is subject to sequential electroweak and QCD misalignment, and can give an appreciable dark-matter relic abundance only when the Stueckelberg scale is sufficiently large. This perspective connects naturally with George's earlier insight that the vacuum structure of axion models must be understood together with the gauge structure in which it is embedded. I dedicate these notes to his memory, with gratitude for the collaboration and for the clarity with which he connected particle physics to the early universe.

### [30] [Emergent Features in $U(N) \times U(\tilde{N})$ Bi-adjoint Cubic Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24830)
*Lauren Smyth*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper explores the $U(N) \times U(\tilde{N})$ global symmetry in tree-level scattering amplitudes of the bi-adjoint $\phi^3$ theory from combinatorial, correlation function, and a massive extension of the CHY formalism perspectives. It derives a planar scattering potential, counts kinematic invariants using Ferrers shapes, and provides a physical interpretation of Catalan recursion relations. The study also constructs correlation functions for a fixed particle ordering and derives an off-shell scattering potential.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand the role of the $U(N) \times U(\tilde{N})$ global symmetry in the context of tree-level scattering amplitudes of the bi-adjoint $\phi^3$ theory. This involves exploring the symmetry's implications on combinatorics, correlation functions, and the CHY formalism, with the aim of providing deeper insights into the dynamics of these amplitude structures. 

动机是理解$U(N) \times U(\tilde{N})$全局对称性在双伴随$\phi^3$理论的树级散射振幅中的作用。这包括探索该对称性在组合、关联函数和CHY形式主义中的影响，目的是更深入地了解这些振幅结构的动力学。

Method: The method involves three main approaches: (1) Combinatorics, where a planar scattering potential is derived whose extrema reproduce Dolan and Goddard's massive scattering equations, and kinematic invariants are counted via maximally symmetric Ferrers shapes; (2) Correlation functions, where the CHY formalism is used to construct correlation functions for a fixed particle ordering; (3) A massive extension of the CHY formalism, which provides a new perspective on the dynamics of the amplitude structures. 

方法涉及三个主要方面：（1）组合，其中导出了一个平面散射势，其极值再现了Dolan和Goddard的大质量散射方程，并通过最大对称的Ferrers形状来计数运动学不变量；（2）关联函数，其中使用CHY形式主义为固定粒子顺序构建关联函数；（3）CHY形式主义的大质量扩展，为振幅结构的动力学提供了新的视角。

Result: The results include the derivation of a planar scattering potential that reproduces the massive scattering equations, the counting of kinematic invariants using Ferrers shapes, and the construction of correlation functions for a fixed particle ordering. Additionally, a closed form expression for the reduced number of solutions and an off-shell scattering potential are derived. 

结果包括导出了再现大质量散射方程的平面散射势，使用Ferrers形状计数运动学不变量，以及为固定粒子顺序构建关联函数。此外，还推导了减少解数量的封闭形式表达式和一个非壳散射势。

Conclusion: The work concludes by providing a deeper understanding of the $U(N) \times U(\tilde{N})$ global symmetry in the context of bi-adjoint $\phi^3$ theory, particularly through the lens of combinatorial, correlation function, and CHY formalism perspectives. The findings offer new insights into the dynamics of such amplitude structures and provide a framework for further exploration. 

研究通过组合、关联函数和CHY形式主义的角度，提供了对双伴随$\phi^3$理论中$U(N) \times U(\tilde{N})$全局对称性的更深入理解。这些发现为这种振幅结构的动力学提供了新的见解，并为进一步探索提供了一个框架。

Abstract: This work investigates the role of the $U(N) \times U(\tilde{N})$ global symmetry in tree-level scattering amplitudes of the bi-adjoint $φ^3$ theory from three perspectives: combinatorics, correlation functions, and a massive extension of the CHY formalism. We derive a planar scattering potential whose extrema reproduce Dolan and Goddard's massive scattering equations, providing physical intuition of the construction. This potential enables the counting of kinematic invariants via maximally symmetric Ferrers shapes, and it is expressed in terms of conformally invariant cross-ratios. We find that the $U(1)$ decoupling identity provides a physical interpretation of two different Catalan recursion relations, and also reveals an interplay between Catalan and Narayana numbers in the $U(1)$ splitting. Finally, we construct correlation functions for a fixed particle ordering using the CHY formalism, offering new insights into the dynamics of such amplitude structures. We derive a closed form expression of the reduced number of solutions for this set-up, as well as an off-shell scattering potential.

### [31] [Revisiting near-extremal and near-BPS black holes in AdS3 supergravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24834)
*Adam Bac,Alejandra Castro,Diksha Jain*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper systematically investigates the behavior of the Euclidean path integral at low temperatures in AdS3 supergravity, focusing on quantum fluctuations in both near-horizon and asymptotic regions. It clarifies and corrects aspects of bosonic fluctuations, emphasizing the role of boundary conditions, and shows that the gravitational path integral in the near-horizon region is different from that around BTZ at low temperature. The analysis also includes contributions from Chern-Simons fields and spin-3/2 modes, refining the differences between near-extremal and near-BPS limits at low temperature, and highlighting a disagreement in the gravitational path integral at the quantum level.

该论文系统地研究了AdS3超引力中低温下的欧几里得路径积分的行为，重点关注近视界和渐近区域的量子涨落。它澄清并纠正了玻色涨落的某些方面，强调了边界条件的作用，并表明近视界区域的引力路径积分与低温下的BTZ周围的引力路径积分不同。分析还包括来自Chern-Simons场和自旋-3/2模式的贡献，细化了低温下近极值和近BPS极限之间的差异，并突出了量子水平上引力路径积分的不一致。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation for this study is to address the imprecise and incomplete features of the BTZ background in quantifying quantum aspects of black holes, particularly at low temperatures. Method: The method involves a systematic investigation of the Euclidean path integral at low temperatures in AdS3 supergravity, analyzing quantum fluctuations in both the near-horizon and asymptotic regions. 该方法涉及在AdS3超引力中系统地研究低温下的欧几里得路径积分，分析近视界和渐近区域的量子涨落。研究澄清并纠正了玻色涨落的某些方面，强调了AdS3中边界条件的作用。此外，还考虑了Chern-Simons场和自旋-3/2模式的贡献，细化了低温下近极值和近BPS极限之间的差异。

Result: The results show that the gravitational path integral in the near-horizon region is inequivalent to that around BTZ at low temperature. The analysis also highlights the importance of boundary conditions and the contributions of Chern-Simons fields and spin-3/2 modes, leading to a refined understanding of the disparities between the near-extremal and near-BPS limits. The study demonstrates a disagreement in the gravitational path integral at the quantum level, sharpening the distinction between near- and far-region dynamics.

结果表明，近视界区域的引力路径积分与低温下的BTZ周围的引力路径积分不同。分析还强调了边界条件的重要性以及Chern-Simons场和自旋-3/2模式的贡献，从而细化了近极值和近BPS极限之间的差异。研究表明，在量子水平上引力路径积分存在不一致，进一步明确了近视界和远区域动力学之间的区别。

Conclusion: The paper concludes by demonstrating a disagreement in the gravitational path integral at the quantum level, which sharpens the distinction between near- and far-region dynamics. The study provides a more precise understanding of the behavior of the Euclidean path integral in the context of AdS3 supergravity, including the roles of boundary conditions and the contributions of various fields and modes.

该论文通过展示量子水平上引力路径积分的不一致，进一步明确了近视界和远区域动力学之间的区别。研究提供了在AdS3超引力背景下对欧几里得路径积分行为的更精确理解，包括边界条件的作用以及各种场和模式的贡献。

Abstract: Despite the archetypal status of the BTZ background in quantifying quantum aspects of black holes, several features at low temperatures remain imprecise and incomplete. Here, we systematically investigate the behaviour of the Euclidean path integral at low temperatures in the context of AdS3 supergravity, including an analysis of quantum fluctuations in both the near-horizon and asymptotic regions. We clarify and rectify aspects of the bosonic fluctuations, highlighting the role of boundary conditions in AdS3, and show in particular that the gravitational path integral in the near-horizon region is inequivalent to that around BTZ at low temperature. We further account in detail for the contributions of Chern-Simons fields and spin-3/2 modes, thereby refining the disparities between the near-extremal and near-BPS limits at low temperature. Altogether, our analysis sharpens the distinction between near- and far-region dynamics and demonstrates a disagreement in the gravitational path integral at the quantum level.

### [33] [Optimal paths across potentials on scalar field space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24843)
*Saskia Demulder,Dieter Lust,Carmine Montella,Thomas Raml*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper uses Optimal Transport to define a (generalized) Wasserstein distance in field space, linking it to the Swampland Distance Conjecture. It relates the transport problem to Hamilton-Jacobi and continuity equations without dynamical gravity, and extends this to include gravity via the ADM formalism and the Wheeler-DeWitt equation.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the Swampland Distance Conjecture, which posits constraints on the allowed effective field theories. By employing Optimal Transport, the authors aim to provide a rigorous mathematical framework to quantify distances in field space, thereby offering new insights into the conjecture and its implications for quantum gravity and string theory.

Method: The method employs the framework of Optimal Transport to define a (generalized) Wasserstein distance between probability distributions over field space. In scenarios without dynamical gravity, the transport problem is linked to Hamilton-Jacobi and continuity equations derived from a WKB expansion of the Schrödinger equation. For cases with dynamical gravity, the ADM formalism is used to formulate the transport problem through the Wheeler-DeWitt equation, introducing different cost functions.

Result: The results include a definition of a (generalized) Wasserstein distance in field space, which is related to the physical configuration through the Schrödinger equation in the absence of dynamical gravity. In the presence of dynamical gravity, the ADM formalism and the Wheeler-DeWitt equation are used to extend the framework, leading to various choices of cost functions. These distances are defined on the full configuration space, with potential modifications needed for scalar field distances.

Conclusion: The study introduces a novel approach to understanding distances in field space using Optimal Transport, leading to a generalized Wasserstein distance. It connects the transport problem to Hamilton-Jacobi and continuity equations in the absence of dynamical gravity, and extends this framework to include dynamical gravity via the ADM formalism and the Wheeler-DeWitt equation. The resulting distance notions are applicable to the full configuration space, with potential implications for the Swampland program.

Abstract: Motivated by the Swampland Distance Conjecture, we study distances in field space using the framework of Optimal Transport. The associated optimisation problem naturally leads to a notion of distance in terms of a (generalised) Wasserstein distance between probability distributions over field space. In the absence of dynamical gravity, we relate the transport problem to Hamilton-Jacobi and continuity equations arising from a WKB expansion of a Schrödinger equation associated with the physical configuration. We then formulate an extension in the presence of dynamical gravity. Using the ADM formalism, we establish the corresponding transport problem through the Wheeler-DeWitt equation, giving rise to different possible choices of cost functions. The resulting notions of distances are naturally defined on the full configuration space, while an interpretation in terms of a genuine scalar field distance requires additional modifications. We further discuss several applications and examples, and indicate possible implications for different themes within the Swampland program.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation behind this work is to explore the structure of scattering amplitudes in a curved spacetime, specifically in global de Sitter spacetime. Understanding these amplitudes in such a setting can provide deeper insights into quantum field theories in non-trivial backgrounds and potentially lead to new theoretical frameworks.

这项工作的动机是探索弯曲时空中的散射振幅结构，特别是全局德西特时空中。在这种背景下理解这些振幅可以提供对非平凡背景下的量子场论更深入的理解，并可能引出新的理论框架。

Method: The method involves the use of intertwiner integrals of harmonic one-forms on the three-sphere to determine the three-gluon scattering amplitudes at the tree level. 该研究提供了在德西特时空中的三胶子散射振幅的一般公式，用Wigner 3j符号表示。该结果对所有螺旋度构型都有效，并为弯曲时空中的这些振幅结构提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We study three-gluon scattering amplitudes in global de Sitter spacetime, in the angular momentum basis of SO(1,4) symmetry representations. At the tree level, they are determined by the intertwiner integrals of harmonic one-forms on the three-sphere. We derive a general formula valid for all helicity configurations of incoming and outgoing gluons and express the amplitudes in terms of Wigner 3j symbols.

### [35] [On the structure of higher-dimensional integrable field theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24864)
*Marco Benini,Ryan A. Cullinan,Alexander Schenkel,Benoit Vicedo*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper introduces a general framework for integrable field theories in any spacetime dimension using $d$-term $L_\infty$-algebras, specifically focusing on topological-holomorphic higher Chern-Simons theories. It employs homological perturbation theory and homotopy transfer to construct equivalent models that are integrable, as evidenced by the existence of conserved charges. The framework is shown to generalize the Costello-Yamazaki construction to higher dimensions.

该论文提出了一种使用$d$-项$L_\infty$-代数在任意时空维度中的可积场论的一般框架，特别关注拓扑-全纯高阶Chern-Simons理论。它利用同调扰动理论和同伦转移构建了等价模型，并通过存在守恒荷证明了这些模型的可积性。该框架展示了如何将Costello-Yamazaki构造推广到更高维度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation behind this work is to develop a general and mathematically rigorous framework for constructing integrable field theories in arbitrary dimensions. By leveraging the power of $L_\infty$-algebras, the authors aim to provide a systematic way to understand and generate integrable systems, which are important in both theoretical physics and mathematics due to their rich structure and solvability. This approach not only unifies various known constructions but also opens up new possibilities for exploring integrability in higher-dimensional settings.

本文的工作动机是开发一种在任意维度下构建可积场论的一般且数学上严格的框架。通过利用$L_\infty$-代数的力量，作者旨在提供一种系统的方法来理解和生成可积系统。由于其丰富的结构和可解性，这些系统在理论物理和数学中都非常重要。这种方法不仅统一了各种已知的构造方法，而且为探索更高维度下的可积性开辟了新的可能性。

Method: The method involves the use of $d$-term $L_\infty$-algebras to describe topological-holomorphic higher Chern-Simons theories on manifolds of the form $M \times \mathbb{C}P^1$. These algebras are cyclic and controlled by a meromorphic $1$-form on $\mathbb{C}P^1$, which dictates the singularity structures and boundary conditions. Homological perturbation theory and homotopy transfer are then employed to construct weakly equivalent, but more tractable, models of these theories. The integrability of these models is demonstrated through the existence of a natural map to an $L_\infty$-algebra describing higher Lax connections, which yields conserved charges associated with higher-dimensional cycles in $M$.

该方法涉及使用$d$-项$L_\infty$-代数来描述形式为$M \times \mathbb{C}P^1$的流形上的拓扑-全纯高阶Chern-Simons理论。这些代数是循环的，并由$\mathbb{C}P^1$上的亚纯$1$-形式控制，该形式决定了奇点结构和边界条件。然后利用同调扰动理论和同伦转移来构建这些理论的弱等价但更易于处理的模型。通过存在一个自然映射到描述高阶Lax联络的$L_\infty$-代数，这些模型的可积性得以展示，这产生了与$M$中高维周期相关的守恒荷。

Result: The result is the successful construction of a general framework for integrable field theories in $(d+1)$-dimensions based on $d$-term $L_\infty$-algebras. This framework allows for the description of topological-holomorphic higher Chern-Simons theories with specific singularity structures and boundary conditions. The constructed models are shown to be integrable, with the existence of conserved charges related to higher-dimensional cycles. Additionally, the framework recovers the Costello-Yamazaki construction in two dimensions, thereby providing a consistent generalization to higher dimensions.

结果成功地基于$d$-项$L_\infty$-代数构建了一个$(d+1)$维可积场论的一般框架。该框架允许描述具有特定奇点结构和边界条件的拓扑-全纯高阶Chern-Simons理论。所构建的模型被证明是可积的，存在与高维周期相关的守恒荷。此外，该框架在二维情况下恢复了Costello-Yamazaki构造，从而提供了一致的推广到更高维度。

Conclusion: The conclusion drawn from this work is that $d$-term $L_\infty$-algebras provide a powerful and flexible tool for constructing integrable field theories in arbitrary dimensions. The ability to recover known results in two dimensions while extending them to higher dimensions demonstrates the robustness and generality of the proposed framework. This paves the way for further exploration into the rich structure of integrable systems and their applications in theoretical physics and mathematics.

从这项工作中得出的结论是，$d$-项$L_\infty$-代数为在任意维度下构建可积场论提供了强大而灵活的工具。能够在二维情况下恢复已知结果的同时将其扩展到更高维度，展示了所提框架的稳健性和普遍性。这为进一步探索可积系统的丰富结构及其在理论物理和数学中的应用铺平了道路。

Abstract: We propose a general framework for integrable field theories in arbitrary spacetime dimension $d+1$ which is based on $d$-term $L_\infty$-algebras. Specifically, we introduce cyclic $L_\infty$-algebras describing topological-holomorphic higher Chern-Simons theories on $M \times \mathbb{C}P^1$ with suitable singularity structures and boundary conditions, controlled by a meromorphic $1$-form on $\mathbb{C}P^1$. Using homological perturbation theory and homotopy transfer, we construct weakly equivalent models describing $(d+1)$-dimensional field theories on $M$. Their integrability is witnessed by a natural map to an $L_\infty$-algebra describing higher Lax connections, yielding conserved charges associated with higher-dimensional cycles in $M$. The resulting theories admit natural action functionals and recover the Costello-Yamazaki construction in $2$ dimensions.

Abstract: Self-dual theories are powerful toy models of their completions. It was shown recently that there are infinitely many SD-theories once massless higher-spin fields are allowed. This entropy is expressed as a function of pressure and angular momentum, derived from the Brown-York stress tensor. Additional discussions include the second law, factors of $i$, and connections to JT gravity.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand the thermodynamics of cosmological horizons in de Sitter space and to map these laws to a holographic description at future infinity, $\mathcal{I}^+$. The goal is to derive a universal form of the first law of thermodynamics that applies when matter-energy crosses both horizons and interacts with the boundary, leading to a well-defined notion of entropy in the holographic dual.

动机是理解de Sitter空间中宇宙视界的热力学，并将这些定律映射到未来无穷远的全息描述，$\mathcal{I}^+$。目标是推导出一个普遍形式的第一热力学定律，当物质-能量穿过两个视界并与边界相互作用时，该定律适用，并在全息对偶中得出一个明确的熵概念。

Method: The method involves analyzing the thermodynamic laws governing the behavior of cosmological horizons in de Sitter space and mapping them to a holographic description at future infinity, $\mathcal{I}^+$. The authors derive a universal form of the first law of thermodynamics that is valid in general circumstances, where matter-energy crosses both horizons and impinges on the boundary. This leads to a well-defined notion of entropy specified on a co-dimension one surface of the boundary, which can be expressed as a function of two boundary charges, pressure and angular momentum, both of which are derived from the Brown-York stress tensor. Additional discussions include the second law, confusing factors of $i$, and comments on JT gravity.

方法涉及分析de Sitter空间中宇宙视界的热力学定律，并将其映射到未来无穷远的全息描述，$\mathcal{I}^+$。作者推导出了一个普遍形式的第一热力学定律，该定律在一般情况下有效，即物质-能量穿过两个视界并与边界相互作用。这导致了在边界的一个余维一表面上定义良好的熵概念，该熵可以表示为两个边界电荷（压力和角动量）的函数，这两个电荷都来自Brown-York应力张量。此外，还讨论了第二定律、令人困惑的$i$因子以及关于JT引力的评论。

Result: A universal form of the first law of thermodynamics is derived, which is valid when matter-energy crosses both cosmological horizons and impinges on the boundary. This leads to a well-defined notion of entropy on the boundary, which can be expressed as a function of two boundary charges, pressure and angular momentum, both derived from the Brown-York stress tensor. Additional results include insights into the second law, clarification of confusing factors of $i$, and comments on JT gravity.

推导出了一个普遍形式的第一热力学定律，该定律在物质-能量穿过两个宇宙视界并与边界相互作用时有效。这导致了在边界上定义良好的熵概念，该熵可以表示为两个边界电荷（压力和角动量）的函数，这两个电荷都来自Brown-York应力张量。此外，还包括对第二定律的见解、对令人困惑的$i$因子的澄清以及关于JT引力的评论。

Conclusion: The study provides a deeper understanding of the thermodynamics of cosmological horizons in de Sitter space and their holographic description at future infinity, $\mathcal{I}^+$. The universal form of the first law of thermodynamics derived in this work leads to a well-defined notion of entropy on the boundary, expressed as a function of pressure and angular momentum. The results also shed light on the second law, clarify factors of $i$, and provide insights into JT gravity.

研究提供了对de Sitter空间中宇宙视界的热力学及其在未来无穷远处的全息描述的更深入理解，$\mathcal{I}^+$。本文推导出的第一热力学定律的普遍形式导致了在边界上定义良好的熵概念，该熵可以表示为压力和角动量的函数。结果还阐明了第二定律，澄清了$i$因子，并提供了对JT引力的见解。

Abstract: We analyse the laws of thermodynamics governing the behaviour of cosmological horizons in de Sitter space and their map to a holographic description at future infinity, $\mathcal{I}^+$. In this case, the boundary can receive signals from two cosmological horizons. We find a universal form for the first law of thermodynamics, valid in general circumstances, when matter-energy crosses both horizons and impinges on the boundary. This universal form leads to a well defined notion of entropy in the holographic dual. It is specified on a co-dimension one surface of the boundary, and can be expressed as a function of two boundary charges, pressure and angular momentum, both of which are derived from the Brown-York stress tensor. Additional comments on the second law, confusing factors of $i$ which arise, and comments pertaining to JT gravity, are included towards the end.

### [38] [Path integral for the closed superstring and the matrix model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25052)
*Yuhma Asano*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper addresses the ambiguity in the path integral of the IKKT matrix model by revisiting and reformulating the path-integral approach for perturbative string theory, particularly in Minkowski signature. It establishes equivalences among different formulations (Nambu-Goto, Schild, Polyakov) and demonstrates stringy causality, leading to a Minkowskian version of the NBI-type IKKT matrix model.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to resolve the ambiguity in the definition of the path integral for the IKKT matrix model, which is a non-perturbative formulation of superstring theory. The authors aim to provide a more rigorous and consistent framework for the path integral, especially in the Minkowski signature, where such ambiguities are more pronounced.

动机是解决IKKT矩阵模型路径积分定义中的模糊性，IKKT矩阵模型是超弦理论的一种非微扰形式。作者旨在为路径积分提供一个更严格和一致的框架，特别是在闵可夫斯基签名中，这种模糊性更为明显。

Method: The method involves a detailed review and derivation of the Minkowskian path integral for critical closed string theory, showing equivalences between the Nambu-Goto, Schild, and Polyakov formulations. The authors also demonstrate that stringy causality is realized in the path-integral formulation at the level of string perturbation theory. They then apply matrix regularization to the path integral for perturbative type IIB string theory to obtain a Minkowskian version of the NBI-type IKKT matrix model.

该方法包括对临界闭弦理论的闵可夫斯基路径积分进行详细的回顾和推导，展示Nambu-Goto、Schild和Polyakov公式之间的等价性。作者还证明了在弦微扰理论水平上，路径积分公式中实现了“弦因果性”。然后，他们将矩阵正则化应用于IIB型微扰弦理论的路径积分，得到了NBI型IKKT矩阵模型的闵可夫斯基版本。

Result: The results include the derivation of the Minkowskian path integral for the Nambu-Goto type, equivalent to Polyakov's Euclidean path integral for critical closed string theory. The authors establish equivalences among the Nambu-Goto, Schild, and Polyakov formulations in both Minkowskian and Euclidean signatures. They also show that stringy causality is realized in the path-integral formulation. Finally, they derive a Minkowskian version of the NBI-type IKKT matrix model with properties similar to stringy causality.

结果包括推导出Nambu-Goto类型的闵可夫斯基路径积分，这与Polyakov的欧几里得路径积分对于临界闭弦理论是等价的。作者建立了Nambu-Goto、Schild和Polyakov公式在闵可夫斯基和欧几里得签名中的等价性。他们还证明了在路径积分公式中实现了弦因果性。最后，他们推导出了具有类似弦因果性性质的NBI型IKKT矩阵模型的闵可夫斯基版本。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that by revisiting the path-integral formulation of perturbative string theory, the authors have provided a more robust and consistent framework for the IKKT matrix model. This includes the derivation of the Minkowskian path integral, the establishment of equivalences among different formulations, and the realization of stringy causality. The resulting Minkowskian version of the NBI-type IKKT matrix model provides a new perspective on the non-perturbative formulation of superstring theory.

结论是，通过重新审视微扰弦理论的路径积分公式，作者为IKKT矩阵模型提供了一个更稳健和一致的框架。这包括推导出闵可夫斯基路径积分，建立不同公式之间的等价性，以及实现弦因果性。由此得到的NBI型IKKT矩阵模型的闵可夫斯基版本为超弦理论的非微扰形式提供了新的视角。

Abstract: The IKKT matrix model, which is proposed as a non-perturbative formulation of superstring theory, has an issue typical of zero-dimensional theory -- ambiguity in the definition of its path integral. To tackle this issue, we revisit the path-integral formulation of perturbative string theory. In this article, we review recent progress in the string world-sheet path-integral formulation, especially in the Minkowski signature. We first derive the Minkowskian path integral of the Nambu-Goto type equivalent to Polyakov's Euclidean path integral for critical closed string theory, showing equivalences among the Nambu-Goto-, Schild- and Polyakov-type formulations both in the Minkowskian and Euclidean signatures. We also show that ``stringy causality'' is realised in the path-integral formulation at the level of string perturbation theory. We then obtain the matrix model with a property like the stringy causality, which turns out to be a Minkowskian version of the NBI-type IKKT matrix model, by matrix regularisation of the path integral for perturbative type IIB string theory.

### [39] [Thermodynamic Phase Transitions in Einstein-Maxwell-Scalar-Gauss-Bonnet Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25100)
*Cristián Erices,Stella Kiorpelidi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper explores the thermodynamic phase transitions in electrically charged black holes within the Einstein-Maxwell-Scalar-Gauss-Bonnet (EMSG) theory. It shows that curvature-induced scalarization can lead to nontrivial thermodynamic behavior, including second-order and zeroth-order phase transitions, without requiring external confining mechanisms or extended thermodynamic formalisms. The study reveals a complex structure of free energy, leading to up to three phase transitions as the coupling strength increases, with the Reissner-Nordström phase becoming the preferred configuration in the strong-coupling limit.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to investigate the thermodynamic properties of electrically charged black holes in the context of EMSG theory, specifically focusing on the role of curvature-induced scalarization. The authors aim to demonstrate that such scalarization can naturally lead to nontrivial thermodynamic behavior, including phase transitions, without the need for additional confining mechanisms or extended thermodynamic formalisms. This exploration is significant because it provides a new perspective on the thermodynamics of black holes, particularly in theories beyond general relativity.

Method: The method involves working within the canonical ensemble and using the Euclidean approach to analyze the thermodynamic behavior of electrically charged black holes in EMSG theory. The authors identify the coexistence of locally stable scalarized and small Reissner-Nordström thermal states, which leads to free-energy crossings and phase transitions. They also examine how the nature of these phase transitions changes with the coupling strength, from second-order to zeroth-order, and how the Helmholtz free energy structure evolves.

Result: The results show that for weak coupling, a second-order phase transition occurs at the second bifurcation point where the scalarized branch reconnects with the Reissner-Nordström branch. As the coupling strength increases, this transition becomes zeroth order, and the scalarized branch shrinks, leading to a fish-like structure in the Helmholtz free energy. This structure renders some locally stable thermal states partially metastable and can yield up to three phase transitions. In the strong-coupling limit, the scalarized branch reduces to a Schwarzschild-like solution, and the Reissner-Nordström phase emerges as the preferred thermodynamic configuration.

Conclusion: The conclusion is that curvature-induced scalarization in EMSG theory can lead to rich and nontrivial thermodynamic behavior in electrically charged black holes. The study demonstrates that phase transitions can occur naturally without the need for external confining mechanisms or extended thermodynamic formalisms. The nature of these phase transitions and the structure of the Helmholtz free energy are shown to depend on the coupling strength, with the Reissner-Nordström phase becoming the dominant configuration in the strong-coupling limit.

Abstract: Although asymptotically flat black holes generically lack thermodynamic phase transitions, we show that curvature-induced scalarization of electrically charged black holes in Einstein-Maxwell- Scalar-Gauss-Bonnet theory provides a natural setting for nontrivial thermodynamic behavior, without invoking external confining mechanisms or an extended thermodynamic formalism. Working within the canonical ensemble and employing the Euclidean approach, we identify the coexistence of locally stable scalarized and small Reissner-Nordström thermal states, which promotes free-energy crossings to bona fide phase transitions between equilibrium phases. For weak coupling, a second-order phase transition coincides with the second bifurcation point, at which the scalarized branch reconnects with the Reissner-Nordström branch and scalar hair is spontaneously shed. As the coupling strength increases, this transition becomes zeroth order, the scalarized branch shrinks, and a fish-like structure develops in its Helmholtz free energy, rendering locally stable thermal states partially metastable, and yielding up to three phase transitions. In the strong-coupling limit, the scalarized branch reduces to a Schwarzschild-like solution, and the Reissner-Nordström phase ultimately emerges as the sole thermodynamically preferred configuration

*P. Beretta,A. Codello*

TL;DR: A new Functional Dimensional Regularization (FDR) scheme is proposed, combining the agility of dimensional regularization with the generality of functional RG, leading to faster convergence and better estimates for critical exponents in the Ising universality class in three dimensions.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to develop a more efficient and accurate renormalization group (RG) calculation method for critical phenomena by extending the use of dimensional regularization (DR) beyond the typical $\varepsilon$-expansion. The goal is to combine the advantages of DR with the general approach of functional RG.

动机是通过将维度正则化(DR)的使用扩展到典型的$\varepsilon$-展开之外，来开发一种更高效、更准确的临界现象重正化群(RG)计算方法。目标是将DR的优点与泛函RG的一般方法结合起来。

Method: The authors propose a novel method called Functional Dimensional Regularization (FDR), which extends the use of dimensional regularization beyond the usual $\varepsilon$-expansion. This method is then applied to a scalar theory in three dimensions, where they compute the critical exponents of the Ising universality class under various approximations.

Result: The results show that the FDR method can be effectively used to calculate the critical exponents of the Ising universality class directly in $d=3$. The method demonstrates faster convergence and better accuracy compared to other functional RG methods at the same order of approximation.

Conclusion: The new Functional Dimensional Regularization (FDR) scheme, which combines the agility of dimensional regularization with the generality of functional RG, provides faster convergence and better estimates for critical exponents in the Ising universality class in three dimensions, compared to other functional RG schemes.

新的Functional Dimensional Regularization (FDR)方案结合了维度正则化的灵活性和泛函RG的一般性，在三维Ising普适类的临界指数计算中，与其他泛函RG方案相比，提供了更快的收敛性和更好的估计。

Abstract: We show that it is possible to use dimensional regularization (DR) beyond the usual $\varepsilon$-expansion in the context of renormalization group (RG) calculations in Critical Phenomena. Based on this fact, we propose a new functional RG scheme - Functional Dimensional Regularization (FDR) - and apply it to a scalar theory in three dimensions. We compute the critical exponents of the Ising universality class directly in $d=3$ under various typical approximations. The method that emerges combines the agility typical of DR with the generality proper of functional RG. Moreover, at a given order of approximation, FDR seems to provide faster convergence and better estimates than other functional RGs.

### [42] [Simple Analytical Solutions of the Wheeler-DeWitt Equation in the Classical Hamilton-Jacobi Limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25240)
*Naoto Maki,Chia-Min Lin,Kazunori Kohri*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper investigates the Wheeler-DeWitt equation for a flat, homogeneous, and isotropic universe with a canonical scalar field. Under the constraint $|Ψ|=1$, the potential form is determined by the operator ordering parameter, leading to simple forms like exponential, quadratic, and cosine-type potentials. Analytical solutions for the scale factor and scalar field are derived for the cosine-type potential with a negative cosmological constant, and their cosmological implications are discussed.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to explore the connection between the quantum description of the universe, given by the Wheeler-DeWitt equation, and its classical counterpart, the Hamilton-Jacobi equation, under specific conditions. By constraining the wave function amplitude to be unity, the authors aim to find the exact form of the scalar field potential that allows for this transition, which can provide insights into the nature of the early universe and its evolution.

本文的动机是探索在特定条件下，由Wheeler-DeWitt方程给出的宇宙量子描述与其经典对应物Hamilton-Jacobi方程之间的联系。通过将波函数振幅约束为单位值，作者旨在找到允许这种过渡的标量场势的确切形式，这可以为我们提供关于早期宇宙及其演化的洞见。

Method: The method involves solving the Wheeler-DeWitt equation for a flat, homogeneous, and isotropic universe with a canonical scalar field, under the constraint $|Ψ|=1$. This constraint transforms the Wheeler-DeWitt equation into the classical Hamilton-Jacobi equation, allowing the determination of the scalar field potential. The authors then classify the resulting potentials based on the value of the operator ordering parameter and derive analytical solutions for the scale factor and scalar field for the case of a cosine-type potential with a negative cosmological constant.

该方法涉及在一个平坦、均匀且各向同性的宇宙中，对于具有规范标量场的情况，在约束$|Ψ|=1$下求解Wheeler-DeWitt方程。此约束将Wheeler-DeWitt方程转换为经典的Hamilton-Jacobi方程，从而能够确定标量场势。然后，作者根据算子排序参数的值对得到的势进行分类，并推导出负宇宙常数余弦型势情况下的尺度因子和标量场的解析解。

Result: The results show that the form of the scalar field potential is completely determined by the operator ordering parameter under the condition $|Ψ|=1$. The classified potentials include exponential, quadratic (with a negative cosmological constant), and cosine-type (also with a negative cosmological constant) forms. For the cosine-type potential, the authors derive explicit analytical solutions for both the scale factor and the scalar field, which have been previously considered in the context of inflation or dark energy.

结果显示，在条件$|Ψ|=1$下，标量场势的形式完全由算子排序参数决定。分类得到的势包括指数型、二次型（带有一个负宇宙常数）和余弦型（也带有负宇宙常数）。对于余弦型势，作者推导出了尺度因子和标量场的具体解析解，这些解之前已在暴涨或暗能量的背景下被考虑过。

Conclusion: The conclusion drawn from this work is that the Wheeler-DeWitt equation, when constrained to $|Ψ|=1$, can lead to a variety of simple and well-known forms of the scalar field potential, depending on the operator ordering parameter. These forms, such as exponential, quadratic, and cosine-type potentials, have direct relevance to models of inflation and dark energy. The derived solutions for the cosine-type potential with a negative cosmological constant provide a deeper understanding of the possible dynamics of the early universe and its later stages.

从这项工作中得出的结论是，当Wheeler-DeWitt方程被约束到$|Ψ|=1$时，可以根据算子排序参数导致多种简单且熟知的标量场势形式。这些形式，如指数型、二次型和余弦型势，与暴涨模型和暗能量模型直接相关。对于带有负宇宙常数的余弦型势所推导出的解，为我们提供了对早期宇宙及其后期阶段可能动力学的更深入理解。

Abstract: We investigate the Wheeler-DeWitt equation for a flat, homogeneous, and isotropic Universe containing a canonical scalar field with a potential. We show that under the constraint $|Ψ|=1$, where the Wheeler-DeWitt equation exactly becomes the classical Hamilton-Jacobi equation, the form of the potential is completely determined depending on the value of the operator ordering parameter. Furthermore, we demonstrate that the classified potentials admit simple forms, such as the exponential, quadratic with a negative cosmological constant, and cosine-type potential with a negative cosmological constant. Several of these have already been explored in the context of inflation or dark energy. Finally, focusing on the system with the cosine-type potential and a negative cosmological constant in the classified potentials, we derive the analytical solutions for the scale factor and the scalar field and discuss the cosmological implications.

### [43] [Integrand Analysis, Leading Singularities and Canonical Bases beyond Polylogarithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25270)
*Felix Forner,Cesare Carlo Mella,Christoph Nega,Lorenzo Tancredi,Fabian J. Wagner*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper explores the connection between leading singularities and canonical bases of Feynman integrals beyond polylogarithms, showing that unit leading singularities require new transcendental functions. These integrals satisfy $\varepsilon$-factorized differential equations, with new transcendental functions corresponding to new differential forms in their Gauss-Manin connection. This is mathematically equivalent to splitting the period matrix into semi-simple and unipotent parts, plus a clean-up step, demonstrated through examples of increasing complexity.

  <summary>Details</summary>

The authors aim to generalize the notion of leading singularities from the Riemann sphere to more complex geometries and show how this leads to the introduction of new transcendental functions related to the periods of these geometries. [English Text]
The motivation of this paper is to understand the structure of Feynman integrals beyond polylogarithms by connecting them to the concept of leading singularities. The authors aim to generalize the notion of leading singularities from the Riemann sphere to more complex geometries and show how this leads to the introduction of new transcendental functions related to the periods of these geometries. [Chinese Text]

Method: The method involves generalizing the concept of leading singularities to more complex geometries within dimensional regularization. The authors then select Feynman integrals with unit leading singularities, which necessitates the introduction of new transcendental functions. They demonstrate that these integrals satisfy $\varepsilon$-factorized differential equations, and the new transcendental functions correspond to new differential forms in the Gauss-Manin connection. The construction is shown to be mathematically equivalent to the splitting of the period matrix into semi-simple and unipotent parts, followed by a clean-up step. [English Text]
The method involves generalizing the concept of leading singularities to more complex geometries within dimensional regularization. The authors then select Feynman integrals with unit leading singularities, which necessitates the introduction of new transcendental functions. They demonstrate that these integrals satisfy $\varepsilon$-factorized differential equations, and the new transcendental functions correspond to new differential forms in the Gauss-Manin connection. The construction is shown to be mathematically equivalent to the splitting of the period matrix into semi-simple and unipotent parts, followed by a clean-up step. [Chinese Text]

The equivalence to the splitting of the period matrix into semi-simple and unipotent parts, along with a clean-up step, offers a new perspective on the mathematical structure of these integrals. [English Text]
The paper concludes that the generalized notion of leading singularities and the associated new transcendental functions provide a deeper understanding of the structure of Feynman integrals beyond polylogarithms. The equivalence to the splitting of the period matrix into semi-simple and unipotent parts, along with a clean-up step, offers a new perspective on the mathematical structure of these integrals. [Chinese Text]

Abstract: In this paper, we elaborate on the connection between leading singularities and canonical bases of Feynman integrals beyond polylogarithms. We start by discussing a notion of leading singularities in dimensional regularization, which can be generalized from the Riemann sphere to more complex geometries, and use it to demonstrate how selecting Feynman integrals with unit leading singularities necessitates introducing new transcendental functions related to the periods of the underlying geometries. Integrals with unit leading singularities in this generalized sense, satisfy $ε$-factorized differential equations, and the new transcendental functions are in direct correspondence to the new differential forms appearing in their Gauss-Manin connection. We argue that this construction is mathematically equivalent to the splitting of the period matrix into semi-simple and unipotent parts plus a clean-up step, and demonstrate its use with examples of increasing complexity that require the interplay of multiple geometries.

</details>


### [44] [Liouville Blocks from Spectral Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25463)
*Lotte Hollands,Subrabalan Murugesan*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper explores the role of spectral networks, particularly Fenchel-Nielsen-type, in quantum Liouville theory. It introduces q-parallel transport for these networks and compares it with quantum parallel transport using the Moore-Seiberg formalism. The study also develops an extended free-field formalism for smooth spectral coverings, suggesting it generates the full spectrum of Liouville conformal blocks and defines Goncharov-Shen conformal blocks.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand and develop a more complete framework for generating Liouville conformal blocks, which are essential in the study of two-dimensional conformal field theories. The authors aim to extend the existing free-field formalism to handle wall-crossing phenomena and to provide a first-principle definition for Goncharov-Shen conformal blocks.

Method: The method involves constructing q-parallel transport for Fenchel-Nielsen networks via q-nonabelianisation and comparing it with quantum parallel transport computed using the Moore-Seiberg formalism. Additionally, the authors extend the free-field formalism to smooth spectral coverings, utilizing the Maulik-Okounkov R-matrix to address wall-crossing issues.

Result: The results show that the standard free-field formalism with Fenchel-Nielsen-type integration contours is not sufficient for handling wall-crossing. The extended free-field formalism, incorporating the Maulik-Okounkov R-matrix, is conjectured to generate the full spectrum of Liouville conformal blocks and to define Goncharov-Shen conformal blocks.

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the proposed extension of the free-field formalism, with the inclusion of the Maulik-Okounkov R-matrix, provides a more comprehensive approach to generating Liouville conformal blocks, addressing the limitations of the standard formalism and potentially offering a first-principle definition for Goncharov-Shen conformal blocks.

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate the role of spectral networks in quantum Liouville theory, with particular emphasis on spectral networks of Fenchel-Nielsen-type. In the first part, we construct q-parallel transport for Fenchel-Nielsen networks through q-nonabelianisation, and compare with quantum parallel transport computed using the Moore-Seiberg formalism. This motivates a proposal for a quantum version of the NRS proposal. In the second part, we reproduce Liouville conformal blocks through the standard free-field formalism with Fenchel-Nielsen-type integration contours. However, we observe that this approach is not complete with respect to wall-crossing. We therefore develop an extension of the free-field formalism to smooth spectral coverings, with the Maulik-Okounkov R-matrix playing a central role. We conjecture that this new formalism generates the full spectrum of Liouville conformal blocks, and provides a first-principle definition for Goncharov-Shen conformal blocks.

### [45] [Phase Transitions and Chaos Bound in Horava Lifshitz Black Holes using Lyapunov Exponents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25495)
*Mozib Bin Awal,Prabwal Phukon*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper explores the thermodynamic phase structure of 4D Horava-Lifshitz black holes using Lyapunov exponent analysis, revealing multivalued behavior and a critical exponent consistent with mean-field universality. The chaos bound is violated below a certain horizon radius, even in the absence of a phase transition.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to investigate the thermodynamic phase structure of four-dimensional Horava-Lifshitz black holes through the lens of Lyapunov exponent analysis. The authors aim to understand the behavior of these black holes during phase transitions and to establish the robustness and universality of Lyapunov exponents as probes of black hole thermodynamics in alternative theories of gravity.

本文的动机是通过Lyapunov指数分析来研究四维Horava-Lifshitz黑洞的热力学相结构。作者旨在理解这些黑洞在相变过程中的行为，并确立Lyapunov指数作为替代引力理论中黑洞热力学探测工具的稳健性和普适性。

Method: The method used in this paper involves the Lyapunov exponent analysis for both massless and massive test particles in the context of four-dimensional Horava-Lifshitz black holes. The authors analyze the dependence of the Lyapunov exponent on temperature, identifying distinct branches corresponding to small, intermediate, and large black hole phases. They also examine the discontinuity in the Lyapunov exponent as an effective order parameter and determine the critical exponent $\delta=1/2$ at the critical point. Additionally, they investigate the violation of the chaos bound below a threshold horizon radius.

本文采用的方法是针对四维Horava-Lifshitz黑洞，对无质量和有质量的测试粒子进行Lyapunov指数分析。作者分析了Lyapunov指数随温度的变化，识别出分别对应小、中、大黑洞相的不同分支。他们还检查了Lyapunov指数的不连续性作为一个有效的序参数，并确定了临界点处的临界指数$\delta=1/2$。此外，他们还研究了低于某一视界半径阈值时混沌边界被违反的情况。

Result: The results show that the Lyapunov exponent exhibits a multivalued dependence on temperature in regimes with a first-order phase transition, with distinct branches corresponding to small, intermediate, and large black hole phases. The discontinuity in the Lyapunov exponent acts as an effective order parameter with a critical exponent $\delta=1/2$, consistent with mean-field universality. Furthermore, the chaos bound is generically violated below a threshold horizon radius, even in the absence of a phase transition.

结果表明，在一级相变区域内，Lyapunov指数表现出多值依赖于温度的行为，分别对应小、中、大黑洞相的不同分支。Lyapunov指数的不连续性作为一个有效的序参数，其临界指数为$\delta=1/2$，与平均场普适性一致。此外，即使在没有相变的情况下，当视界半径低于某一阈值时，混沌边界通常会被违反。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that the Lyapunov exponent is a robust and universal probe of the thermodynamic phase structure of four-dimensional Horava-Lifshitz black holes. The multivalued behavior and critical exponent are consistent with mean-field universality, and the violation of the chaos bound below a threshold horizon radius is a significant finding, indicating the importance of Lyapunov exponents in understanding black hole thermodynamics in alternative theories of gravity.

本文得出结论，Lyapunov指数是四维Horava-Lifshitz黑洞热力学相结构的稳健且普适的探测工具。多值行为和临界指数与平均场普适性一致，而在低于某一视界半径阈值时混沌边界的违反是一个重要发现，表明Lyapunov指数在理解替代引力理论中的黑洞热力学方面的重要性。

Abstract: We probe the thermodynamic phase structure of four dimensional Horava Lifshitz black holes by Lyapunov exponent analysis. For both massless and massive test particles, the Lyapunov exponent exhibits a multivalued dependence on temperature in regimes with a first-order phase transition, with distinct branches corresponding to small, intermediate, and large black hole phases, and this behaviour disappears at the critical point. The discontinuity in the Lyapunov exponent acts as an effective order parameter with critical exponent $δ=1/2$, consistent with mean-field universality. We also find that the chaos bound is generically violated below a threshold horizon radius, with the violation occurring within the thermodynamically stable phase and persisting even in the absence of a phase transition. These results establish the robustness and universality of Lyapunov exponents as probes of black hole thermodynamics in alternative theories of gravity.

### [46] [Criticality of ISCOs and AdS/CFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25518)
*Chandrasekhar Bhamidipati,Parashar Chatterjee,Sudipta Mukherji,Yogesh Kumar Srivastava*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper analyzes the trajectories of massive particles in spherically symmetric black holes across various dimensions, focusing on the topological classification of fixed points. It identifies two outcomes for systems with a center: the center always survives or disappears below a critical angular momentum. A critical point is found where the center and saddle coalesce, showing van der Waals-like scaling. The anomalous dimensions of double-twist operators are calculated using AdS/CFT and four-point correlators, revealing non-analytic behavior at the ISCO.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to understand the universal features of particle trajectories in spherically symmetric black holes in arbitrary dimensions, particularly focusing on the role of fixed points and their topological classification. The study aims to uncover the conditions under which the center of such systems persists or disappears, and to explore the critical behavior at the point where the center and saddle coalesce, including the emergence of non-analytic behavior in the anomalous dimensions of double-twist operators.

本文的动机是理解任意维度球对称黑洞中粒子轨迹的普遍特征，特别是关注固定点及其拓扑分类的作用。研究旨在揭示系统中心在何种条件下持续存在或消失，并探索中心和鞍点合并时的临界行为，包括双扭算子反常维度中非解析行为的出现。

Method: The method involves the analysis of particle trajectories in spherically symmetric black holes using the topological classification of fixed points. The authors examine the survival or disappearance of the center based on the angular momentum and find that there is always a saddle point if the center disappears. They use topological arguments to determine the critical values of energy, angular momentum, and angular velocity where the center and saddle coalesce, leading to innermost stable circular orbits (ISCOs). The anomalous dimensions of double-twist operators are then computed using both the AdS/CFT correspondence and heavy-heavy-light-light four-point correlators, and subleading corrections in $\frac{1}{\Delta_H}$ are also considered.

该方法涉及使用固定点的拓扑分类分析球对称黑洞中的粒子轨迹。作者根据角动量检查中心的持续存在或消失，并发现在中心消失的情况下总是存在一个鞍点。他们利用拓扑论据确定能量、角动量和角速度的临界值，在这些临界值处中心和鞍点合并，导致最内稳定圆形轨道（ISCO）。然后，使用AdS/CFT对应关系和重-重-轻-轻四点关联函数计算双扭算子的反常维度，并考虑了$\frac{1}{\Delta_H}$的次级修正。

Result: The results show that for systems admitting a center, it either always survives or disappears below a critical angular momentum. In the latter case, a saddle point must exist. The critical point where the center and saddle coalesce is identified, and it is shown that conserved quantities exhibit van der Waals-like mean-field scaling, typical of a second-order phase transition. The anomalous dimensions of double-twist operators are found to be negative for the center and positive for the saddle, with non-analytic behavior emerging at the ISCO. Subleading corrections in $\frac{1}{\Delta_H}$ to the anomalous dimension for the center are also provided.

结果表明，对于允许中心存在的系统，中心要么始终存在，要么在低于某个临界角动量时消失。在后一种情况下，必须存在一个鞍点。识别出中心和鞍点合并的临界点，并显示守恒量表现出类似于范德瓦尔斯的平均场标度，这是二级相变的典型特征。双扭算子的反常维度在中心为负，在鞍点为正，并且在ISCO处出现非解析行为。还提供了中心反常维度的$\frac{1}{\Delta_H}$次级修正。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that the topological classification of fixed points in spherically symmetric black holes leads to universal features in the dynamics of massive particles. The existence of a critical point where the center and saddle coalesce, and the associated van der Waals-like scaling, indicate a second-order phase transition. The anomalous dimensions of double-twist operators, with their non-analytic behavior at the ISCO, provide further insights into the critical behavior of these systems. The results have implications for understanding the holographic dual CFT and the behavior of heavy-heavy-light-light four-point correlators.

论文得出结论，球对称黑洞中固定点的拓扑分类导致了大质量粒子动力学中的普遍特征。中心和鞍点合并的临界点的存在以及相关的范德瓦尔斯类标度表明了二级相变。双扭算子的反常维度及其在ISCO处的非解析行为进一步揭示了这些系统的临界行为。这些结果对理解全息对偶CFT和重-重-轻-轻四点关联函数的行为具有重要意义。

Abstract: We study the trajectories of massive particles in spherically symmetric black holes in arbitrary dimensions, and find certain universal features based on the topological classification of the fixed points. If the system admits a center, we find two possible outcomes: regardless of the value of the angular momentum, the center always survives, which is realized in global AdS spacetimes or, the center disappears below a critical value of angular momentum, which happens for various spherically symmetric black holes. For the latter case, we find that irrespective of the details of the black hole, there must always be a saddle point. Topological arguments show that there exists a certain critical value of energy, angular momentum and the angular velocity, where the center and the saddle coalesce. This happens at a special point in the parameter space where the trajectories are the limiting innermost stable circular orbits (ISCOs). At the critical point, conserved quantities show universal, van der Waals-like mean-field scaling typical of a second-order phase transition. The anomalous dimensions $γ$ of the double-twist operators in the CFT are found, both using AdS/CFT and through the the heavy-heavy-light-light four point correlators, giving negative and positive values for the center and saddle, respectively, including the emergence of certain non-analytic behaviour at the ISCO. For the center, we also find subleading corrections in $\frac{1}{Δ_H}$ to $γ$ in the dual CFT, and dsicuss the implications of our results.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>
