The authors aim to provide a calculable semiclassical realization of this process by considering a simple five-dimensional $S^1$ compactification in a time-dependent open FRW background. This work aims to illustrate a broader mechanism for dynamical compactification that could be relevant in pre-inflationary cosmology.

结果表明，负曲率可以维持radion的类跟踪器演化，导致其在紧致化的真空态中稳定和被捕获。这发生在随后的四维暴胀阶段之前，该阶段会稀释剩余的曲率。研究表明了一种机制，通过这种机制，动态紧致化可以在暴胀前的高维宇宙学中自然出现。

This provides a concrete example of how such a transition can occur in a pre-inflationary cosmological setting, potentially offering new insights into the early universe's dynamics and the nature of extra dimensions.

结论是，所提出的曲率辅助模捕获机制可以成功地导致额外维度的动态紧致化，使宇宙从高维状态过渡到有效四维状态。这为在暴胀前宇宙学环境中此类转变如何发生提供了一个具体示例，可能为早期宇宙动力学和额外维度的本质提供了新的见解。

Abstract: We investigate a pre-inflationary dynamical compactification scenario in which a higher-dimensional expanding universe evolves into an effectively four-dimensional one through curvature-assisted modulus trapping. To obtain a calculable semiclassical realization, we consider a simple five-dimensional $S^1$ compactification in a time-dependent open FRW background. We also show that a coisotropic reduction of this model reproduces the recent model of ref [1], which is formulated in terms of constrained fields.

</details>


### [50] [Candidate Gaugings of Categorical Continuous Symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25820)
*Qiang Jia,Cheng Ma,Jiahua Tian*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper explores the relationship between different gaugings of a global symmetry and the phases of a quantum field theory. Using a semiclassical kernel-theoretic model, it derives candidate modular S- and T-kernels from Hopf-link and framing correlators in $S^3$, leading to candidate modular invariants and gaugings. The results are consistent with known cases and hint at an extension to compact Lie groups.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand how different gaugings of a global symmetry in a quantum field theory (QFT) can lead to various phases of the QFT. The authors aim to identify candidate gaugeable symmetries by analyzing the Lagrangian algebra data in the Drinfeld center of a symmetry category associated with a QFT that has a continuous global $G$-symmetry and a possible 't Hooft anomaly.

研究动机在于理解量子场论（QFT）中全局对称性的不同规范如何导致QFT的不同相。作者旨在通过分析与具有连续全局$G$-对称性和可能的't Hooft异常的QFT相关的对称性范畴的Drinfeld中心中的Lagrangian代数数据，来识别候选的可规范对称性。

Method: The method involves using a combination of $BF$ theory and level-$k$ Chern-Simons theory with gauge group $G$ as a semiclassical kernel-theoretic model for the SymTFT. Under two explicit assumptions, the authors derive candidate modular $S$- and $T$-kernels from Hopf-link and framing correlators in $S^3$. These kernels are then used to obtain candidate modular invariants and candidate gaugings.

该方法涉及使用$BF$理论和层次为$k$的Chern-Simons理论（规范群为$G$）的组合，作为SymTFT的半经典核理论模型。在两个明确假设下，作者从$S^3$中的Hopf-link和framing相关器导出候选模$S$-和$T$-核。然后利用这些核获得候选模不变量和候选规范。

Result: The derived formulas for candidate modular $S$- and $T$-kernels recover established cases and suggest a potential extension of this kernel-theoretic approach to compact Lie groups. This provides a systematic way to explore candidate gaugings and their implications on the phases of the QFT.

推导出的候选模$S$-和$T$-核的公式恢复了已知情况，并暗示这种核理论方法可能扩展到紧致李群。这提供了一种系统的方法来探索候选规范及其对QFT相的影响。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates a novel approach to identifying candidate gaugeable symmetries and their corresponding phases in QFTs through the analysis of Lagrangian algebra data in the Drinfeld center. The use of a semiclassical kernel-theoretic model, specifically the $BF{+}k$CS theory, provides a powerful tool for deriving modular kernels and invariants, which can be extended to compact Lie groups.

研究表明，通过分析Drinfeld中心中的Lagrangian代数数据，可以识别QFT中候选的可规范对称性及其相应的相。使用半经典核理论模型，特别是$BF{+}k$CS理论，提供了一个强大的工具来推导模核和不变量，这种方法可以扩展到紧致李群。

Abstract: Different gaugings of the global symmetry of a quantum field theory are closely related to its various phases. In this work, we study candidate gaugeable symmetries by analyzing candidate Lagrangian algebra data in the Drinfeld center of a symmetry category $\mathscr{C}^k(G)$ associated to a QFT with continuous global $G$-symmetry and possible 't Hooft anomaly labeled by an integer $k$. We use the combination of the $BF$ theory and the level-$k$ Chern-Simons theory with gauge group $G$ as a semiclassical kernel-theoretic model for the corresponding SymTFT. Under two explicit assumptions, namely that this $BF{+}k$CS theory provides the relevant SymTFT model and that the common $+1$ eigenspaces of the resulting modular kernels detect candidate Lagrangian algebra data in the continuous setting, we derive candidate modular $S$- and $T$-kernels from Hopf-link and framing correlators in $S^3$ semi-classically. We then use these kernels to obtain candidate modular invariants and candidate gaugings. The resulting formulas recover the established cases and suggest a possible extension of this kernel-theoretic picture to compact Lie groups.

</details>


### [51] [Categorical Symmetries via Operator Algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25821)
*Qiang Jia,Ran Luo,Jiahua Tian,Yi-Nan Wang,Yi Zhang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper proposes a new symmetry category for 2D quantum field theories with 0-form G-symmetry and 't Hooft anomaly, which is the category of twisted measurable fields of Hilbert spaces. The Drinfeld center of this category is characterized by the transgression of the anomaly, and the framework applies to a wide range of Lie groups. The authors also compute the braiding of anyon lines in 3D SymTFT and provide physical examples.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to develop a mathematical framework that can describe the symmetry and anomaly structure of 2D quantum field theories (QFTs) with 0-form $G$-symmetry and 't Hooft anomaly. This framework aims to provide a more general and unified description of such QFTs, particularly in terms of their symmetry categories and how these categories relate to the bulk 3D Symmetric Topological Field Theory (SymTFT). 

动机是开发一个数学框架，能够描述具有0形式$G$对称性和't Hooft反常的二维量子场论（QFT）的对称性和反常结构。该框架旨在为这些QFT提供更通用和统一的描述，特别是关于它们的对称性类别以及这些类别如何与三维对称拓扑场论（SymTFT）相关联。

Method: The authors propose that the symmetry category associated with a 2D QFT having 0-form $G$-symmetry and 't Hooft anomaly $k \in H^4(BG,\mathbb{Z})$ is the category of twisted measurable fields of Hilbert spaces over $G$, denoted as $\mathrm{Hilb}^k(G)$. This category is equivalent to the category of unitary representations of $C_0(G)$ with convolution product twisted by a multiplicative bundle gerbe labeled by $k$, denoted as $\textbf{Rep}^k(C_0(G))$. They further show that the Drinfeld center of the symmetry category $\mathcal{Z}(\mathrm{Hilb}^{k}(G))$ is equivalent to the category of unitary representations of the groupoid $C^*$-algebra of the Fell line bundle $Σ_k$ over the conjugation action groupoid $G//_{\rm Ad} G$, denoted by $\textbf{Rep}(C^*(G//_{\rm Ad}G,Σ_k))$, where the twist is characterized by the transgression $τ(k) \in H^2(G//_{\rm Ad}G,U(1))$. The method applies generally to Lie groups that are direct products of compact connected Lie groups and a number of $\mathbb{R}$ or $GL(1,\mathbb{C})$ factors.

作者提出，与具有0形式$G$对称性和't Hooft反常$k \in H^4(BG,\mathbb{Z})$的二维QFT相关的对称性类别是$G$上的扭曲可测希尔伯特空间场的类别，记作$\mathrm{Hilb}^k(G)$。这个类别等价于$C_0(G)$的酉表示类别，其卷积乘积被标记为$k$的乘法丛胚扭曲，记作$\textbf{Rep}^k(C_0(G))$。他们进一步表明，对称性类别的Drinfeld中心$\mathcal{Z}(\mathrm{Hilb}^{k}(G))$等价于共轭作用群组$G//_{\rm Ad} G$上Fell线丛$Σ_k$的群组$C^*$-代数的酉表示类别，记作$\textbf{Rep}(C^*(G//_{\rm Ad}G,Σ_k))$，其中扭曲由转换$τ(k) \in H^2(G//_{\rm Ad}G,U(1))$表征。此方法普遍适用于直接乘积为紧连通李群和多个$\mathbb{R}$或$GL(1,\mathbb{C})$因子的李群。

Result: The main result is the identification of the symmetry category for 2D QFTs with 0-form $G$-symmetry and 't Hooft anomaly, which is the category of twisted measurable fields of Hilbert spaces $\mathrm{Hilb}^k(G)$. Additionally, it is shown that the Drinfeld center of this category, $\mathcal{Z}(\mathrm{Hilb}^{k}(G))$, is equivalent to the category of unitary representations of the groupoid $C^*$-algebra of the Fell line bundle $Σ_k$ over the conjugation action groupoid $G//_{\rm Ad} G$. The framework is applied to compute the braiding of anyon lines in 3D SymTFT and provides physical examples for abelian and non-abelian $G$.

主要结果是确定了具有0形式$G$对称性和't Hooft反常的二维QFT的对称性类别，即扭曲可测希尔伯特空间场的类别$\mathrm{Hilb}^k(G)$。此外，还表明该类别的Drinfeld中心$\mathcal{Z}(\mathrm{Hilb}^{k}(G))$等价于共轭作用群组$G//_{\rm Ad} G$上Fell线丛$Σ_k$的群组$C^*$-代数的酉表示类别。该框架用于计算3D SymTFT中anyon线的编织，并提供了阿贝尔和非阿贝尔$G$的物理实例。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that the proposed symmetry category $\mathrm{Hilb}^k(G)$, along with its Drinfeld center, provides a robust framework for understanding the symmetry and anomaly structure of 2D QFTs with 0-form $G$-symmetry and 't Hooft anomaly. The formalism is applicable to a broad class of Lie groups and allows for the computation of topological invariants, such as the braiding of anyon lines in 3D SymTFT. The results have implications for the study of continuous global symmetries and their gauging in QFTs.

论文得出结论，所提出的对称性类别$\mathrm{Hilb}^k(G)$及其Drinfeld中心为理解具有0形式$G$对称性和't Hooft反常的二维QFT的对称性和反常结构提供了一个稳健的框架。该形式主义适用于广泛的李群类别，并允许计算拓扑不变量，如3D SymTFT中anyon线的编织。这些结果对于研究连续全局对称性及其在QFT中的规范有重要意义。

Abstract: We propose that the symmetry category associated to a 2D quantum field theory with 0-form $G$-symmetry with 't Hooft anomaly $k\in H^4(BG,\mathbb{Z})$ for a large class of Lie groups $G$ is the category of twisted measurable fields of Hilbert spaces over $G$ denoted by $\mathrm{Hilb}^k(G)$, which is equivalent to the category of unitary representations of $C_0(G)$ with convolution product twisted by a multiplicative bundle gerbe labeled by $k$ denoted by $\textbf{Rep}^k(C_0(G))$. We find that the Drinfeld center of the symmetry category $\mathcal{Z}(\mathrm{Hilb}^{k}(G))$ equivalent to the category of unitary representations of the groupoid $C^*$-algebra of the Fell line bundle $Σ_k$ over the conjugation action groupoid $G//_{\rm Ad} G$, denoted by $\textbf{Rep}(C^*(G//_{\rm Ad}G,Σ_k))$, where the twist is characterized by the transgression $τ(k)\in H^2(G//_{\rm Ad}G,U(1))$. To the full generality, our framework applies to a Lie group $G$ that is a direct product of a compact connected Lie group and a number of $\mathbb{R}$ or $GL(1,\mathbb{C})$ factors. We compute the braiding of anyon lines in the bulk 3D SymTFT from this formalism. Finally we provide physical examples for abelian and non-abelian $G$, and discuss the physical consequences of flat gauging continuous global symmetries.

</details>


### [52] [(Super-)renormalizable hairy meronic black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25844)
*Luis Avilés,Borja Diez*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper presents an analytical black hole solution in the Einstein-Maxwell-Yang-Mills theory with a conformally coupled scalar field, generalizing the charged MTZ black hole and extending to non-Abelian gauge fields. It also introduces new meronic spacetimes and considers a non-Noetherian extension of the conformal scalar fields, allowing for static black hole solutions with Yang-Mills charges.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to generalize the known charged MTZ black hole solution by incorporating self-gravitating non-Abelian gauge fields and to explore the implications of these fields on the black hole's properties. Additionally, the authors aim to construct new meronic spacetimes and investigate the effects of a non-Noetherian extension of the conformal scalar fields.

动机是通过引入自引力非阿贝尔规范场来推广已知的带电MTZ黑洞解，并探索这些场对黑洞性质的影响。此外，作者还旨在构建新的meronic时空，并研究共形标量场的非诺特定扩展的影响。

Method: The method involves constructing an analytical black hole solution in the Einstein-Maxwell-Yang-Mills (EMYM) theory with a conformally coupled scalar field. The internal gauge group is determined by the horizon curvature, being $SU(N)$ for positive curvature and $SU(N-1,1)$ for negative curvature. This solution is then used as a conformal seed to generate new meronic spacetimes, including all (super-)renormalizable contributions from the scalar field. Finally, the non-Noetherian extension of the conformal scalar fields is considered, which still yields a second-order conformally invariant scalar equation, even though the action is not.

方法涉及在带有共形耦合标量场的爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-杨-米尔斯（EMYM）理论中构造一个解析黑洞解。内部规范群由视界曲率决定，对于正曲率为$SU(N)$，对于负曲率为$SU(N-1,1)$。然后，该解被用作共形种子，以生成新的meronic时空，包括来自标量场的所有(超)可重整化贡献。最后，考虑了共形标量场的非诺特定扩展，尽管作用量不是这样的，但仍产生二阶共形不变标量方程。

Result: The result is a generalized charged MTZ black hole solution that includes self-gravitating non-Abelian gauge fields. The internal gauge group depends on the sign of the horizon curvature, and the solution can be used to generate new meronic spacetimes. Additionally, the non-Noetherian extension of the conformal scalar fields allows for the construction of static black hole solutions with Yang-Mills charges.

结果是一个包含自引力非阿贝尔规范场的广义带电MTZ黑洞解。内部规范群取决于视界曲率的符号，并且该解可用于生成新的meronic时空。此外，共形标量场的非诺特定扩展允许构造具有杨-米尔斯电荷的静态黑洞解。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the inclusion of self-gravitating non-Abelian gauge fields in the EMYM theory leads to a richer structure of black hole solutions, with the internal gauge group depending on the horizon curvature. The new meronic spacetimes and the non-Noetherian extension of the conformal scalar fields provide additional insights into the nature of these solutions, particularly in the presence of Yang-Mills charges.

结论是在EMYM理论中包含自引力非阿贝尔规范场导致了更丰富的黑洞解结构，其中内部规范群取决于视界曲率。新的meronic时空和共形标量场的非诺特定扩展为这些解的性质提供了额外的见解，特别是在存在杨-米尔斯电荷的情况下。

Abstract: We construct an analytical black hole solution in the Einstein-Maxwell-Yang-Mills theory with a conformally coupled scalar field in four dimensions, which generalizes the charged Martínez-Troncoso-Zanelli (MTZ) black hole in the presence of self-gravitating non-Abelian gauge fields. The internal gauge group is determined by the horizon curvature, becoming $SU(N)$ in the case of positive curvature and $SU(N-1,1)$ when the curvature is negative. Moreover, this solution is employed as a conformal seed to obtain new meronic spacetimes dressed with all (super-)renormalizable contributions of the scalar field, which provides the generalization of the Anabalón-Cisterna (AC) solution when self-gravitating non-Abelian gauge fields are included. Finally, we consider the non-Noetherian extension of the conformal scalar fields, which still yields a second-order conformally invariant scalar equation, even though the action is not. In that case, we show that static black hole solutions can also be charged with Yang-Mills fields.

</details>


### [53] [Nonlocal-in-time tail effects in gravitational scattering to fifth Post-Minkowskian and tenth self-force orders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25916)
*Christoph Dlapa,Gregor Kälin,Zhengwen Liu,Rafael A. Porto*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper uses the worldline effective field theory to derive nonlocal-in-time conservative contributions in gravitational scattering up to 5PM and 10SF orders, featuring multiple polylogarithms. The computation employs advanced integration techniques, including a new Sparse Integral Reducer (SpideR) algorithm, and agrees with existing literature up to 6PN order. This work is crucial for isolating the local-in-time component of the conservative two-body dynamics at 5PM order.

该论文使用世界线有效场论形式，推导了引力散射中高达5PM和10SF阶的非局域时间保守贡献，这些结果包含多重对数函数。计算采用了先进的积分技术，包括一种新的稀疏积分约化（SpideR）算法，并且与现有文献在6PN阶之前的结果完全一致。这项工作对于在5PM阶分离二体系统保守动力学中的局域时间成分至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to derive the nonlocal-in-time conservative contributions in gravitational scattering, which are essential for understanding the dynamics of binary inspirals. These contributions, arising from tail effects, are important for accurate modeling of gravitational waveforms and the corresponding observables in gravitational wave astronomy.

动机是推导引力散射中的非局域时间保守贡献，这对于理解双星旋近的动力学至关重要。这些由尾效应引起的贡献对于精确建模引力波形及其在引力波天文学中的相应可观测量非常重要。

Method: The method involves using the worldline effective field theory formalism to compute the nonlocal-in-time conservative contributions. Advanced integration techniques, such as the novel Sparse Integral Reducer (SpideR) algorithm, are employed to handle the challenging integrals that feature multiple polylogarithms of up to weight three.

方法涉及使用世界线有效场论形式来计算非局域时间保守贡献。采用先进的积分技术，如新型的稀疏积分约化（SpideR）算法，来处理包含多达三重对数函数的复杂积分。

Result: The results include the derivation of nonlocal-in-time conservative contributions up to 5PM and 10SF orders, featuring multiple polylogarithms of up to weight three. The computations show perfect agreement with all existing literature through sixth post-Newtonian (6PN) order.

结果包括推导出高达5PM和10SF阶的非局域时间保守贡献，这些结果包含多达三重对数函数。计算结果显示与现有文献在6PN阶之前的结果完全一致。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the derived nonlocal-in-time conservative contributions provide a key ingredient for isolating the local-in-time component of the conservative two-body dynamics at 5PM order. This work advances the understanding of gravitational scattering and is crucial for the accurate modeling of binary inspirals in gravitational wave astronomy.

结论是，推导出的非局域时间保守贡献为在5PM阶分离二体系统保守动力学中的局域时间成分提供了关键要素。这项工作推进了对引力散射的理解，在引力波天文学中准确建模双星旋近方面至关重要。

Abstract: Using the worldline effective field theory formalism, we derive the nonlocal-in-time conservative contributions arising from tail effects in gravitational scattering to fifth Post-Minkowskian (5PM) and tenth self-force (10SF) orders. The result features multiple polylogarithms of up to weight three. This challenging computation relies on state-of-the-art integration techniques, including a novel integration-by-parts algorithm: the Sparse Integral Reducer (SpideR). We find perfect agreement in the overlap with all existing literature through sixth post-Newtonian order. The results presented here provide a key ingredient for isolating the local-in-time component of the conservative two-body dynamics of binary inspirals at 5PM order.

### [54] [de Sitter in String Theory vs. Gibbons & Hawking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25918)
*Yoav Zigdon*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper confirms that perturbative string theory does not support a de Sitter spacetime metric, assuming the logarithm of the sphere partition function in Euclidean quantum gravity has a nonzero contribution proportional to $\frac{1}{G_N}$. This is linked to the Gibbons-Hawking entropy proposal. The effective action of string theory suggests the tree-level action vanishes for closed Euclidean solutions, implying the Universe may not remain in an asymptotically de Sitter state.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore the compatibility of de Sitter spacetimes with perturbative string theory, particularly under the assumption that the logarithm of the sphere partition function of Euclidean quantum gravity has a nonzero term proportional to $\frac{1}{G_N}$, which is related to the Gibbons-Hawking entropy of the cosmological horizon. 

动机是探讨德西特时空与微扰弦理论的兼容性，特别是假设欧几里得量子引力的球面配分函数的对数有一个非零项与$\frac{1}{G_N}$成正比，这与宇宙学视界的吉本斯-霍金熵有关。

Method: The method involves analyzing the effective action of string theory at various levels, including the tree-level, and considering the implications of the assumption that the logarithm of the sphere partition function receives a nonzero contribution proportional to $\frac{1}{G_N}$. The analysis is based on the known results from independent approaches to the effective action of string theory.

方法包括在不同层次上分析弦理论的有效作用量，包括树图层次，并考虑假设球面配分函数的对数有一个非零项与$\frac{1}{G_N}$成正比所带来的影响。该分析基于从独立的方法得到的弦理论有效作用量的结果。

Result: The result is that perturbative string theory does not admit a solution with a de Sitter spacetime metric, as the tree-level action vanishes for closed Euclidean target-space solutions. This finding is consistent across multiple independent approaches to the effective action of string theory.

结果是微扰弦理论不支持具有德西特时空度规的解，因为对于闭合欧几里得目标空间解，树图层次的作用量为零。这一发现在多种独立的弦理论有效作用量方法中是一致的。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that if the logarithm of the sphere partition function of Euclidean quantum gravity indeed receives a nonzero contribution proportional to $\frac{1}{G_N}$, then perturbative string theory does not support de Sitter spacetimes. This implies that the state of the Universe may eventually depart from an asymptotically de Sitter spacetime.

结论是，如果欧几里得量子引力的球面配分函数的对数确实有一个非零项与$\frac{1}{G_N}$成正比，那么微扰弦理论不支持德西特时空。这意味着宇宙的状态最终可能偏离渐近德西特时空。

Abstract: This paper corroborates a statement that perturbative string theory does not admit a solution whose spacetime metric is de Sitter times a closed manifold, to all orders in the $α'$ and $g_s$ expansions, under the assumption that the logarithm of the sphere partition function of Euclidean quantum gravity receives a nonzero contribution proportional to $\frac{1}{G_N}$ in a saddle-point approximation. This assumption is related to the Gibbons-Hawking proposal that the entropy of the cosmological horizon of the static patch is $\frac{A}{4G_N}$. Evidence for the statement comes from independent approaches to the effective action of string theory, all of which agree that the tree-level action vanishes for closed Euclidean target-space solutions. One possible implication is that the state of the Universe will depart from an asymptotically de Sitter spacetime.

</details>

### [55] [The Szekeres metrics with $M < 0$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24786)
*Andrzej Krasiński*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The abstract discusses the properties of Szekeres metrics with a negative mass function, which leads to negative mass density. These solutions do not have a Big Bang singularity and no origin, and thus are not considered valid cosmological models.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore the conditions under which the Szekeres metrics can have a negative mass function and to understand the implications for the mass density and the validity as cosmological models.

动机是探讨Szekeres度规在何种条件下可以具有负质量函数，并理解其对质量密度和作为宇宙学模型的有效性的影响。

Method: The method involves analyzing the evolution equation of the Szekeres metrics, particularly focusing on the cases where the mass function $M < 0$. The analysis includes examining the conditions for no shell crossings and their relation to the mass density $\rho$ of the dust source in the Einstein equations.

方法包括分析Szekeres度规的演化方程，特别是关注质量函数$M < 0$的情况。分析包括检查没有壳层交叉的条件及其与Einstein方程中尘埃源的质量密度$\rho$的关系。

Result: The results show that when the mass function $M < 0$, the Szekeres metrics do not have a Big Bang singularity and no origin. Additionally, the conditions for no shell crossings ensure that the mass density $\rho$ remains negative at all times, making these metrics unsuitable as cosmological models.

结果表明，当质量函数$M < 0$时，Szekeres度规没有大爆炸奇点和起源。此外，没有壳层交叉的条件确保了质量密度$\rho$始终为负，使得这些度规不适合作为宇宙学模型。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that Szekeres metrics with a negative mass function do not qualify as cosmological models due to the presence of negative mass density and the absence of a Big Bang singularity and an origin. The Friedmann limit immediately implies that $M < 0 \Longrightarrow \rho < 0$, while the general case requires more intricate reasoning.

结论是，由于存在负质量密度且没有大爆炸奇点和起源，具有负质量函数的Szekeres度规不适合作为宇宙学模型。Friedmann极限立即暗示了$M < 0 \Longrightarrow \rho < 0$，而一般情况则需要更复杂的推理。

Abstract: The evolution equation of the Szekeres metrics allows solutions with the mass function $M < 0$. They exist in both classes of the Szekeres metrics, have no Big Bang singularity and no origin. In both classes, the conditions for no shell crossings ensure that the mass density $ρ$ of the dust source in the Einstein equations is negative at all times. Thus, these metrics do not qualify as cosmological models. In the Friedmann limit, the implication $M < 0 \Longrightarrow ρ< 0$ is immediate. In the general Szekeres metrics it follows through a rather intricate reasoning.

</details>


### [56] [Renormalization-group improved Schwarzschild black hole: shadow, ringdown, and strong cosmic censorship](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24798)
*Ahmad Al-Badawi,Faizuddin Ahmed,İzzet Sakallı*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper analyzes a renormalization-group (RG) improved Schwarzschild-like black hole, exploring its horizon structure, photon sphere, and shadow radius. It also investigates quasinormal modes, Strong Cosmic Censorship, and thermodynamic properties, including a Davies-type phase transition and Hawking radiation characteristics.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to study the properties of a Schwarzschild-like black hole that has been improved by renormalization group (RG) techniques, with a focus on how quantum effects at a cutoff scale $\xi$ and an interpolation parameter $\gamma$ modify the classical black hole's features. This includes examining the horizon structure, photon sphere, and shadow radius, as well as quasinormal modes, Strong Cosmic Censorship, and thermodynamic behavior.

动机是研究通过重整化群（RG）技术改进的类Schwarzschild黑洞的性质，重点在于在截断尺度$\xi$和插值参数$\gamma$处的量子效应如何修改经典黑洞的特征。这包括研究视界结构、光子球和阴影半径，以及准正规模、强宇宙监督和热力学行为。

Method: The authors use a unified treatment to set up the scalar, electromagnetic, and Dirac Regge-Wheeler-Zerilli problems for the RG-improved Schwarzschild-like black hole. They compute the fundamental and overtone quasinormal modes using sixth-order WKB methods, cross-checked against time-domain ringdown. The analysis includes the examination of the Strong Cosmic Censorship (SCC) at the inner Cauchy horizon and a thermodynamic analysis, uncovering a Davies-type phase transition and a nontrivial Weinhold-Ruppeiner geometry. A scan of the $(\xi, \gamma)$ plane summarizes the joint behavior of various physical quantities, and a comparison with other regular black holes (Bardeen, Hayward, and Bonanno-Reuter) is made.

作者使用统一处理方法为RG改进的类Schwarzschild黑洞设置标量、电磁和Dirac Regge-Wheeler-Zerilli问题。他们使用六阶WKB方法计算基本和泛音准正模式，并与时间域振铃进行交叉检查。分析包括在内部Cauchy视界处对强宇宙监督（SCC）的检查以及热力学分析，揭示了Davies型相变和非平凡的Weinhold-Ruppeiner几何。扫描$(\xi, \gamma)$平面总结了各种物理量的联合行为，并与其他规则黑洞（Bardeen、Hayward和Bonanno-Reuter）进行了比较。

Result: The results show that the RG-improved Schwarzschild-like black hole has a unique horizon structure, including an inner Cauchy horizon generated without charge or rotation. The SCC ratio $\beta = |\mathrm{Im}\,\omega|/\kappa_-$ is found to be multipole-independent at the 6% level. The thermodynamic analysis reveals a Davies-type phase transition and a nontrivial Weinhold-Ruppeiner geometry. The Hawking temperature profile exhibits a bell-curve peaking at $T_H^{\max} \simeq 0.062$. The shadow radius and other physical quantities are summarized in the $(\xi, \gamma)$ plane, and the RG-improved Schwarzschild-like black hole is found to be the most Schwarzschild-like among regular black holes at matched perturbation scale, with shadow-degenerate imaging at the 1% level against Hayward and Bonanno-Reuter black holes.

结果表明，RG改进的类Schwarzschild黑洞具有独特的视界结构，包括在没有电荷或旋转的情况下生成的内部Cauchy视界。SCC比率$\beta = |\mathrm{Im}\,\omega|/\kappa_-$在6%水平上被发现是多极独立的。热力学分析揭示了Davies型相变和非平凡的Weinhold-Ruppeiner几何。Hawking温度曲线呈现出峰值为$T_H^{\max} \simeq 0.062$的钟形曲线。阴影半径和其他物理量在$(\xi, \gamma)$平面上进行了总结，发现RG改进的类Schwarzschild黑洞在匹配扰动尺度下是最接近Schwarzschild黑洞的规则黑洞，其阴影退化成像在1%水平上与Hayward和Bonanno-Reuter黑洞一致。

Conclusion: The RG-improved Schwarzschild-like black hole provides a novel framework for understanding the interplay between classical and quantum aspects of black holes. The presence of an inner Cauchy horizon, the multipole-independent SCC ratio, and the thermodynamic phase transition indicate significant deviations from the classical Schwarzschild solution. The black hole's shadow and other physical properties are highly dependent on the parameters $\xi$ and $\gamma$, suggesting that these parameters play a crucial role in characterizing the quantum nature of the black hole. The RG-improved Schwarzschild-like black hole is the most Schwarzschild-like among regular black holes, making it a promising candidate for further theoretical and observational studies.

RG改进的类Schwarzschild黑洞提供了一个理解黑洞经典和量子方面相互作用的新框架。内部Cauchy视界的出现、多极独立的SCC比率和热力学相变表明与经典的Schwarzschild解有显著偏离。黑洞的阴影和其他物理性质高度依赖于参数$\xi$和$\gamma$，这表明这些参数在表征黑洞的量子性质中起着关键作用。RG改进的类Schwarzschild黑洞在规则黑洞中最接近Schwarzschild黑洞，使其成为进一步理论和观测研究的有希望的候选者。

Abstract: We study a renormalization-group (RG) improved Schwarzschild-like black hole (BH) whose lapse interpolates between a classical Schwarzschild exterior and a quantum-smoothed interior governed by a cutoff scale $ξ$ and an interpolation parameter $γ$. We work out the horizon structure together with the photon sphere and shadow radius $R_{\mathrm{sh}}$, set up the scalar, electromagnetic, and Dirac Regge-Wheeler-Zerilli problems in a unified treatment, and compute fundamental and overtone quasinormal modes via sixth-order WKB cross-checked against time-domain ringdown. We examine Strong Cosmic Censorship (SCC) at the inner Cauchy horizon -- a horizon the improved geometry generates without charge or rotation -- and find the ratio $β=|\mathrm{Im}\,ω|/κ_-$ to be multipole-independent at the $6\%$ level, following $β\simeqλ_{L}/κ_{-}$. A thermodynamic analysis uncovers a Davies-type phase transition of the outer horizon and a nontrivial Weinhold-Ruppeiner geometry on the $(S,γ)$ slice; the Schwarzschild $T_{H}\propto 1/r_{+}$ decay is replaced by a bell-curve profile peaking at $T_{H}^{\max}\simeq 0.062$. A scan of the $(ξ,γ)$ plane summarizes the joint behavior of the shadow, the scalar barrier, the SCC ratio, and $T_H$, and exhibits a thin crescent adjacent to the extremal boundary where Christodoulou-SCC marginally fails. A comparison against Bardeen, Hayward, and Bonanno-Reuter BHs places the improved Schwarzschild BH as the most Schwarzschild-like of the regular-BH family at matched perturbation scale, with shadow-degenerate imaging against Hayward and Bonanno-Reuter at the $1\%$ level. We close with the sparsity of the Hawking flux and the energy-emission rate, both depending cleanly on $(ξ,γ)$ through a single auxiliary function tied to the outer-horizon surface gravity.

### [57] [Link-based causal set propagators in $1+1$ dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24812)

TL;DR: The paper investigates the expression of retarded scalar propagators on causal sets in terms of the link matrix $\mathbf{L}$. The inverse kernel exp$(-\mathbf{L})$ is proposed as a discrete d'Alembertian.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of the paper is to explore the possibility of expressing retarded scalar propagators on causal sets using the link matrix $\mathbf{L}$. This is important for developing a more fundamental understanding of quantum field theory on discrete spacetime structures, which could lead to insights into quantum gravity. [English Text]\n\nThe motivation of the paper is to探索在因果集上使用链接矩阵$\mathbf{L}$表达延迟标量传播子的可能性。这对于发展对离散时空结构上的量子场论的更基本理解非常重要，可能为量子引力提供见解。

Method: The authors use asymptotic analysis and numerical simulations to show that the averaged massless retarded propagator in $1+1$ dimensional Minkowski spacetime can be associated with a normalized exponential of the link matrix $\mathbf{L}$. They extend this construction to the massive case using a mass-scattering series. [English Text]\n\n作者使用渐近分析和数值模拟来展示在$1+1$维闵可夫斯基时空中，平均无质量延迟传播子可以与链接矩阵$\mathbf{L}$的归一化指数相关联。他们通过质量散射级数将这一构造扩展到有质量的情况。

Result: The results show that the averaged massless retarded propagator is naturally associated with a normalized exponential of the link matrix $\mathbf{L}$. [English Text]\n\n结果表明，平均无质量延迟传播子自然地与链接矩阵$\mathbf{L}$的归一化指数相关联。对于有质量的情况，在平均后与连续传播子的一致性良好。提出了逆核exp$(-\mathbf{L})$作为离散达朗贝尔算子的可能候选者。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that the link matrix $\mathbf{L}$ can be used to express the averaged massless and massive retarded propagators on causal sets, and suggests that the inverse kernel exp$(-\mathbf{L})$ may serve as a discrete d'Alembertian. [English Text]\n\n论文得出结论，链接矩阵$\mathbf{L}$可以用来表达因果集上的平均无质量和有质量延迟传播子，并建议逆核exp$(-\mathbf{L})$可能作为离散达朗贝尔算子。

Abstract: We investigate whether retarded scalar propagators on causal sets can be expressed in terms of the link matrix $\mathbf{L}$. For Poisson sprinklings into $1+1$ dimensional Minkowski spacetime, we show by asymptotic analysis and supporting numerical simulations that the averaged massless retarded propagator is naturally associated with a normalized exponential exp$(\mathbf{L})$. We then extend the construction to the massive case via the usual mass-scattering series and obtain good agreement with the continuum propagator after averaging. Finally, we discuss the inverse kernel exp$(-\mathbf{L})$ as a possible candidate for a discrete d'Alembertian.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: The method involves computing the quasinormal mode frequencies of the QOS black hole, surrounded by quintessence dark energy and a cloud of strings, using the 6th-order Wentzel-Kramers-Brillouin (WKB) approximation. The effective potentials for both scalar and vector perturbation fields are calculated and their graphical behavior is analyzed. Result: The results show that the quasinormal mode frequencies and greybody factors of the QOS black hole are significantly influenced by the parameters of the string cloud, quantum deformation, and quintessence. Specifically, the greybody factors are found to be highly sensitive to changes in $\tilde{a}_{e}$, $\tildeσ_{e}$, and $\tilde{h}_{e}$. For scalar perturbations, strict limits on the greybody factors are provided, and the influence of the parameters $\tilde{a}_{e}$, $\tildeσ_{e}$, and $\tilde{h}_{e}$ is checked.

Conclusion: The study concludes that the presence of quintessential dark energy and string clouds significantly affects the quasinormal modes and greybody factors of the QOS black hole. The 6th-order WKB approximation method provides a reliable way to compute these quantities, and the results highlight the importance of considering additional fields and exotic matter in the analysis of black hole properties.

研究表明，暗能量和弦云的存在显著影响了QOS黑洞的准正模和灰体因子。6阶WKB近似方法提供了一种可靠的计算这些量的方法，结果强调了在分析黑洞性质时考虑额外场和奇异物质的重要性。

Abstract: We obtained quasinormal modes and greybody factors of the quantum Oppenheimer-Snyder (QOS) black hole with quintessential dark energy and string clouds. We compute the effective potentials of the scalar and the vector perturbation fields and analyze their graphical behavior. For this, we compute quasinormal mode frequencies of the QOS black hole, that is surrounded by quintessence dark energy and a cloud of strings and this is done by 6th-order Wentzel-Kramers-Brillouin (WKB) approximation method. We observe the quasinormal frequencies by analyzing both the quintessence parameters and the string cloud parameters. We also examine the GFs by analyzing the role of string cloud ($\tilde{a}_{e}$), quantum deformation ($\tildeσ_{e}$), and quintessence ($\tilde{h}_{e}$) parameters. It is found that GFs are significantly influenced by the parameters of $\tilde{a}_{e}$, $\tildeσ_{e}$, and $\tilde{h}_{e}$. In the case of scalar perturbation, we also give strict limits of the GFs and check the influence of the parameters of $\tilde{a}_{e}$, $\tildeσ_{e}$, and $\tilde{h}_{e}$.

### [59] [Bouncing cosmologies from Born-Infeld-type gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24860)
*Yermek Aldabergenov,Wei Lin,Rongjian Li,Ding Ding,Yidun Wan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper constructs a Born-Infeld-type $f(R, \cal{G})$ gravity by embedding Born-Infeld electrodynamics in a five-dimensional modified gravity. This theory is ghost-free and reduces to Einstein gravity at low energies. The focus is on bouncing cosmological solutions with positive spatial curvature, revealing a wide range of solutions with different asymptotic behaviors, including multiple bounces. Observational consequences will be explored in future work.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to develop a new type of modified gravity theory that incorporates the structure of Born-Infeld electrodynamics into the gravitational sector. This is achieved by establishing a correspondence between curvature scalars and electromagnetic field strength scalars, leading to a Born-Infeld-type $f(R, \cal{G})$ gravity. The aim is to explore the cosmological implications of such a theory, particularly focusing on bouncing solutions which are not possible in standard Einstein gravity.

动机是开发一种新的修改引力理论，将Born-Infeld电磁动力学的结构纳入引力部分。这是通过建立曲率标量和电磁场强度标量之间的对应关系来实现的，从而形成Born-Infeld型$f(R, \cal{G})$引力。目的是探讨这种理论的宇宙学意义，特别是聚焦于在标准爱因斯坦引力中不可能出现的反弹解。

Method: The method involves constructing a Born-Infeld-type $f(R, \cal{G})$ gravity by embedding Born-Infeld electrodynamics in a five-dimensional pure modified gravity. The correspondence between curvature scalars and electromagnetic field strength scalars -- $R \leftrightarrow F_{\mu\nu}F^{\mu\nu}$ and ${\cal G} \leftrightarrow (\varepsilon_{\mu\nu\rho\sigma}F^{\mu\nu}F^{\rho\sigma})^2$ -- is used to replicate the structure of Born-Infeld electrodynamics in the gravitational sector. The analysis is performed in both the Jordan and Einstein frames to find a variety of bouncing solutions with different asymptotic behaviors.

方法涉及通过将Born-Infeld电磁动力学嵌入五维纯修改引力中，构建一个Born-Infeld型$f(R, \cal{G})$引力。使用曲率标量和电磁场强度标量之间的对应关系 -- $R \leftrightarrow F_{\mu\nu}F^{\mu\nu}$ 和 ${\cal G} \leftrightarrow (\varepsilon_{\mu\nu\rho\sigma}F^{\mu\nu}F^{\rho\sigma})^2$ -- 来复制引力部分中的Born-Infeld电磁动力学结构。分析在Jordan框架和Einstein框架下进行，以找到具有不同渐近行为的各种反弹解。

Result: The result is a ghost-free Born-Infeld-type $f(R, \cal{G})$ gravity that reduces to Einstein gravity in the low energy limit. The theory admits a wide range of bouncing cosmological solutions with positive spatial curvature, including solutions with multiple bounces. The analysis in both the Jordan and Einstein frames reveals different asymptotic behaviors for these solutions.

结果是一个无鬼（ghost-free）的Born-Infeld型$f(R, \cal{G})$引力，在低能极限下还原为爱因斯坦引力。该理论允许存在广泛的具有正空间曲率的宇宙反弹解，包括多次反弹的解。在Jordan框架和Einstein框架下的分析揭示了这些解的不同渐近行为。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the constructed Born-Infeld-type $f(R, \cal{G})$ gravity provides a rich framework for exploring bouncing cosmological solutions with positive spatial curvature. The theory is ghost-free and reduces to Einstein gravity at low energies, making it a viable candidate for modified gravity. Future work will investigate the observational consequences of these solutions.

结论是所构建的Born-Infeld型$f(R, \cal{G})$引力为探索具有正空间曲率的宇宙反弹解提供了丰富的框架。该理论无鬼且在低能极限下还原为爱因斯坦引力，使其成为修改引力的一个可行候选者。未来的工作将研究这些解的观测后果。

Abstract: We construct a Born-Infeld-type $f(R,{\cal G})$ modification of gravity, where ${\cal G}$ is the Gauss-Bonnet term, by embedding Born-Infeld electrodynamics in a five-dimensional pure modified gravity. This method leads to the correspondence between curvature scalars and electromagnetic field strength scalars -- $R\leftrightarrow F_{μν}F^{μν}$ and ${\cal G}\leftrightarrow (ε_{μνρσ}F^{μν}F^{ρσ})^2$ -- allowing us to replicate the structure of Born-Infeld electrodynamics in the gravitational sector. The resulting Born-Infeld-type gravity is a ghost-free $f(R,{\cal G})$ theory which reduces to Einstein gravity in the low energy limit. In this work we focus on bouncing cosmological solutions of such a theory, which require positive spatial curvature. By using both the Jordan and Einstein frame analyses, we find a vast space of bouncing solutions with different asymptotic behaviors, including solutions with multiple bounces grouped together. Observational consequences of such solutions will be investigated in the future.

### [60] [Hawking radiation with dispersion: reconciling the Bogoliubov and tunneling approaches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24861)
*Francesco Del Porro,Stefano Liberati,Marc Schneider*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper explores Hawking-like particle production in analogue gravity systems with superluminal modified dispersion relations, showing that the emission spectrum is controlled by an effective surface gravity. The results establish a connection between Bogoliubov and tunneling descriptions and clarify the robustness of Hawking radiation against ultraviolet modifications.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand how Hawking-like particle production behaves in systems with superluminal modified dispersion relations, which are relevant for analogue gravity. The study aims to connect the Bogoliubov and tunneling methods and to determine the conditions under which Hawking radiation remains robust against ultraviolet (UV) modifications.

Method: The authors use a near-horizon S-matrix method extended beyond the purely sonic regime to compute the Bogoliubov coefficients. They also employ the tunneling approach to derive the emission spectrum. Both methods are applied to a class of even, convex, and polynomially bounded dispersion relations, and the results are compared in the low-energy and adiabatic limits.

Result: The results show that the emission spectrum is controlled by an effective surface gravity associated with the effective horizon. The Bogoliubov coefficients and the tunneling result agree in the low-energy and adiabatic limits, leading to controlled deviations from exact thermality. This establishes an analytical connection between the two methods and clarifies the robustness of Hawking radiation in dispersive settings.

Conclusion: The conclusion is that Hawking-like particle production in analogue gravity systems with superluminal modified dispersion relations is governed by an effective surface gravity, and the emission spectrum deviates controllably from thermality. The agreement between the Bogoliubov and tunneling methods provides a deeper understanding of the conditions under which Hawking radiation remains robust against UV modifications.

Abstract: We investigate Hawking-like particle production in analogue gravity systems with superluminal modified dispersion relations. For a broad class of even, convex, and polynomially bounded dispersion relations, we show that the relevant outgoing modes are governed by an effective horizon induced by dispersive propagation. Extending the near-horizon S-matrix method beyond the purely sonic regime, we compute the Bogoliubov coefficients and demonstrate that, in the low-energy and adiabatic limits, they agree with the tunneling result obtained from the approximant ray. In both cases, the emission spectrum is controlled by an effective surface gravity associated to the effective horizon, leading to controlled deviations from exact thermality. Our results establish an analytical connection between the Bogoliubov and tunneling descriptions in dispersive settings and clarify the conditions under which Hawking radiation remains robust against ultraviolet modifications, with implications extending beyond analogue gravity.

### [61] [Underlying mechanisms of phase transitions in scalar-tensor theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24867)

This is crucial for understanding astrophysical observables related to scalarization.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The spontaneous scalarization phenomenon in scalar-tensor gravity is a phase transition whose order changes with the theory's parameters. While a phenomenological description exists via Landau theory, the underlying mechanisms determining the coefficients of the Landau expansion were not known. The motivation is to understand these mechanisms and predict the phase transition order for different conditions. [English Text]
The spontaneous scalarization phenomenon in scalar-tensor gravity is a phase transition, and its order changes with the parameters of the theory. Although there is a phenomenological description based on Landau theory, the underlying mechanisms that determine the coefficients of the Landau expansion were unknown. The motivation is to understand these mechanisms and predict the order of the phase transition under different conditions. [Chinese Text]

Method: The authors start with an energy functional that captures the nonlinear behavior of the scalar-tensor theory and reduce it to an energy function. This allows them to calculate the coefficients of the Landau expansion from first principles, providing a deeper understanding of the scalarization phase transition. [English Text]
作者从一个描述标量-张量理论非线性行为的能量泛函开始，将其简化为能量函数。这使他们能够从第一原理计算Landau展开的系数，从而更深入地理解标量化相变。[Chinese Text]

Result: The calculated coefficients of the Landau expansion explain the previously observed but not well-understood features of the scalarization phase transition. Additionally, the results enable the prediction of the phase transition order for different coupling functions and parameter regimes. [English Text]

[English Text]
通过从第一原理计算Landau展开系数，该研究提供了对标量-张量引力中自发标量化现象的更深层次理解。这使得预测相变阶数成为可能，并对天体物理可观测量（如一阶标量化中亚稳态之间的跃迁信号）具有重要意义。[Chinese Text]

Abstract: Spontaneous scalarization phenomenon in scalar-tensor gravity is known to be a form of phase transition, and it was recently shown that the order of this transition changes depending on the parameters of the theory. There exists a phenomenological description of this result based on Landau theory, but the underlying mechanisms which determine the coefficients of the Landau expansion were unknown. In this study we calculate these coefficients starting from first principles. To this end, we start with an energy functional that describes the nonlinear behavior of the theory, and reduce it to an energy function. This allows us to explain the previously observed, but not well-understood, features of the scalarization phase transition, and enables us to predict which phase transition order will be present for which coupling function or in which regime of the parameter space. The details of the phase transition determine certain astrophysical observables such as signals sourced by transitions from metastable states in first-order scalarization. Thus, predicting these details is an important part of understanding scalarization itself.

### [62] [Sensitivity of black hole spectral instability against perturbations of the effective potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24926)
*Ramin G. Daghigh,Michael D. Green,Guan-Ru Li,Jodin C. Morey,Wei-Liang Qian,Stefan J. Randow*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper investigates the spectral instability of black hole quasinormal modes, focusing on the sensitivity of the fundamental mode to small perturbations in the effective potential. Both analytical and numerical methods are used to explore how different factors, such as the shape of the potential and the nature of the perturbation, influence this instability.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand the counterintuitive behavior of black hole quasinormal modes, specifically the spectral instability, which contradicts many plausible assumptions. The study aims to explore the strong sensitivity of the fundamental mode to small perturbations in the effective potential, caused by modifications in the spacetime metrics.

研究动机是理解黑洞准正则模式的反直觉行为，特别是谱不稳定性，这与许多合理的假设相矛盾。研究旨在探索基本模式对有效势微小扰动的强烈敏感性，这些扰动是由时空度量的小尺度修改引起的。

Method: The method involves both analytical and numerical approaches. Analytical methods are used to derive and understand the equations governing the perturbations, while numerical simulations are employed to visualize and quantify the effects of these perturbations on the black hole's quasinormal modes.

该方法包括分析和数值方法。分析方法用于推导和理解控制扰动的方程，而数值模拟用于可视化和量化这些扰动对黑洞准正则模式的影响。

Result: The results show that the fundamental mode of the black hole's quasinormal spectrum is highly sensitive to small perturbations in the effective potential. The qualitative way in which the fundamental mode becomes perturbed varies depending on the shape of the potential and the nature of the perturbation.

结果表明，黑洞准正则谱的基本模式对有效势的微小扰动非常敏感。基本模式受扰动的方式根据势的形状和扰动的性质而有所不同。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the spectral instability of black holes is a complex phenomenon, with the fundamental mode being particularly sensitive to small-scale modifications of the spacetime metrics. This sensitivity depends on multiple factors, including the shape of the potential and the specific nature of the perturbation.

结论是，黑洞的谱不稳定性是一个复杂的现象，其中基本模式对时空度量的小尺度修改特别敏感。这种敏感性取决于多种因素，包括势的形状和扰动的具体性质。

Abstract: Black hole spectral instability is counterintuitive and contradicts many plausible assumptions of the properties of black hole quasinormal modes. The present study aims to explore different types of instability phenomena. It is understood that the fundamental mode is surprisingly sensitive to small perturbations of the effective potential of the linearized wave equation. Such perturbations can be produced by small-scale modifications of the spacetime metrics. From both the analytical and numerical perspectives, we elaborate on a few qualitatively different examples illustrating the strong sensitivity and diversity in black hole spectral instability caused by such effective potential perturbations. It turns out that the qualitative way in which the fundamental mode becomes perturbed depends on many factors such as the shape of the potential and how the perturbation changes as it moves away from the central black hole.

### [63] [Wellposedness of the initial boundary value problem for the conformal field equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24931)
*Chris Stevens,Juan A. Valiente Kroon*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper formulates the initial boundary value problem for Friedrich's extended conformal Einstein field equations with boundary data on a timelike hypersurface. It uses a gauge based on conformal geodesics, identifies consistent maximally dissipative boundary conditions, and establishes well-posedness and constraint propagation.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to provide a rigorous mathematical framework for the initial boundary value problem in the context of Friedrich's extended conformal Einstein field equations. The authors aim to address the challenges associated with prescribing boundary data on a timelike hypersurface and to establish the well-posedness of the problem under certain boundary conditions.

本文的动机是为Friedrich扩展共形爱因斯坦场方程的初边值问题提供一个严格的数学框架。作者旨在解决在类时超曲面上规定边界数据所面临的挑战，并在某些边界条件下建立该问题的适定性。

Method: The method employed in this paper involves the use of a gauge based on the properties of conformal geodesics. The authors require that the boundary be ruled by timelike conformal geodesics, which leads to specific constraints on the boundary data. They then identify a subset of maximally dissipative boundary conditions that are consistent with these constraints. Using this setup, they prove the well-posedness of the initial boundary value problem and the propagation of the constraints.

本文采用的方法基于共形测地线的性质。作者要求边界由类时共形测地线决定，这导致了对边界数据的具体约束。然后，他们确定了一组与这些约束一致的最大耗散边界条件。利用这种设置，他们证明了初边值问题的适定性和约束的传播。

Result: The results of this paper include the formulation of the initial boundary value problem for Friedrich's extended conformal Einstein field equations with boundary data prescribed on a timelike hypersurface. The authors successfully identify a class of maximally dissipative boundary conditions that are consistent with the assumption that the boundary is ruled by timelike conformal geodesics. They also establish the well-posedness of the problem and prove that the constraints propagate correctly.

本文的结果包括在类时超曲面上规定边界数据的情况下，Friedrich扩展共形爱因斯坦场方程的初边值问题的表述。作者成功地确定了一组与边界由类时共形测地线决定这一假设一致的最大耗散边界条件。他们还建立了问题的适定性，并证明了约束正确传播。

Conclusion: In conclusion, the paper provides a novel and mathematically rigorous approach to the initial boundary value problem for Friedrich's extended conformal Einstein field equations. By using a gauge based on conformal geodesics and identifying consistent boundary conditions, the authors have established the well-posedness of the problem and the propagation of the constraints, thus contributing to the theoretical understanding of general relativity and its applications.

总之，本文为Friedrich扩展共形爱因斯坦场方程的初边值问题提供了新颖且数学上严格的处理方法。通过使用基于共形测地线的规范并确定一致的边界条件，作者建立了问题的适定性和约束的传播，从而为广义相对论及其应用的理论理解做出了贡献。

Abstract: We provide a formulation of the initial boundary value problem for Friedrich's extended conformal Einstein field equations in which boundary data is prescribed on a timelike hypersurface located at a finite position in the spacetime. Our construction relies on a gauge based on the properties of conformal geodesics and requires the the boundary is ruled by timelike conformal geodesics. The consequences of this assumption on the timelike boundary are analysed and we identify a subset of maximally dissipative boundary conditions which are consistent with this assumption. For this class of consistent boundary conditions we establish the wellposedness of the initial boundary value problem and prove the propagation of the constraints.

### [64] [A general formalism for coupling scalar fields to the Einstein equations without a variational principle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24944)
*Joshua Ritchie*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper introduces a new method for coupling scalar fields to gravity without using a variational principle or Lagrangian. It shows that the method can reproduce minimally and $k$-essence scalar field couplings with a non-zero potential, and it explores Bianchi I type solutions, establishing conditions for asymptotically Kasner solutions near the initial singularity and investigating their stability.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this work is to develop a generic method for coupling scalar fields to gravity within General Relativity, which does not rely on the traditional variational principle or Lagrangian formalism. The authors aim to explore the implications of such a coupling on the dynamics of the universe, particularly in the context of anisotropic (Bianchi I) models.

本文的动机是在广义相对论框架内开发一种将标量场与引力耦合的一般方法，这种方法不依赖于传统的变分原理或拉格朗日形式。作者旨在探索这种耦合对宇宙动力学的影响，特别是在各向异性（Bianchi I型）模型中的影响。

Method: A new method is proposed for coupling scalar fields to the Einstein equations without employing a variational principle or a Lagrangian. This method is shown to be capable of reproducing known couplings, such as minimal and $k$-essence scalar field couplings, with a non-zero potential. The approach allows for free parameters, referred to as constitutive freedoms, which are then chosen to make the system 'near minimal'. The resulting system is analyzed for Bianchi I type solutions, focusing on the conditions for asymptotically Kasner behavior and the stability of these solutions near the initial singularity.

提出了一种新的方法，用于将标量场与爱因斯坦方程耦合，而无需使用变分原理或拉格朗日函数。该方法被证明能够重现已知的耦合，如最小和$k$-本质标量场耦合，并且具有非零势能。该方法允许自由参数，称为构成自由度，然后选择这些自由参数以使系统“接近最小”。分析了由此产生的系统在Bianchi I型解下的情况，重点是渐近Kasner行为的条件以及这些解在初始奇点附近的稳定性。

Result: The results show that the new method for coupling scalar fields to gravity can indeed reproduce the known forms of scalar field couplings, including minimal and $k$-essence couplings. By choosing the free fields appropriately, the system can be made to exhibit 'near minimal' behavior. The analysis of Bianchi I type solutions reveals that under certain conditions, the solutions are asymptotically Kasner, and the stability properties of these solutions near the initial singularity are investigated.

结果表明，用于将标量场与引力耦合的新方法确实可以重现已知的标量场耦合形式，包括最小和$k$-本质耦合。通过适当选择自由场，可以使系统表现出“接近最小”的行为。对Bianchi I型解的分析表明，在某些条件下，解是渐近Kasner的，并且研究了这些解在初始奇点附近的稳定性。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that the new method for coupling scalar fields to gravity is a viable alternative to the traditional Lagrangian-based approach. It provides a generic framework that can accommodate different types of scalar field couplings and allows for the exploration of anisotropic cosmological models. The investigation of Bianchi I type solutions further demonstrates the applicability of this method in understanding the early universe's dynamics, especially near the initial singularity.

本文得出结论，将标量场与引力耦合的新方法是传统基于拉格朗日方法的一个可行替代方案。它提供了一个通用框架，可以容纳不同类型的标量场耦合，并允许探索各向异性的宇宙模型。对Bianchi I型解的研究进一步证明了该方法在理解早期宇宙动力学方面的适用性，尤其是在初始奇点附近。

Abstract: The purpose of this work is to discuss how matter fields are coupled to gravity within the framework of General Relativity. Our particular focus here is on the coupling of scalar field models. In a first step, we suggest a new method for coupling scalar fields to the Einstein equations \emph{without} the use of a variational principle or Lagrangian. We show that, under the appropriate assumptions, this new method (for coupling scalar fields to gravity) reproduces the minimally and $k$-essence scalar field couplings with a non-zero potential. We therefore interpret this formalism as describing a \emph{generic} method for coupling scalar fields to gravity. The approach described here allows for a number of free fields which we interpret as constitutive freedoms. In a second step, we choose these free fields in such a way that the resulting system is somehow ``near minimal''. In this setting we investigate Bianchi I type solutions. We establish conditions under which the solutions are asymptotically Kasner, near the initial singularity, and investigate their stability properties.

### [65] [Toller matrices and the Feynman $i\varepsilon$ in spinfoams](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24945)
*Eugenio Bianchi,Chaosong Chen,Mauricio Gamonal*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper analyzes the Toller matrices $T^{(\pm)}$ in 4d Lorentzian quantum gravity, showing their equivalence to the Feynman $i\varepsilon$ prescription and an integral over eigenvalues of the boost operator. Explicit expressions are provided using hypergeometric functions, and the connection to the Wick rotation from Euclidean to Lorentzian spinfoams is discussed.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to explore the analytic properties and equivalent representations of the Toller matrices $T^{(\pm)}$ that appear in the causal formulation of spinfoam transition amplitudes for 4d Lorentzian quantum gravity. The goal is to establish a deeper understanding of these matrices and their role in the context of quantum gravity by connecting them with different mathematical frameworks.

本文的动机是研究在四维洛伦兹量子引力的因果形式中出现的Toller矩阵$T^{(\pm)}$的解析性质和等价表示。目的是通过将这些矩阵与不同的数学框架联系起来，更深入地理解这些矩阵及其在量子引力中的作用。

Method: The authors use Ruhl's definition of $T^{(\pm)}$ in terms of analyticity and asymptotic properties, and show its equivalence to the recently introduced Feynman $i\varepsilon$ prescription in spinfoams. They also represent $T^{(\pm)}$ as an integral over eigenvalues of the boost operator, which results in a sum over residues. This representation reproduces the Wick rotation relating Euclidean $Spin(4)$ to Lorentzian $SL(2,\mathbb{C})$ spinfoams. Explicit expressions for $T^{(\pm)}$ are derived using hypergeometric functions, with a focus on $\gamma$-simple representations relevant for spinfoams.

作者使用Ruhl关于$T^{(\pm)}$的定义，基于解析性和渐近性质，并展示了它与最近引入的Feynman $i\varepsilon$ 处方在自旋泡沫中的等价性。他们还将$T^{(\pm)}$ 表示为增益算子特征值上的积分，这导致了留数之和。这种表示再现了从欧几里得$Spin(4)$到洛伦兹$SL(2,\mathbb{C})$自旋泡沫的Wick旋转。使用超几何函数推导出$T^{(\pm)}$ 的显式表达式，重点在于与自旋泡沫相关的$\gamma$-简单表示。

Result: The key results include the demonstration of the equivalence between Ruhl's definition and the Feynman $i\varepsilon$ prescription, and the representation of $T^{(\pm)}$ as an integral over eigenvalues of the boost operator. The explicit expressions for $T^{(\pm)}$ in terms of hypergeometric functions are provided, and the connection to the Wick rotation is established. These findings provide a new perspective on the Toller matrices and their role in spinfoam models.

主要结果包括证明了Ruhl的定义与Feynman $i\varepsilon$ 处方之间的等价性，以及将$T^{(\pm)}$ 表示为增益算子特征值上的积分。提供了$T^{(\pm)}$ 在超几何函数方面的显式表达式，并建立了与Wick旋转的联系。这些发现为Toller矩阵及其在自旋泡沫模型中的作用提供了新的视角。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that the Toller matrices $T^{(\pm)}$ can be equivalently described using Ruhl's definition, the Feynman $i\varepsilon$ prescription, and an integral over eigenvalues of the boost operator. These descriptions provide a unified framework for understanding the analytic properties and representations of $T^{(\pm)}$ in the context of 4d Lorentzian quantum gravity. The explicit expressions and the connection to the Wick rotation further enrich the theoretical framework of spinfoam models.

论文得出结论，Toller矩阵$T^{(\pm)}$ 可以用Ruhl的定义、Feynman $i\varepsilon$ 处方和增益算子特征值上的积分等价描述。这些描述为理解四维洛伦兹量子引力背景下$T^{(\pm)}$ 的解析性质和表示提供了一个统一的框架。显式表达式和与Wick旋转的联系进一步丰富了自旋泡沫模型的理论框架。

Abstract: We study the analytic properties and three equivalent representations of the Toller matrices $T^{(\pm)}$ which appear in the causal formulation of spinfoam transition amplitudes for 4d Lorentzian quantum gravity. These are polynomially bounded functions on the Lorentz group which satisfy the relation $T^{(+)}+T^{(-)}=D$, where the Wigner matrix $D$ provides a unitary irreducible representation of $SL(2,C)$. Ruhl's definition of $T^{(\pm)}$ in terms of analyticity and asymptotic properties is shown to be equivalent to the recently introduced Feynman $i\varepsilon$ prescription in spinfoams. We show that, equivalently, they can be represented as an integral over eigenvalues of the boost operator, which results in a sum over residues. The latter reproduces the Wick rotation relating Euclidean $Spin(4)$ to Lorentzian $SL(2,C)$ spinfoams studied by Dona, Gozzini and Nicotra. We provide explicit expressions in terms of hypergeometric functions and specialize them to the $γ$-simple representations relevant for spinfoams.

### [66] [Peculiar velocities in the $Λ$CDM universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24974)
*Evanthia Patliaka,Christos G. Tsagas*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper analyzes the linear evolution of peculiar-velocity perturbations in pressureless matter from the Einstein-de Sitter epoch to the $\Lambda$-dominated phase. It finds that peculiar velocities grow linearly during the Einstein-de Sitter era but are suppressed and eventually decay as $\Omega_\Lambda$ increases, leading to higher bulk-flow velocities at intermediate redshifts compared to $\Lambda$CDM predictions.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to provide a comprehensive understanding of the linear evolution of peculiar-velocity perturbations in a cosmological context, encompassing both the Einstein-de Sitter and $\Lambda$-dominated epochs. The study aims to reconcile theoretical predictions with observed peculiar-velocity profiles reported in the literature.

动机是提供对宇宙学背景下从爱因斯坦-德西特时期到$\Lambda$主导时期的特殊速度扰动线性演化的全面理解。研究旨在将理论预测与文献中报道的观测到的特殊速度分布进行调和。

Method: The method involves deriving generalized differential equations for the evolution of peculiar-velocity perturbations in a non-interacting, non-comoving mixture of radiation and dust, using full general relativity. The analysis covers both the Einstein-de Sitter and $\Lambda$-dominated phases, providing a unified framework for the entire post-recombination period.

方法涉及使用完整的广义相对论推导出在非相互作用、非共动的辐射和尘埃混合物中特殊速度扰动演化的广义微分方程。分析涵盖了爱因斯坦-德西特时期和$\Lambda$主导时期，为再结合后的整个时期提供了统一的框架。

Result: The results show that peculiar velocities grow linearly with time ($v \propto t$) during the Einstein-de Sitter era. As the $\Omega_\Lambda$ contribution increases, the growth of peculiar velocities is suppressed and eventually decays. This leads to higher bulk-flow velocities at intermediate redshifts, which are expected to exceed those predicted by the $\Lambda$CDM model, followed by a decline at lower redshifts.

结果显示，在爱因斯坦-德西特时期，特殊速度随时间线性增长（$v \propto t$）。随着$\Omega_\Lambda$贡献的增加，特殊速度的增长受到抑制并最终衰减。这导致在中间红移处有更高的整体流动速度，这些速度预计将超过$\Lambda$CDM模型的预测，然后在较低红移处下降。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the peculiar-velocity field undergoes a transition from growth to suppression and eventual decay as the universe evolves from the Einstein-de Sitter to the $\Lambda$-dominated phase. This transition can explain the observed peculiar-velocity profiles at intermediate redshifts, which are higher than those predicted by the standard $\Lambda$CDM model, and their subsequent decline at lower redshifts.

结论是，随着宇宙从爱因斯坦-德西特时期演化到$\Lambda$主导时期，特殊速度场经历了从增长到抑制再到最终衰减的转变。这种转变可以解释在中间红移处观察到的比标准$\Lambda$CDM模型预测更高的特殊速度分布，以及它们在较低红移处的随后下降。

Abstract: We present a unified analysis of the linear evolution of peculiar-velocity perturbations in the distribution of pressureless matter after recombination. Our study is carried out within the framework of full general relativity and encompasses both the earlier Einstein-de Sitter epoch and the subsequent $Λ$-dominated phase. Starting from a non-interacting, non-comoving mixture of radiation and dust, we derive the generalized differential equations governing the evolution of these velocity perturbations. We confirm that linear peculiar velocities ($v$) grow as $v\propto t$ throughout the Einstein-de Sitter era. In contrast, during a later phase of increasing $Ω_Λ$-contribution, we find that the growth of the peculiar-velocity field is progressively suppressed, before reversing to decay. Nevertheless, part of the earlier velocity growth persists to the present. Hence, bulk-flow velocities at intermediate redshifts are expected to exceed those predicted by the $Λ$CDM model, followed by a decline in their value at lower redshifts. Interestingly, such peculiar-velocity profiles have already been reported in the literature.

### [67] [Gauge Theoretic Signal Processing II: Zero-Latency Whitening for Early Warning Pipelines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25116)
*James Kennington,Joshua Black,Zach Yarbrough,Yun-Jing Huang,Chad Hanna,Leo Tsukada,Amanda Baylor,Olivia Godwin,Prathamesh Joshi,Cody Messick,Surabhi Sachdev,Ron Tapia*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper introduces and validates a gauge theoretic signal processing framework for causal, minimum-phase whitening filters in gravitational-wave search pipelines. This framework preserves the matched-filter SNR and sky-localization accuracy, reducing the algorithmic latency by 1.0 s (33%) at a 4-second noise estimation cadence. Up to 91% of baseline trigger latency can be eliminated with sub-second pipeline cadence.

本文介绍并验证了一种用于因果、最小相位白化滤波器的规范理论信号处理框架。该框架保持了匹配滤波信噪比和天空定位精度，将算法延迟减少了1.0秒（33%），在4秒噪声估计周期下。通过次秒级管道周期，最多可以消除91%的基线触发延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to eliminate the several seconds of algorithmic latency introduced by acausal, linear-phase filters in low-latency gravitational-wave search pipelines. The goal is to develop causal, minimum-phase whitening filters that can operate under non-stationary noise conditions without degrading the matched-filter SNR or sky-localization accuracy.

动机是消除低延迟引力波搜索管道中非因果、线性相位滤波器引入的几秒钟算法延迟。目标是开发能够在非平稳噪声条件下运行的因果、最小相位白化滤波器，同时不降低匹配滤波信噪比或天空定位精度。

Method: A gauge theoretic signal processing framework is introduced, which uses the minimum-phase connection on the manifold of power spectra to provide a geometrically exact update rule for causal filters. The framework is validated numerically and operationally through an injection campaign on O3 data with 15,347 binary black hole signals across the LIGO-Virgo network. The framework is implemented in the production sgnl pipeline, and its performance is confirmed in controlled tests and on live O3 replay data at production scale.

引入了一种规范理论信号处理框架，该框架使用功率谱流形上的最小相位连接来提供因果滤波器的几何精确更新规则。通过在LIGO-Virgo网络中的O3数据上进行包含15,347个双黑洞信号的注入实验，数值和操作上验证了该框架。该框架在生产sgnl管道中实现，并在其性能在受控测试和生产规模下的实时O3重放数据中得到确认。

Result: The results show that the gauge theoretic signal processing framework strictly preserves the minimum-phase property while exactly conserving the matched-filter SNR. The framework also maintains sky-localization accuracy and detection sensitivity. Implementing the framework in the sgnl pipeline reduces whitening latency by 1.0 s (33%) at a 4-second noise estimation cadence. Stride reduction experiments show that up to 91% of baseline trigger latency can be eliminated with sub-second pipeline cadence.

结果表明，规范理论信号处理框架严格保持了最小相位特性，同时精确地保持了匹配滤波信噪比。该框架还保持了天空定位精度和检测灵敏度。在sgnl管道中实施该框架，在4秒噪声估计周期下将白化延迟减少了1.0秒（33%）。步长减少实验表明，通过次秒级管道周期，最多可以消除91%的基线触发延迟。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that the introduced gauge theoretic signal processing framework is effective in reducing the algorithmic latency of low-latency gravitational-wave search pipelines while preserving the key performance metrics such as matched-filter SNR, sky-localization accuracy, and detection sensitivity. The framework provides a path-independent state function of the instantaneous noise, ensuring optimal filter updates.

本文得出结论，引入的规范理论信号处理框架在保持关键性能指标（如匹配滤波信噪比、天空定位精度和检测灵敏度）的同时，有效减少了低延迟引力波搜索管道的算法延迟。该框架提供了瞬时噪声的路径独立状态函数，确保了最优滤波器更新。

Abstract: Low-latency gravitational-wave search pipelines provide early-warning alerts for multimessenger astrophysical transients. Current pipelines whiten the data stream using acausal, linear-phase filters, which require a look-ahead buffer that introduces several seconds of algorithmic latency. Eliminating this latency requires causal, minimum-phase whitening filters using only past data. However, operating causal filters under non-stationary noise is non-trivial: the drifting power spectral density must be tracked without degrading the matched-filter signal-to-noise ratio (SNR), filter updates must preserve the minimum-phase condition, and the altered phase response must be compensated to maintain sky-localization accuracy. In Paper I we introduced a gauge theoretic signal processing framework and showed that the minimum-phase connection on the manifold of power spectra provides a geometrically exact update rule for causal filters. Here we validate that framework numerically and operationally, demonstrating that parallel transport along this connection strictly preserves the minimum-phase property while exactly conserving the matched-filter SNR. We numerically certify the flatness of this connection, showing that the optimal filter is a path-independent state function of the instantaneous noise. Through an injection campaign on O3 data with 15,347 binary black hole signals across the LIGO-Virgo network, we confirm that this architecture preserves the detection sensitivity and inter-detector timing and phase accuracy of the linear-phase baseline. Implementing the framework in the production sgnl pipeline reduces whitening latency by 1.0 s (33%) at a 4-second noise estimation cadence, confirmed in controlled tests and on live O3 replay data at production scale. Stride reduction experiments show that up to 91% of baseline trigger latency can be eliminated with sub-second pipeline cadence.

### [68] [Covariant quantization of the Einstein-Hilbert theory in first-order form](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25117)
*S. Martins-Filho*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper presents a covariant quantization of the first-order formulation of the Einstein-Hilbert theory using path integral and BV formalisms, showing that the gauge algebra is closed and irreducible. A new trivial local symmetry leads to structural identities for the Green's functions of the auxiliary field. The quantum equivalence between first- and second-order formulations is revisited, and a manifestly covariant Senjanović measure is derived. The effective actions of both formulations are shown to be equivalent when the auxiliary field is on-shell.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to provide a rigorous and covariant quantization of the first-order formulation of the Einstein-Hilbert theory, which treats the metric $g^{\mu\nu}$ and the connection $\Gamma^\lambda_{\mu\nu}$ as independent fields. This approach aims to explore the gauge symmetries, derive a covariant form of the Senjanovi\'c measure, and establish the quantum equivalence with the second-order formulation.

Method: The method involves the use of the path integral and Batalin-Vilkovisky (BV) formalisms to quantize the first-order formulation of the Einstein-Hilbert action. The authors treat the metric and the connection as independent fields, where the connection acts as an auxiliary field. They analyze the gauge algebra, identify a novel trivial local symmetry, and derive structural identities. Additionally, they derive a covariant form of the Senjanovi\'c measure and show the equivalence of the effective actions for both formulations when the auxiliary field is on-shell.

Result: The results include the demonstration that the gauge algebra is closed and irreducible. A new trivial local symmetry is identified, leading to structural identities that relate the Green's functions of the auxiliary field to its classical value. A manifestly covariant form of the Senjanovi\'c measure is obtained. The effective actions of the first- and second-order formulations are shown to be equivalent when the auxiliary field is on-shell.

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the first-order formulation of the Einstein-Hilbert theory can be consistently quantized in a covariant manner using the path integral and BV formalisms. The identification of a new trivial local symmetry and the derivation of the covariant Senjanovi\'c measure are significant contributions. The quantum equivalence between the first- and second-order formulations is established, providing a deeper understanding of the quantization of gravity.

Abstract: We present a covariant quantization of the first-order formulation of the Einstein-Hilbert theory using the path integral and BV formalisms. In this approach, the metric $g^{μν}$ and the connection $Γ^λ_{μν}$ are treated as independent, with the connection playing the role of an auxiliary field. We show that the gauge algebra is closed and irreducible. A novel trivial local symmetry arises, leading to structural identities that relate the Green's functions of the auxiliary field to its classical value. We revisit the quantum equivalence between the first- and second-order formulations of the Einstein-Hilbert theory. By employing a suitable trick, a manifestly covariant form of the Senjanović measure is derived. We also show that the two formulations are equivalent at the level of the effective action when the auxiliary field is on-shell.

### [69] [Early-Time Nonlinear Growth in an Unstable Q-Ball Hairy Black Hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25223)
*Lang Cheng,Guangzhou Guo,Peng Wang,Haitang Yang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The early-time evolution of a Q-ball hairy black hole in Einstein-Maxwell theory, with a charged self-interacting scalar field, is not solely governed by the linear instability. The more strongly responding component of the scalar field follows the linear unstable quasinormal mode (QNM), while the growth of the weaker component is dominated by a second-order QNM, even when the system remains in a perturbative regime.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to investigate the early-time evolution of a Q-ball hairy black hole in Einstein-Maxwell theory with a charged self-interacting scalar field, particularly focusing on the role of quasinormal modes (QNMs) during the unstable growth stage. The authors aim to challenge the common expectation that the early-time evolution is primarily governed by the associated linear instability, and to demonstrate that higher-order effects can significantly influence the dynamics of the system.

Method: The authors combine full nonlinear evolution with first- and second-order quasinormal mode (QNM) calculations. They analyze the behavior of the scalar field components, where one component has a much larger amplitude in the linear unstable QNM than the other. The method involves detailed numerical simulations and theoretical analysis to track the evolution of the system and the contributions from different QNMs.

Result: The results show that the early-time evolution of the Q-ball hairy black hole is not solely governed by the linear instability. Specifically, the more strongly responding component of the scalar field follows the linear unstable QNM, while the early growth of the more weakly responding component is dominated by a second-order QNM sourced by the linear unstable mode. This occurs even when the evolution remains in a perturbative regime, indicating that higher-order QNMs play a significant role in the system's dynamics.

Conclusion: The study concludes that the early growth of an individual component of the scalar field in a Q-ball hairy black hole need not be governed by its linear response. Instead, the dynamics can be influenced by higher-order quasinormal modes, which are sourced by the linear unstable mode. This finding challenges the conventional understanding and highlights the importance of considering higher-order effects in the analysis of nonlinear systems.

Abstract: Early-time evolution away from an unstable equilibrium in a nonlinear system is often expected to be governed by the associated linear instability. Combining full nonlinear evolution with first- and second-order quasinormal mode (QNM) calculations, we show that this expectation can fail during the unstable growth stage of a Q-ball hairy black hole in Einstein-Maxwell theory with a charged self-interacting scalar field. The linear unstable QNM has a much larger amplitude in one component of the scalar field than in the other: the more strongly responding component follows that mode, whereas the early growth of the more weakly responding component is dominated by a second-order QNM sourced by the linear unstable mode. This occurs while the evolution remains perturbative. Our results thus show that the early growth of an individual component need not be governed by its linear response.
