### [70] [The properties and predictions of quasi-periodic oscillations around a black hole in nonlocal gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25254)
*Tao-Tao Sui,Chen Long,Ye zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper explores the dynamics of massive test particles around a static black hole in nonlocal gravity, focusing on the impact of the nonlocal parameter $\alpha$ on the effective potential, energy, angular momentum, and high-frequency quasi-periodic oscillations (HF QPOs). The study finds that $\alpha$ systematically reduces the ISCO radius, energy, and angular momentum, while increasing the radiative efficiency. The Keplerian and vertical epicyclic frequencies are suppressed by $\alpha$, but the radial epicyclic frequency is enhanced. The resonance condition $2\nu_U = 3\nu_L$ is used to analyze the resonant radius, upper QPO frequency, and black hole mass, with the upper frequency constrained to $\nu_U \lesssim 1450$Hz, leading to a maximum black hole mass of $M \lesssim 43.6M_\odot$. The gravitational time delay, although increased, remains below $\sim 1.3$ms.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to investigate how the nonlocal parameter $\alpha$ affects the dynamics of massive test particles around a static black hole in the context of nonlocal gravity. This includes examining the properties of high-frequency quasi-periodic oscillations (HF QPOs) and constraining the nonlocal parameter based on the observed properties of these oscillations. The study aims to understand the impact of $\alpha$ on the effective potential, energy, angular momentum, and other relevant physical quantities, as well as to explore the implications for the black hole mass and the time delay between the shadow and QPO signals.

本文的动机是研究在非局域引力框架下，非局域参数$\alpha$如何影响静态黑洞周围大质量测试粒子的动力学。这包括检查高频准周期振荡（HF QPOs）的性质，并基于这些振荡的观测特性约束非局域参数。研究旨在理解$\alpha$对有效势能、能量、角动量及其他相关物理量的影响，以及对黑洞质量和阴影与QPO信号之间时间延迟的影响。

Method: The method employed in this paper involves the analysis of the dynamics of massive test particles around a static black hole in the context of nonlocal gravity. The authors calculate the effective potential $V_{eff}$, the energy $E$, and the angular momentum $L$ of circular orbits, and examine how these quantities change with the nonlocal parameter $\alpha$. They also investigate the influence of $\alpha$ on the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO) radius, the radiative efficiency, and the three epicyclic frequencies: the Keplerian frequency $\Omega_\phi$, the vertical epicyclic frequency $\Omega_\theta$, and the radial epicyclic frequency $\Omega_r$. Additionally, they analyze the effect of $\alpha$ on several twin-peak HF QPO models and use the $2\nu_U = 3\nu_L$ resonance condition to constrain the resonant radius, the upper QPO frequency, and the maximum allowed black hole mass. Finally, they consider the time delay between the shadow and QPO signals.

本文采用的方法是在非局域引力框架下分析静态黑洞周围大质量测试粒子的动力学。作者计算了圆轨道的有效势能$V_{eff}$、能量$E$和角动量$L$，并研究了这些量随非局域参数$\alpha$的变化。他们还研究了$\alpha$对最内稳定圆轨道（ISCO）半径、辐射效率以及三个进动频率：开普勒频率$\Omega_\phi$、垂直进动频率$\Omega_\theta$和径向进动频率$\Omega_r$的影响。此外，他们分析了$\alpha$对几种双峰HF QPO模型的影响，并使用$2\nu_U = 3\nu_L$共振条件来约束共振半径、上QPO频率和最大允许的黑洞质量。最后，他们考虑了阴影与QPO信号之间的时间延迟。

Result: The results of this paper show that the nonlocal parameter $\alpha$ significantly affects the dynamics of massive test particles around a static black hole. Specifically, $\alpha$ enhances the effective potential $V_{eff}$, leading to a reduction in the energy $E$ and angular momentum $L$ of circular orbits. The ISCO radius, along with the associated energy and angular momentum, decreases monotonically with $\alpha$, while the radiative efficiency increases, reaching a maximum of approximately $8.9\%$. The Keplerian and vertical epicyclic frequencies are suppressed by $\alpha$, whereas the radial epicyclic frequency is enhanced. The impact of $\alpha$ on HF QPO models is such that both the lower and upper bounds of the predicted QPO frequency ranges increase. By imposing the $2\nu_U = 3\nu_L$ resonance condition, the resonant radius is found to decrease with $\alpha$, while the upper QPO frequency increases, spanning the range $\nu_U \sim(673/M - 4360/M)$Hz. When the TOV limit is imposed, the upper frequency is further constrained to $\nu_U \lesssim 1450$Hz. The maximum allowed black hole mass is $M \lesssim 43.6M_\odot$. The gravitational time delay, although increased, remains below $\sim 1.3$ms.

本文的结果表明，非局域参数$\alpha$显著影响静态黑洞周围大质量测试粒子的动力学。具体来说，$\alpha$增强了有效势能$V_{eff}$，导致圆轨道的能量$E$和角动量$L$减少。最内稳定圆轨道（ISCO）半径及其相关的能量和角动量随着$\alpha$单调减少，而辐射效率增加，达到约$8.9\%$的最大值。开普勒频率和垂直进动频率被$\alpha$抑制，而径向进动频率增强。$\alpha$对HF QPO模型的影响使得预测的QPO频率范围的上下限都增加。通过施加$2\nu_U = 3\nu_L$共振条件，发现共振半径随$\alpha$减小，而上QPO频率增加，范围为$\nu_U \sim(673/M - 4360/M)$Hz。当施加TOV极限时，上频率进一步限制为$\nu_U \lesssim 1450$Hz。最大允许的黑洞质量为$M \lesssim 43.6M_\odot$。虽然引力时间延迟增加，但仍然低于$\sim 1.3$毫秒。

Conclusion: In conclusion, the nonlocal parameter $\alpha$ has a significant impact on the dynamics of massive test particles around a static black hole, affecting the effective potential, energy, angular momentum, and HF QPOs. The constraints on $\alpha$ and the black hole mass, as well as the upper QPO frequency, provide valuable insights into the nature of nonlocal gravity and its observational signatures. The study highlights the importance of considering nonlocal effects in the context of black hole physics and astrophysical observations.

总之，非局域参数$\alpha$对静态黑洞周围大质量测试粒子的动力学有显著影响，影响了有效势能、能量、角动量和HF QPOs。对$\alpha$和黑洞质量以及上QPO频率的约束提供了关于非局域引力本质及其观测特征的重要见解。研究表明，在黑洞物理学和天体物理观测中考虑非局域效应的重要性。

Abstract: We investigate the dynamics of massive test particles around a static black hole in nonlocal gravity and examine the corresponding properties of HF QPOs, constraining the nonlocal parameter to $α/M \leq 0.452$. The nonlocal parameter $α$ enhances the effective potential $V_{eff}$ and leads to a systematic reduction in the energy E and angular momentum L of circular orbits. Consequently, the ISCO radius, along with the associated energy and angular momentum, decreases monotonically with $α$, while the radiative efficiency increases, reaching a maximum of approximately $8.9\%$. Due to the spherical symmetry of the spacetime, the Keplerian frequency $Ω_φ$ and the vertical epicyclic frequency $Ω_θ$ coincide and are suppressed by $α$, whereas the radial epicyclic frequency $Ω_{r}$ is enhanced. The impact of $α$ on several twin-peak HF QPO models is examined, revealing that $α$ increases both the lower and upper bounds of the predicted QPO frequency ranges. By imposing the $2ν_U = 3ν_L$ resonance condition, we analyze the resonant radius, upper QPO frequency, maximum allowed black hole mass, and the time delay between the shadow and QPO signals. We find that the resonant radius decreases with $α$, while the upper QPO frequency increases, spanning the range $ν_U \sim(673/M-4360/M)$Hz. When the TOV imit is imposed, the upper frequency is further constrained to $ν_U \lesssim 1450$Hz. Combining astronomical observations for the classification of QPOs, where $ν_U \geq 100$Hz, the black hole mass in the nonlocal gravity should satisfy $M \lesssim 43.6M_\odot$. Although the radial separation between the resonant radius and the photon sphere decreases with $α$, the associated gravitational time delay increases, remaining below $\sim 1.3$ms and thus negligible for current observational capabilities.

### [71] [Dynamical analysis of the covariant $f(Q)$ gravity models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25412)
*S. A. Narawade,S. A. Kadam*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The study explores the cosmological evolution in $f(Q)$ gravity with a dynamically evolving coupling function. Two models, power-law and logarithmic, are analyzed through an autonomous dynamical system. The results show that both models can reproduce the cosmic evolution sequence and transitions, and the stability of critical points is examined using center manifold theory. Phase space trajectories and evolution plots for key cosmological parameters are presented, suggesting that these $f(Q)$ models offer a consistent description of cosmic evolution and late-time acceleration.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore the viability of $f(Q)$ gravity as a framework for understanding the cosmological evolution of the Universe, particularly focusing on whether it can consistently describe the different epochs of cosmic history, including the transitions between radiation, matter, and dark energy dominance, and the late-time acceleration of the Universe.

动机是探讨$f(Q)$引力作为理解宇宙演化框架的可行性，特别是关注它是否能够一致地描述宇宙历史的不同时期，包括辐射、物质和暗能量主导时期的过渡，以及宇宙晚期加速。

Method: The method involves formulating the cosmological field equations in the context of covariant $f(Q)$ gravity, where the coupling function evolves dynamically in proportion to the Hubble parameter. The field equations are then rewritten as an autonomous dynamical system, and the critical points of this system are determined and classified. The stability of these critical points is analyzed, and for non-hyperbolic points, center manifold theory is used. Additionally, phase space trajectories and evolution plots for key cosmological parameters (density parameters, EoS parameter, deceleration parameter) are provided for further analysis.

方法涉及在协变$f(Q)$引力的背景下建立宇宙场方程，其中耦合函数与哈勃参数成比例动态演化。然后将场方程重写为一个自治动力系统，并确定和分类该系统的临界点。分析这些临界点的稳定性，对于非双曲线点使用中心流形理论。此外，还提供了关键宇宙学参数（密度参数、EoS参数、减速参数）的相空间轨迹和演化图以供进一步分析。

Result: The results show that both the power-law and logarithmic forms of the $f(Q)$ function can reproduce the sequence of cosmic evolution, including the radiation, matter, and dark energy-dominated eras, along with the transitions between them. The physical properties at each critical point are described by key cosmological quantities such as the total EoS parameter, density parameters, and the deceleration parameter. The stability of the non-hyperbolic critical point is analyzed through center manifold theory. Phase space trajectories and evolution plots for the density parameters of radiation, matter, and dark energy, along with the EoS parameter for the total, are illustrated for further analysis.

结果表明，$f(Q)$函数的幂律形式和对数形式都能再现宇宙演化的序列，包括辐射、物质和暗能量主导时期及其之间的过渡。每个临界点的物理性质通过关键的宇宙学量来描述，如总EoS参数、密度参数和减速参数。通过中心流形理论分析了非双曲线临界点的稳定性。展示了辐射、物质和暗能量密度参数的相空间轨迹和演化图，以及总的EoS参数，以便进一步分析。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the $f(Q)$ gravity models, with a coupling function that evolves dynamically in proportion to the Hubble parameter, provide a consistent and viable description of the cosmic evolution. Both the power-law and logarithmic models are able to reproduce the sequence of cosmic epochs and the transitions between them, and they offer a promising approach to explaining the late-time acceleration of the Universe.

结论是，具有与哈勃参数成比例动态演化的耦合函数的$f(Q)$引力模型提供了一致且可行的宇宙演化描述。幂律模型和对数模型都能够再现宇宙时期的序列及其之间的过渡，并且它们为解释宇宙晚期加速提供了一个有前景的方法。

Abstract: In this study, we explore the cosmological evolution of the Universe in the framework of covariant $f(Q)$ gravity, with a coupling function that evolves dynamically in proportion to the Hubble parameter. Two specific forms of the function are examined: a power-law model and a logarithmic model. By rewriting the cosmological field equations as an autonomous dynamical system, we determine and classify the corresponding critical points and analyze their stability. Our results show that both models are able to reproduce the sequence of cosmic evolution, including radiation, matter, and dark energy-dominated eras, along with the transitions between them. The physical properties at each critical point are described using key cosmological quantities such as the total EoS parameter, density parameters, and the deceleration parameter. The stability of the non-hyperbolic critical point is analyzed through center manifold theory. In addition, we present phase space trajectories along with the stability behavior of each critical point. The evolution plots for the density parameters of radiation, matter, and dark energy, along with the EoS parameter for the total, are illustrated for further analysis. Overall, the analysis suggests that the $f(Q)$ models considered here, within the context of covariant formulation, provide a consistent description of cosmic evolution and offer a promising approach to explaining the late-time acceleration of the Universe.

Abstract: We study the quasinormal spectrum of a massive test scalar field in the exact asymptotically flat regular black-hole geometry supported by a phantom Dirac--Born--Infeld scalar. Using high-order WKB approximation improved by Padé resummation, together with characteristic time-domain integration and Prony extraction, we compute the fundamental mode and the first two overtones for representative values of the regularity parameter and the field mass. We show that increasing the field mass raises the oscillation frequency and reduces the damping rate, while increasing the regularity scale generally makes the ringing softer and longer lived. The time-domain profiles are in very good agreement with the WKB--Padé results and confirm the robustness of the spectrum. For sufficiently large field mass, the damping tends to zero, indicating the onset of quasiresonant behavior, although in the time domain these modes are eventually masked by oscillatory late-time tails. Our results show that massive scalar ringing provides a sensitive probe of this DBI-supported regular geometry.

The waveforms are compared to post-Newtonian expressions during the early inspiral, and quasi-normal mode frequencies are extracted from the remnants during the late ringdown. The study also examines the excitation of subdominant odd $m$-multipoles in the gravitational-wave emission and uses inspiral-merger-ringdown consistency tests to distinguish between boson-star and black-hole signals.

方法包括使用数值相对论模拟来建模等质量吸积玻色星双星的引力波信号。在早期吸积阶段，波形与后牛顿表达式进行比较；在晚期振铃阶段，从残余物中提取准正规模频率。研究还检查了引力波辐射中次主导奇数$m$多极矩的激发，并使用吸积-合并-振铃一致性测试来区分玻色星和黑洞信号。

Result: The results show that the largest deviations from comparable binary black-hole systems occur during the late inspiral and merger phases for boson-star binaries. For a subset of these binaries, the study identifies the excitation of subdominant odd $m$-multipoles in the gravitational-wave emission, which are absent in equal-mass nonspinning black-hole binaries. Despite these differences, some boson-star signals can still be degenerate with current waveform approximants, but inspiral-merger-ringdown consistency tests can help overcome these degeneracies.

结果表明，对于玻色星双星，在晚期吸积和合并阶段，与可比的黑洞双星系统相比，偏差最大。对于这些双星的一部分，研究发现引力波辐射中次主导奇数$m$多极矩的激发，而在等质量非旋转黑洞双星中不存在这种现象。尽管存在这些差异，某些玻色星信号仍然可能与当前波形近似值退化，但吸积-合并-振铃一致性测试可以帮助克服这些退化。

Conclusion: The study concludes that there are significant differences in the gravitational-wave signals between equal-mass inspiralling boson-star binaries and binary black-hole systems, particularly in the late inspiral and merger phases. The excitation of subdominant odd $m$-multipoles in the gravitational-wave emission is a unique feature of certain boson-star binaries. Inspiral-merger-ringdown consistency tests are effective in distinguishing between boson-star and black-hole signals, even when some boson-star signals are degenerate with current waveform approximants.

研究得出结论，等质量吸积玻色星双星与黑洞双星系统的引力波信号之间存在显著差异，特别是在晚期吸积和合并阶段。引力波辐射中次主导奇数$m$多极矩的激发是某些玻色星双星的独特特征。即使某些玻色星信号与当前波形近似值退化，吸积-合并-振铃一致性测试也能有效地区分玻色星和黑洞信号。

Abstract: We explore the gravitational-wave phenomenology of equal-mass inspiralling boson-star binaries using numerical relativity simulations. In particular, we characterise the waveform differences between binary boson-star and black-hole systems across (i) the early inspiral, by matching our waveforms to post-Newtonian expressions, (ii) merger, and (iii) late ringdown, by extracting the quasi-normal mode frequencies of the remnants. We find that boson-star binaries exhibit the largest deviations from comparable binary black-hole systems during the late inspiral and merger phases. Remarkably, for a subset of these equal-mass boson-star binaries (with certain phase offsets in the scalar-field profiles) we identify the excitation of subdominant odd $m$-multipoles in the gravitational-wave emission, absent in equal-mass nonspinning black-hole binaries. Despite differences in the phenomenology of binary boson-star and black-hole signals, injections of some boson-star signals into detector noise exhibit degeneracy with current waveform approximants. Building on these results, we demonstrate how inspiral-merger-ringdown consistency tests can overcome these degeneracies.

</details>


### [75] [Thermodynamic and Radiative Properties of Euler-Heisenberg AdS Black Holes Surrounded by Quintessence and Dark Matter with a Cloud of Strings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25629)
*Faizuddin Ahmed,Edilberto O. Silva*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper examines the thermodynamics, critical behavior, and radiative and optical properties of an Euler-Heisenberg AdS black hole surrounded by quintessence, dark matter, and a string cloud. The study shows that the Euler-Heisenberg coupling and surrounding matter fields significantly alter the temperature profile, stability, and critical point location. It also explores Hawking radiation, the photon sphere, black hole shadow, and geometric-optics emission rate.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand how the presence of Euler-Heisenberg electrodynamics, quintessence, perfect fluid dark matter, and a cloud of strings affect the thermodynamic, critical, and radiative properties of an AdS black hole. This is important for gaining insights into the interplay between quantum electrodynamics, dark energy, dark matter, and string theory in the context of black hole physics.

动机是理解Euler-Heisenberg电动力学、quintessence、完美流体暗物质和弦云的存在如何影响AdS黑洞的热力学、临界和辐射特性。这对于深入了解量子电动力学、暗能量、暗物质和弦理论在黑洞物理中的相互作用非常重要。

Method: The authors use the extended phase-space formalism to derive the thermodynamic quantities, verify the modified first law and Smarr relation, and analyze the equation of state and critical behavior. They also investigate the sparsity of Hawking radiation, the photon sphere, black hole shadow, and the geometric-optics emission rate.

作者使用扩展相空间形式来推导热力学量，验证修正的第一定律和Smarr关系，并分析状态方程和临界行为。他们还研究了Hawking辐射的稀疏性、光子球、黑洞阴影以及几何光学发射率。

Result: The results show that the Euler-Heisenberg coupling and the surrounding matter fields (quintessence, dark matter, and string cloud) significantly modify the temperature profile, stability structure, and the location of the critical point. Additionally, the presence of these fields affects the sparsity of Hawking radiation, the photon sphere, black hole shadow, and the geometric-optics emission rate.

结果表明，Euler-Heisenberg耦合和周围的物质场（quintessence、暗物质和弦云）显著改变了温度分布、稳定性结构和临界点的位置。此外，这些场的存在还影响了Hawking辐射的稀疏性、光子球、黑洞阴影以及几何光学发射率。

Conclusion: The study concludes that the inclusion of Euler-Heisenberg electrodynamics, quintessence, dark matter, and a string cloud in the AdS black hole spacetime leads to significant modifications in the thermodynamic, critical, and radiative properties. These findings provide new insights into the complex interactions between different types of matter and fields in the vicinity of black holes.

研究表明，在AdS黑洞时空中加入Euler-Heisenberg电动力学、quintessence、暗物质和弦云会导致热力学、临界和辐射特性的显著变化。这些发现为黑洞附近不同类型物质和场之间的复杂相互作用提供了新的见解。

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamics, criticality, and selected radiative and optical properties of an Euler-Heisenberg AdS black hole surrounded by quintessence, perfect fluid dark matter, and a cloud of strings. Within the extended phase-space formalism, we derive the thermodynamic quantities, verify the modified first law and Smarr relation, and analyze the corresponding equation of state and critical behavior. We show that the Euler--Heisenberg coupling and the surrounding matter fields substantially modify the temperature profile, the stability structure, and the location of the critical point. We also examine the sparsity of Hawking radiation, together with the photon sphere, black hole shadow, and the associated geometric-optics emission rate.

### [76] [Mean first passage time and the Kramers escape rate of phase transitions for the Bardeen-AdS-class black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25791)
*Chen Ma,Bin Wu,Zhen-Ming Xu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The study uses generalized free energy, Mean First-Passage Time, and Kramers escape rate to analyze the phase transitions of Bardeen-AdS-class black holes, which are categorized into two types with distinct phase transition behaviors.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand the phase transition landscape of Bardeen-AdS-class black holes, which exhibit different solutions and phase transition processes. The study aims to provide a comprehensive analysis using stochastic dynamics methods.

动机是理解Bardeen-AdS类黑洞的相变景观，这类黑洞表现出不同的解和相变过程。研究旨在使用随机动力学方法进行全面分析。

Method: The method involves the use of generalized free energy, Mean First-Passage Time (MFPT), and Kramers escape rate to characterize the phase transitions. The Bardeen-AdS-class black hole model is divided into two categories: Type I, which has a regular black hole solution, and Type II, which has a vacuum state solution. The phase transitions between small and large black holes for each type are analyzed in detail.

该方法涉及使用广义自由能、平均首次通过时间（MFPT）和Kramers逃逸率来表征相变。Bardeen-AdS类黑洞模型分为两类：I型具有常规黑洞解，II型具有真空态解。详细分析了每种类型的小黑洞和大黑洞之间的相变。

Result: For Type I black holes, the phase transition between small and large black holes can pass through a stable, metastable, or unstable regular black hole as an intermediate state. For Type II black holes, the phase transition occurs only between the vacuum state and the small black hole, without any regular black hole intermediate states.

对于I型黑洞，小黑洞和大黑洞之间的相变可以通过稳定的、亚稳态的或不稳定的常规黑洞作为中间状态。对于II型黑洞，相变仅发生在真空态和小黑洞之间，没有任何常规黑洞中间状态。

Conclusion: The study provides a detailed understanding of the phase transition landscape for Bardeen-AdS-class black holes, revealing the different pathways and intermediate states for Type I and Type II black holes. This analysis enhances our knowledge of the thermodynamic behavior of these black holes.

该研究提供了对Bardeen-AdS类黑洞相变景观的详细理解，揭示了I型和II型黑洞的不同路径和中间状态。这一分析增强了我们对这些黑洞热力学行为的认识。

Abstract: In this study, by utilizing the constructed generalized free energy alongside the Mean First-Passage Time and the Kramers escape rate from stochastic dynamics, we have obtained a comprehensive landscape of the phase transitions for the Bardeen-AdS-class black hole. This black hole model admits two distinct categories of solutions. Type I black holes feature a regular black hole solution, and Type II black holes possess a vacuum state solution. In the phase transition between the small black hole and the large black hole for Type I, the process may pass through a stable, metastable, or unstable regular black hole as an intermediate state. In contrast, for Type II black holes, the phase transition occurs exclusively between the vacuum state and the small black hole, and the transition process does not involve any regular black hole intermediate states.

### [77] [The Equivalence Principle and Kinematical Structure in the ADM Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25793)
*L. G. Pereira*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper develops a unified metric description of uniformly accelerated laboratories and those supported in a gravitational field using the ADM formulation, revealing that configurations with identical proper acceleration share an equivalent local shift structure. This clarifies the kinematical relation and apparent asymmetry between spatial displacement and energetic cost in these setups, while maintaining equivalence to standard General Relativity.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to provide a deeper understanding of the kinematical content of the Equivalence Principle beyond strictly local considerations, specifically by unifying the description of uniformly accelerated laboratories and those supported in a gravitational field. The goal is to clarify the subtle differences and similarities in their kinematical properties, such as spatial displacement and energetic cost, and to offer a more explicit and structured framework for these concepts within General Relativity.

动机是提供对等效原理的运动学内容的更深入理解，特别是通过统一描述均匀加速实验室和在引力场中支撑的实验室。目标是澄清这些设置中的运动学性质（如空间位移和能量成本）之间的细微差异和相似性，并在广义相对论中为这些概念提供一个更明确和结构化的框架。

Method: The method involves developing a unified metric description using the Arnowitt-Deser-Misner (ADM) formulation of General Relativity. The ADM shift vector is interpreted as a physical quantity encoding the kinematical relation between spatial slices and their temporal evolution. This approach allows for a common structural framework to describe both uniformly accelerated laboratories and those supported in a gravitational field, emphasizing the role of the ADM shift vector in characterizing the local kinematics of these configurations.

方法涉及使用Arnowitt-Deser-Misner (ADM) 形式的广义相对论来开发统一的度量描述。ADM位移向量被解释为编码空间切片及其时间演化之间运动学关系的物理量。这种方法允许在一个共同的结构框架内描述均匀加速实验室和在引力场中支撑的实验室，强调了ADM位移向量在表征这些构型的局部运动学中的作用。

Result: The result is a unified metric description that shows configurations experiencing identical proper acceleration share an equivalent local shift structure. This interpretation clarifies the kinematical relation and the apparent asymmetry between spatial displacement and energetic cost associated with accelerated motion and their absence in descriptions of observers supported in a gravitational field. The formulation remains fully equivalent to standard General Relativity at the level of the field equations and constraints.

结果是一个统一的度量描述，表明经历相同固有加速度的构型共享等效的局部位移结构。这种解释澄清了与加速运动相关的空间位移和能量成本之间的运动学关系及其明显的不对称性，以及在描述在引力场中支撑的观察者时这些现象的缺失。该表述在场方程和约束的层面上完全等同于标准广义相对论。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the ADM shift vector provides a clear and explicit way to understand the kinematical relation between uniformly accelerated laboratories and those supported in a gravitational field. This new perspective offers a relational account of gravitational time dilation and the emergence of observer-dependent horizons, while maintaining full equivalence with standard General Relativity. This work contributes to a deeper understanding of the Equivalence Principle and its implications for the kinematical properties of spacetime.

结论是，ADM位移向量提供了一种清晰且明确的方式来理解均匀加速实验室和在引力场中支撑的实验室之间的运动学关系。这种新视角提供了关于引力时间膨胀和观察者依赖视界的关联性解释，同时保持与标准广义相对论的完全等价。这项工作有助于更深入地理解等效原理及其对时空运动学性质的影响。

Abstract: The relation between uniformly accelerated laboratories and laboratories supported in a gravitational field lies at the conceptual core of the Equivalence Principle, yet its precise kinematical content beyond strictly local considerations remains subtle. In this work we develop a unified metric description of these configurations using the standard Arnowitt-Deser-Misner (ADM) formulation of General Relativity, which provides an explicit decomposition of spacetime into spatial hypersurfaces and their temporal evolution. In this setting the ADM shift vector is interpreted as a physical quantity encoding the kinematical relation between spatial slices and their temporal embedding associated with a chosen foliation. This interpretation allows uniformly accelerated laboratories and laboratories supported in a gravitational field to be described within a common structural framework, showing that configurations experiencing identical proper acceleration share an equivalent local shift structure. This viewpoint clarifies the apparent asymmetry between the spatial displacement and energetic cost associated with accelerated motion and their apparent absence in phenomenological descriptions of observers supported in a gravitational field. The formulation remains fully equivalent to standard General Relativity at the level of the field equations and constraints while making explicit kinematical features that are usually implicit in its geometric description. Consequences of this interpretation include a relational account of gravitational time dilation and the emergence of observer-dependent horizons.

### [78] [JWST Constraints on Primordial Magnetic Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24835)
*Malcolm Fairbairn,María Olalla Olea-Romacho,Juan Urrutia,Ville Vaskonen*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper investigates the impact of primordial magnetic fields (PMFs) on early structure formation and reionization, using the UV luminosity function (UVLF) to set stringent bounds. It finds that strong PMFs lead to a double reionization at $z \approx 24$, which is inconsistent with CMB measurements, leading to upper limits on PMF strength.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to explore how primordial magnetic fields (PMFs) influence the early universe's structure formation and reionization history. Specifically, it aims to use the ultraviolet luminosity function (UVLF) as a probe to constrain the strength of PMFs by comparing the predicted reionization history with cosmic microwave background (CMB) measurements of the optical depth, $\tau$.

本文的动机是探讨原初磁场（PMFs）如何影响早期宇宙的结构形成和再电离历史。具体来说，它旨在利用紫外线光度函数（UVLF）作为探针，通过将预测的再电离历史与宇宙微波背景（CMB）对光学深度 $\tau$ 的测量结果进行比较，来约束PMFs的强度。

Method: The method involves modeling the effect of PMFs on the small-scale structure formation through the Lorentz force acting on baryons. The authors use the UV luminosity function (UVLF) to calibrate the reionization history and compare it with the CMB measurements of the optical depth, $\tau$. By examining the compatibility of the predicted reionization history with the CMB data, they derive constraints on the strength of PMFs.

该方法涉及通过作用于重子上的洛伦兹力来模拟PMFs对小尺度结构形成的影响。作者使用紫外线光度函数（UVLF）来校准再电离历史，并将其与CMB对光学深度 $\tau$ 的测量结果进行比较。通过检查预测的再电离历史与CMB数据的一致性，他们推导出对PMFs强度的约束。

Result: The results show that strong PMFs lead to a characteristic double reionization at $z \approx 24$, which is incompatible with the CMB measurements of the optical depth. This incompatibility allows the authors to set upper limits on the strength of PMFs, yielding $\sqrt{\left\langle B^2 \right\rangle} < 0.27\,{\rm nG}$ for $n_B = -2$ and $< 0.18\,{\rm nG}$ for $n_B = 2$ at $95\%\,{\rm CL}$ using Planck priors on $\tau$.

结果显示，强PMFs在 $z \approx 24$ 时导致特征性的双重再电离，这与CMB对光学深度的测量不兼容。这种不兼容性使得作者能够设定PMFs强度的上限，在使用Planck对 $\tau$ 的先验条件下，对于 $n_B = -2$ 的情况，$\sqrt{\left\langle B^2 \right\rangle} < 0.27\,{\rm nG}$，而对于 $n_B = 2$ 的情况，$< 0.18\,{\rm nG}$，置信水平为 $95\%\,{\rm CL}$。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the reionization history, calibrated with the UV luminosity function (UVLF), provides stringent bounds on the strength of primordial magnetic fields (PMFs). The derived constraints establish early galaxy observables as among the most sensitive probes of PMFs in Gaussian, non-helical scenarios.

结论是，通过紫外线光度函数（UVLF）校准的再电离历史为原初磁场（PMFs）的强度提供了严格的约束。得出的约束条件确立了早期星系观测结果作为高斯、非螺旋场景下PMFs最敏感的探测手段之一。

Abstract: Primordial magnetic fields (PMFs) enhance small-scale structure formation through the Lorentz force acting on baryons, boosting the abundance of low-mass halos and their hosted galaxies. We show that the reionisation history calibrated with the UV luminosity function (UVLF) provides stringent bounds: strong PMFs induce a characteristic double reionisation at $z \approx 24$ that is incompatible with CMB measurements of the optical depth, yielding $\sqrt{\left\langle B^2 \right\rangle} < 0.27\,{\rm nG}$ and $< 0.18\,{\rm nG}$ for $n_B = -2$ and $n_B = 2$ respectively at $95\%\,{\rm CL}$ using Planck priors on $τ$. This establishes early galaxy observables as among the most sensitive probes of PMFs in Gaussian, non-helical scenarios.

</details>


### [79] [spectroxide: A code package for computing cosmic microwave background spectral distortions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24838)
*Ethan Baker,Hongwan Liu,Siddharth Mishra-Sharma*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper introduces spectroxide, a code package for computing cosmic microwave background (CMB) spectral distortions, developed with AI assistance and human supervision. The solver evolves the photon Boltzmann equation under various physical processes from high redshift to the present, and it is validated against analytic limits, published spectra, and precomputed Green's function tables. The development process is documented as a case study in AI-assisted scientific computing, with recommendations for best practices in human-AI collaboration.

本文介绍了spectroxide，这是一个用于计算宇宙微波背景（CMB）光谱畸变的代码包，由AI辅助和人类监督开发。求解器在各种物理过程下从高红移演化到当前，并通过解析极限、已发表的光谱和预计算的格林函数表进行验证。开发过程被记录为AI辅助科学计算的案例研究，并提供了人类与AI协作的最佳实践建议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation for this work is to develop an open-source code package for computing CMB spectral distortions, which is not currently available. The authors aim to provide a tool that can compute spectral distortions from arbitrary heat and photon injection within a specified redshift range, and to document the development process as a case study in AI-assisted scientific computing.

这项工作的动机是开发一个用于计算CMB光谱畸变的开源代码包，目前尚无此类工具。作者旨在提供一种工具，能够计算指定红移范围内任意热注入和光子注入产生的光谱畸变，并将开发过程记录为AI辅助科学计算的案例研究。

Method: The method involves the development of a code package named spectroxide, which uses the Rust programming language and a Python interface. The solver evolves the photon Boltzmann equation under Compton scattering, double Compton emission, and Bremsstrahlung from $z \sim 5 \times 10^6$ to the present. The code was written by an AI assistant (Claude Code) under the supervision of human physicists, and it includes ${\sim}400$ automated tests to ensure correctness. The validation of the code is done against analytic limits, published spectra, and precomputed Green's function tables.

该方法涉及开发一个名为spectroxide的代码包，使用Rust编程语言和Python接口。求解器在康普顿散射、双康普顿发射和轫致辐射下从$z \sim 5 \times 10^6$演化到当前。代码由AI助手（Claude Code）在人类物理学家的监督下编写，并包括${\sim}400$个自动化测试以确保正确性。代码的验证通过解析极限、已发表的光谱和预计算的格林函数表进行。

Result: The result is a fully functional and validated code package, spectroxide, which can compute CMB spectral distortions from arbitrary heat and photon injection within the specified redshift range. The code has been tested against analytic limits, published spectra, and precomputed Green's function tables, and it is publicly available on GitHub. The development process also provides insights into the challenges and best practices of AI-assisted scientific software development.

结果是一个完全功能性和经过验证的代码包spectroxide，它可以计算指定红移范围内任意热注入和光子注入产生的CMB光谱畸变。该代码已经通过解析极限、已发表的光谱和预计算的格林函数表进行了测试，并且在GitHub上公开可用。开发过程还提供了关于AI辅助科学软件开发的挑战和最佳实践的见解。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that spectroxide, developed with AI assistance and human supervision, is a valuable and reliable tool for computing CMB spectral distortions. The case study highlights the importance of domain expertise in catching physics bugs and the need for robust testing in AI-assisted scientific computing. The authors recommend best practices for human-AI collaborative development of scientific software, including the use of automated tests and continuous human oversight.

结论是，在AI辅助和人类监督下开发的spectroxide是一个有价值的可靠工具，用于计算CMB光谱畸变。案例研究表明了领域专业知识在捕捉物理错误中的重要性以及在AI辅助科学计算中进行稳健测试的必要性。作者推荐了人类与AI协作开发科学软件的最佳实践，包括使用自动化测试和持续的人类监督。

Abstract: We present spectroxide, a code package for computing cosmic microwave background spectral distortions in which all ${\sim}14{,}500$ lines of Rust code, Python interface, and ${\sim}400$ automated tests were written by an AI assistant (Claude Code) under human physicist supervision. The solver evolves the photon Boltzmann equation under Compton scattering, double Compton emission, and Bremsstrahlung from $z \sim 5 \times 10^6$ to the present, computing spectral distortions from arbitrary heat and photon injection within this redshift range. No fully open-source code of this kind is publicly available; we validate against analytic limits, published spectra, and publicly available precomputed Green's function tables. We document the development as a case study in AI-assisted scientific computing, highlighting how domain expertise caught physics bugs (incorrect dimensional prefactors, near-cancellation errors) that evaded the full automated test suite, and provide recommendations for best practices in human--AI collaborative development of scientific software. We make spectroxide publicly available on GitHub.

</details>


### [80] [Cosmic gas accretion from filaments onto galaxy clusters using the IllustrisTNG simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24852)
*Jade Pasté,Céline Gouin,Nabila Aghanim,Jenny G. Sorce*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This study analyzes 415 galaxy clusters from the IllustrisTNG-300 hydrodynamical simulation at $z=0$ to characterize gas accretion onto clusters, focusing on the role of filaments in driving anisotropic inflows and thermodynamic properties. The results highlight two distinct regimes of gas accretion depending on the cluster-centric distances, with fast infalling warm gas entering the warm-hot circumcluster medium in the cluster environment, and gas infalling along filaments into the hot intracluster medium at the cluster outskirts. The mass and dynamical state of clusters significantly impact these accretion features.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand the role of filaments in the anisotropic gas accretion onto galaxy clusters, as it remains a key challenge for cosmology. By characterizing the thermodynamic properties and the anisotropic signatures of gas accretion, the study aims to provide insights into the growth of galaxy clusters through matter accretion from the cosmic web.

Method: The study analyzed 415 galaxy clusters from the IllustrisTNG-300 hydrodynamical simulation at $z=0$. Anisotropic signatures were probed by examining both isotropically and anisotropically (gas in filaments only) the radial profiles of gas properties (temperature, entropy, density, and pressure) and the radial velocity distributions. The analysis was performed at different cluster-centric distances to highlight the distinct regimes of gas accretion.

Result: The results show two distinct regimes of gas accretion: In the cluster environment ($\sim$ 2-4$R_{200}$), fast infalling warm gas enters the warm-hot circumcluster medium, while filaments remain colder due to slow thermalization. At the cluster outskirts ($\sim$ 1-2$R_{200}$), gas infalling along filaments enters the hot intracluster medium, with a strong tangential velocity gradient. Relaxed and massive clusters exhibit stronger and more extended temperature discontinuities. There is no strong evidence of accretion shocks around filaments, suggesting slow thermalization of filament gas as it enters the dense warm-hot circum-cluster environment.

Conclusion: The study provides a coherent picture of anisotropic gas accretion from filaments onto galaxy clusters, emphasizing the importance of the cluster's mass and dynamical state in shaping the accretion features. While virial shocks are observed near the cluster boundary, especially at the filament-cluster interface, the absence of strong accretion shocks around filaments indicates that filament gas thermalizes slowly as it enters the dense warm-hot circum-cluster environment.

Abstract: Galaxy clusters grow through the matter accretion from the cosmic web, mainly along filaments. We aim to characterize the gas accretion onto clusters, focusing on the role of filaments in driving anisotropic inflows and thermodynamic properties, as it remains a key challenge for cosmology. In this study, we analyzed 415 galaxy clusters from the IllustrisTNG-300 hydrodynamical simulation at $z=0$. Anisotropic signatures are highlighted by probing both isotropically and anisotropically (gas in filaments only), the radial profiles of gas properties (including temperature, entropy, density, and pressure), and the radial velocity distributions. Our results highlight two distinct regimes of gas accretion depending on the cluster-centric distances. In the cluster environment ($\sim$ 2-4$R_{200}$), fast infalling warm gas tunneled by cosmic filaments enters the warm-hot circumcluster medium, but filaments remain colder due to their slow thermalization with the surrounding, generating transverse temperature gradients. At the cluster outskirts ($\sim$ 1-2$R_{200}$), gas infalling along filaments enters the hot intracluster medium, with a strong tangential velocity gradient. Warm gas tends to penetrate clusters from filaments, while hot gas is preferentially ejected beyond them. The mass and dynamical state of clusters significantly impact these accretion features, with relaxed and massive clusters exhibiting stronger and more extended temperature discontinuities. Overall, this work emphasizes a coherent picture of anisotropic gas accretion from filaments onto clusters. While virial shocks tend to be observed near the cluster boundary, especially at the filament-cluster interface. We do not find strong evidence of accretion shocks around filaments, suggesting slow thermalization of filament gas as it enters the dense warm-hot circum-cluster environment.

</details>


### [81] [Bound or blown: the fate of hot gas in galaxy groups](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24863)
*R. Seppi,D. Eckert,J. Schaye,J. Braspenning,M. Schaller,B. D. Oppenheimer,E. O'Sullivan,F. Gastaldello,L. Lovisari,M. A. Bourne,M. Sun,A. Finoguenov,H. Khalil,G. Gozaliasl,K. Kolokythas,Y. E. Bahar,R. Santra*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The study compares XMM-Newton Group AGN Project (X-GAP) data with hydrodynamical FLAMINGO simulations to understand the impact of AGN feedback on the hot gas content of galaxy groups. By forward-modelling and generating mock observations, it finds that models with intermediate feedback strength best match the X-GAP data, indicating a preference for stronger feedback than the fiducial FLAMINGO calibration but disfavoring the most extreme ejective models.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to resolve the uncertainty in the effect of AGN feedback on the hot gas content of galaxy groups, which is crucial for understanding galaxy formation and its connection to the large-scale structure of the Universe. The study aims to compare observational data from the X-GAP project with hydrodynamical simulations (FLAMINGO) that include a range of AGN feedback prescriptions, to identify the model that best reproduces the observed properties of galaxy groups.

动机是解决AGN反馈对星系团热气体含量影响的不确定性，这对于理解星系形成及其与宇宙大尺度结构的联系至关重要。研究旨在将X-GAP项目的观测数据与包括一系列AGN反馈处方的流体动力学模拟（FLAMINGO）进行比较，以确定最能再现星系团观测特性的模型。

Method: The method involves constructing X-GAP analogues by forward-modelling the full selection function, including detection and observational systematics, and generating end-to-end XMM-Newton mock observations. These mock observations are then analyzed consistently with the real data. Multiple observables such as the L--T and Mgas--T relations, number of groups, mean temperature, and velocity dispersion are studied, accounting for their covariance. The forward model accurately recovers input luminosities, gas masses, and core-excised temperatures for regular systems, enabling direct comparison in observable space.

方法包括通过前向建模整个选择函数（包括检测和观测系统性误差）来构建X-GAP类似物，并生成端到端的XMM-Newton模拟观测。然后这些模拟观测与真实数据一致地进行分析。研究了多个可观测量，如L-T和Mgas-T关系、群组数量、平均温度和速度弥散，并考虑了它们的协方差。前向模型能够准确恢复规则系统的输入光度、气体质量和去核温度，从而能够在可观测空间中直接进行比较。

Result: The results show that the normalization of the scaling relations is the best discriminator between feedback models. Models with intermediate feedback strength provide the best agreement with X-GAP data, with the fgas-2sigma model yielding the lowest tension of only 0.8sigma. The most extreme feedback scenario (fgas-8sigma) is ruled out at > 4sigma. Cosmic variance introduces significant fluctuations (> 20%) in the number of detected systems, making counts alone a weak discriminator.

结果显示，比例关系的归一化是区分反馈模型的最佳判据。具有中等反馈强度的模型与X-GAP数据最为吻合，其中fgas-2sigma模型产生的张力最小，仅为0.8sigma。最极端的反馈情景（fgas-8sigma）在大于4sigma的情况下被排除。宇宙方差在检测到的系统数量上引入显著波动（> 20%），使得仅凭计数成为弱判据。

Conclusion: The thermodynamic properties of galaxy groups favor feedback stronger than the fiducial FLAMINGO calibration, but disfavor the most ejective models. This highlights the importance of combining forward modelling and multi-observable constraints to probe the fate of hot baryons in low-mass haloes.

星系团的热力学性质倾向于比FLAMINGO基准校准更强的反馈，但不支持最具喷射性的模型。这强调了结合前向建模和多可观测量约束来探测低质量晕中热重子命运的重要性。

Abstract: The impact of AGN feedback on the hot gas content of galaxy groups remains a key uncertainty in galaxy formation and its connection to the large scale structure of the Universe. We aim to compare the XMM-Newton Group AGN Project (X-GAP) sample to the hydrodynamical FLAMINGO simulations, which span a wide range of AGN feedback prescriptions. We construct X-GAP analogues by forward-modelling the full selection function, including detection and observational systematics, and generate end-to-end XMM-Newton mock observations analysed consistently with the data. We study multiple observables, including the L--T and Mgas--T relations, number of groups, mean temperature, and velocity dispersion, accounting for their covariance. The forward model accurately recovers input luminosities, gas masses, and core-excised temperatures for regular systems, enabling direct comparison in observable space. The normalisation of the scaling relations is the best discriminator between feedback models, while cosmic variance introduces > 20% fluctuations in the number of detected systems, making counts alone a weak discriminator. Models with intermediate feedback strength provide the best agreement with X-GAP, with the fgas-2sigma model yielding the lowest tension of only 0.8sigma, while the most extreme feedback scenario (fgas-8sigma) is ruled out at > 4sigma. Our results indicate that the thermodynamic properties of galaxy groups favour feedback stronger than the fiducial FLAMINGO calibration, but disfavour the most ejective models. This highlights the importance of combining forward modelling and multi-observable constraints to probe the fate of hot baryons in low-mass haloes.

### [82] [TDCOSMO XXVI: Uniform lens modeling of eight doubly imaged quasars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24908)
*Ryan Brady,Xiang-Yu Huang,Simon Birrer,Anowar J. Shajib,Nafis Sadik Nihal,Cameron Lemon,Martin Millon,Veronica Motta,Dominique Sluse,Frederic Courbin*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper presents a uniform gravitational lens modeling analysis of eight doubly imaged quasars using the Lenstronomy framework. The study establishes a strong correlation between Fermat potential precision and the surface brightness of the spatially extended host arcs, indicating that arc surface brightness is crucial for mass model precision in doubly imaged systems. The results will accelerate the construction of time-delay cosmography samples from future large lens populations.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation for this paper is to address the underutilization of doubly imaged quasars in time-delay cosmography. While quadruply imaged quasars have been primarily used, doubly imaged systems are more abundant but present fewer geometric constraints. The goal is to develop a uniform pipeline for analyzing these systems and to quantify the information contributed by the lensed arcs, which is essential for improving the precision of mass models and future cosmographic analyses.

Method: The authors use the open-source \texttt{Lenstronomy} framework to reconstruct the lensing systems with a pipeline specifically tailored for doubly imaged quasars. They compare their modeled Einstein radii and image separations to previous literature and Gaia DR2 measurements, respectively. To further quantify the contribution of the lensed arcs, they perform a conjugate point analysis using only the quasar image positions to constrain the lens mass profiles, and compare the resulting posteriors to those from full image modeling.

Result: The modeled Einstein radii agree with the literature at an average of 1.5$\sigma$, and the modeled image separations differ from Gaia DR2 measurements with an r.m.s. of only 3.6 mas. A strong correlation is found between Fermat potential precision and the surface brightness of the spatially extended host arcs, indicating that arc surface brightness is the primary driver of mass model precision in doubly imaged systems. The conjugate point analysis shows substantially broader posteriors compared to full image modeling, confirming that arc brightness determines the degree to which the lens mass profile can be constrained.

Conclusion: The uniform pipeline and the established trends in arc surface brightness will significantly accelerate the construction of time-delay cosmography samples from the large lens populations expected from future surveys like LSST, Roman, and Euclid. The results highlight the importance of arc surface brightness in improving the precision of mass models and the overall accuracy of cosmographic analyses.

Abstract: We present the first uniform gravitational lens modeling analysis of eight doubly imaged quasars from multi-band observations with the Hubble Space Telescope. Previous time-delay cosmography analyses by the TDCOSMO Collaboration have primarily relied on quadruply imaged quasars, while doubly imaged systems, despite being more abundant, remain underutilized due to their fewer geometric constraints. Using an open-source $\texttt{Lenstronomy}$ framework, we reconstruct the lensing systems with a pipeline tailored for doubles. Comparing our results to the literature, the modeled Einstein radii agree at an average of 1.5$σ$, which is expected given data and modeling heterogeneity, while modeled image separations differ from Gaia DR2 measurements with an r.m.s of only 3.6 mas. We find a strong correlation between Fermat potential precision and the surface brightness of the spatially extended host arcs, establishing that arc surface brightness is the primary driver of mass model precision in doubly imaged systems. To further quantify the information contributed by the lensed arcs, we performed a conjugate point analysis that uses only the quasar image positions to constrain the lens mass profiles. The resulting posteriors are substantially broader than those from full image modeling, and a strong anti-correlation between mass parameter hypervolume and arc magnitude additionally confirms that arc brightness determines the degree to which the lens mass profile can be constrained in doubles. A hierarchical cosmographic analysis incorporating time-delay measurements and stellar kinematics to infer $\text{H}_0$ will be presented in a subsequent publication. The uniform pipeline and arc surface brightness trends established here will significantly accelerate the construction of time-delay cosmography samples from the large lens populations expected from LSST, Roman, and Euclid.

### [83] [Variance-aware model discrimination with the Sunyaev-Zel'dovich effect of the 21 cm background (SZE-21cm)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24980)
*Charles Mpho Takalana*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper explores the use of the Sunyaev-Zel'dovich effect of the 21 cm background (SZE-21cm) to distinguish between different Cosmic Dawn scenarios. The authors use semi-numerical simulations and a relativistic scattering kernel, varying parameters such as star-formation efficiency, X-ray spectral hardness, heating timing, and low-mass source suppression. They quantify separability using feature-based summaries, standardized residual spectra, and a band-integrated pairwise separability index. The results indicate that variations in heating timing produce the strongest separations, while X-ray hardness variations are nearly degenerate with the fiducial case.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to explore an alternative method for probing the early universe, specifically the Cosmic Dawn, by using the SZE-21cm. Direct measurement of the sky-averaged redshifted 21 cm signal remains challenging, and the SZE-21cm offers a complementary approach. This method involves the Comptonisation of the 21 cm background by hot electrons in galaxy clusters, which can be observed as a spectral distortion. The goal is to determine how well the SZE-21cm can differentiate between various astrophysical scenarios during the Cosmic Dawn.

本文的动机是探索一种替代方法来探测早期宇宙，特别是宇宙黎明时期，通过使用21厘米背景的Sunyaev-Zel'dovich效应（SZE-21cm）。直接测量红移后的21厘米信号仍然具有挑战性，而SZE-21cm提供了一种互补的方法。这种方法涉及星系团中的热电子对21厘米背景的康普顿散射，可以观察到光谱畸变。目标是确定SZE-21cm在区分宇宙黎明期间的各种天体物理场景方面的效果如何。

Method: The authors use semi-numerical simulations of the global 21 cm background, combined with a relativistic scattering kernel based on the Maxwell-Juttner electron distribution, to model the SZE-21cm. They vary several key parameters, including star-formation efficiency, X-ray spectral hardness, heating timing, and the suppression of low-mass sources. The SZE-21cm spectra are computed over the frequency range of 45-200 MHz. To quantify the separability of different Cosmic Dawn scenarios, they employ feature-based summaries, standardized residual spectra, and a band-integrated pairwise separability index. The latter combines seed-to-seed scatter with an astrophysical variance layer derived from coeval ON-aperture / OFF-annulus statistics.

作者使用半数值模拟全局21厘米背景，并结合基于Maxwell-Juttner电子分布的相对论散射核来建模SZE-21cm。他们改变了几个关键参数，包括恒星形成效率、X射线谱硬度、加热时间以及低质量源的抑制。SZE-21cm光谱在45-200 MHz的频率范围内计算。为了量化不同宇宙黎明情景的可分离性，他们采用了基于特征的摘要、标准化残差光谱和带积分成对可分离性指数。后者结合了从种子到种子的散射和从共时ON孔径/OFF环统计中得出的天体物理方差层。

Result: The results show that variations in heating timing produce the strongest separations between different Cosmic Dawn scenarios. In contrast, the variations in X-ray spectral hardness explored in the study are nearly degenerate with the fiducial case once the ON-OFF variance is included. The authors also propagate an EDGES-like benchmark curve as a morphological stress test of the framework, not as a physically validated model, to illustrate how anomalous global-signal morphologies would map into the SZE-21cm.

结果表明，加热时间的变化在不同的宇宙黎明情景之间产生了最强的分离。相比之下，研究中探讨的X射线谱硬度变化在包含ON-OFF方差后几乎与基准情况退化。作者还传播了一个类似EDGES的基准曲线，作为框架的形态应力测试，而不是作为一个物理验证模型，以说明异常的全局信号形态如何映射到SZE-21cm中。

Conclusion: The SZE-21cm provides a promising complementary method for distinguishing between different Cosmic Dawn scenarios. Variations in heating timing are particularly effective in producing separable signals, while X-ray spectral hardness variations are less distinct. The framework developed in this study can be used to further investigate the potential of the SZE-21cm in probing the early universe.

SZE-21cm为区分不同的宇宙黎明情景提供了一种有前景的互补方法。加热时间的变化在产生可分离信号方面特别有效，而X射线谱硬度的变化则不那么明显。本研究中开发的框架可用于进一步研究SZE-21cm在探测早期宇宙方面的潜力。

Abstract: The sky-averaged redshifted 21 cm signal from Cosmic Dawn is a uniquely sensitive tracer of early heating and ionisation, but it remains challenging to measure directly. The Sunyaev-Zel'dovich effect of the 21 cm background (SZE-21cm) provides a complementary route: Comptonisation of the incident low-frequency background by hot electrons in galaxy clusters produces a spectral distortion that can be recovered as a difference between the line of sight through a galaxy cluster and a nearby blank-sky reference, and is therefore naturally compatible with interferometric observations. We use semi-numerical simulations of the global 21 cm background, together with a relativistic scattering kernel built from the Maxwell-Juttner electron distribution, to assess how well the SZE-21cm separates physically distinct Cosmic Dawn scenarios. The model suite varies star-formation efficiency, X-ray spectral hardness, heating timing, and the suppression of low-mass sources; SZE-21cm spectra are computed over 45-200 MHz. Separability is quantified through feature-based summaries, standardised residual spectra, and a band-integrated pairwise separability index that combines seed-to-seed scatter with an astrophysical variance layer derived from coeval ON-aperture / OFF-annulus statistics. The resulting indices are intrinsic and instrument-free, and therefore upper bounds on what a real experiment with finite thermal noise can achieve. Heating-timing variations produce the strongest separations, while the X-ray hardness variations explored here are nearly degenerate with the fiducial case once the ON-OFF variance is included. We also propagate an EDGES-like benchmark curve as a morphological stress test of the framework, not as a physically validated model, illustrating how anomalous global-signal morphologies would map into the SZE-21cm.

</details>


### [84] [Multi-tracers, multi-surveys: data-driven EFT prior calibration from the PFS--DESI overlap](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25171)
*Nhat-Minh Nguyen*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper proposes a data-driven method, multi-survey priors, to calibrate EFT parameters from overlapping spectroscopic surveys, improving constraints on cosmological parameters like $f\sigma_8$ and $M_\nu$. This method provides a model-independent alternative to simulation-based priors and enhances the precision of full-shape galaxy power spectrum analyses. 

该论文提出了一种数据驱动的方法，即多调查先验，通过重叠的光谱巡天来校准EFT参数，从而改进对宇宙学参数（如$f\sigma_8$和$M_\nu$）的约束。这种方法为基于模拟的先验提供了模型独立的替代方案，并提高了全形状星系功率谱分析的精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The primary motivation is to reduce the systematic cost associated with marginalizing over a large number of EFT nuisance parameters in full-shape galaxy power spectrum analyses. The authors aim to provide a more efficient and model-independent approach to calibrating these parameters, as an alternative to the existing simulation-based priors (SBP) that rely on N-body simulations and HOD models. 

主要动机是减少在全形状星系功率谱分析中边缘化大量EFT讨厌参数所带来的系统性成本。作者旨在提供一种更高效且模型独立的方法来校准这些参数，作为依赖于N体模拟和HOD模型的现有基于模拟的先验（SBP）的替代方法。

Method: The authors introduce a novel, data-driven technique called multi-survey priors, which uses the multi-tracer analysis of overlapping spectroscopic surveys to calibrate EFT parameters. This method leverages cross-spectra between different galaxy populations in the PFS-DESI overlap region, which eliminates stochastic contributions and separates shot noise from the signal. The calibrated priors are then applied to the larger DESI footprint, enhancing the precision of cosmological parameter measurements. 

作者介绍了一种新的数据驱动技术，称为多调查先验，它利用重叠光谱巡天的多示踪分析来校准EFT参数。该方法利用PFS-DESI重叠区域中不同星系群体之间的交叉功率谱，消除了随机贡献并区分了散粒噪声和信号。然后将校准后的先验应用于更大的DESI足迹，从而提高宇宙学参数测量的精度。

Result: The application of multi-survey priors in the PFS-DESI overlap region leads to significant improvements in the precision of $f\sigma_8$ and $M_\nu$ measurements. Specifically, the precision of $f\sigma_8$ is improved by 8% (7-25% per sample), and the precision of $M_\nu$ is improved by 54% (46-71% per sample) at $k_{\rm max}=0.20\,h\,\mathrm{Mpc}^{-1}$. The dominant driver of these gains is the calibration of the $b_1\sigma_8$ prior, which breaks the degeneracy between $b_1\sigma_8$ and $f\sigma_8$. 

在PFS-DESI重叠区域应用多调查先验显著提高了$f\sigma_8$和$M_\nu$测量的精度。具体来说，在$k_{\rm max}=0.20\,h\,\mathrm{Mpc}^{-1}$时，$f\sigma_8$的精度提高了8%（每个样本7-25%），$M_\nu$的精度提高了54%（每个样本46-71%）。这些增益的主要驱动力是$b_1\sigma_8$先验的校准，这打破了$b_1\sigma_8$和$f\sigma_8$之间的简并。

Conclusion: The multi-survey priors method provides a powerful, model-independent approach to calibrating EFT parameters, significantly improving the precision of cosmological parameter measurements. This method not only serves as a consistency check for the assumptions made in the SBP approach but also generalizes to any combination of overlapping spectroscopic surveys. 

多调查先验方法提供了一种强大的、模型独立的方法来校准EFT参数，显著提高了宇宙学参数测量的精度。该方法不仅作为对SBP方法假设的一致性检查，而且可以推广到任何重叠光谱巡天的组合。

Abstract: Marginalizing over roughly 12 effective-field-theory (EFT) nuisance parameters per tracer per redshift bin is the dominant systematic cost in full-shape galaxy power spectrum analyses. Simulation-based priors (SBP) can tighten these parameters but rely on N-body simulations and halo-occupation-distribution (HOD) models. We propose multi-survey priors: a data-driven alternative that calibrates EFT parameters from the multi-tracer analysis of overlapping spectroscopic surveys. In the $\sim\!1{,}200\;\text{deg}^2$ Prime Focus Spectrograph (PFS)--Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument (DESI) overlap at $0.6<z<1.6$, up to 4 tracers (PFS-ELG, DESI-ELG, DESI-LRG, DESI-QSO) and 10 cross-spectra per redshift bin provide model-independent constraints on the DESI nuisance parameters. Cross-spectra between different galaxy populations carry zero stochastic contribution, cleanly separating shot noise from signal. Exporting the calibrated priors to the full $14{,}000\;\text{deg}^2$ DESI footprint of the DESI LRG1--3, ELG1--2 and QSO samples improves $σ(fσ_8)$ by 8\% (7--25\% per sample) and $σ(M_ν)$ by 54\% (46--71\% per sample) at $k_{\rm max}=0.20\,h\,\mathrm{Mpc}^{-1}$. A parameter importance decomposition reveals that the dominant driver is the calibration of the $b_1σ_8$ prior -- constrained from a flat prior to $σ\approx 0.17$ by the multi-tracer Fisher -- which accounts for $\sim\!70\%$ of the $fσ_8$ gain and $\sim\!97\%$ of the $M_ν$ gain by breaking the $b_1σ_8$--$fσ_8$ degeneracy intrinsic to single-tracer analyses. Multi-survey prior calibration parallels the SBP approach, which tightens $b_1$ through HOD model assumptions; multi-survey priors provide a model-independent consistency check on these assumptions and generalize to arbitrary combinations of overlapping spectroscopic surveys.

### [85] [Recovering cosmological parameters from the mock gravitational wave data of the Einstein Telescope](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25307)
*Pinaki Roy,Tomasz Bulik*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper discusses the potential of the Einstein Telescope (ET) for cosmography, specifically in constraining the Hubble constant ($H_0$) and the matter density parameter ($\Omega_{\rm m}$) using the intrinsic chirp mass spectrum of black hole binaries. It demonstrates that at least one year of ET's observation can achieve 1% uncertainty in $H_0$ and 4% uncertainty in $\Omega_{\rm m}$.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore the capability of the Einstein Telescope, a third-generation gravitational wave (GW) detector, in performing precise measurements of cosmological parameters such as the Hubble constant and the matter density parameter. The increased sensitivity of ET allows for the detection of stellar mass binary black hole mergers up to a redshift of 10, making it a powerful tool for cosmography. 

动机是探索第三代引力波探测器——爱因斯坦望远镜（ET）在精确测量宇宙学参数方面的能力，例如哈勃常数和物质密度参数。ET 的灵敏度提高使其能够探测到红移高达10的恒星质量双黑洞合并事件，这使其成为宇宙绘图的强大工具。

Method: A mock gravitational wave event catalog for the Einstein Telescope is generated, and a simple, effective, and fast technique is presented for inferring $H_0$ or $\Omega_{\rm m}$ using the intrinsic chirp mass spectrum of black hole binaries. The method assumes the standard model of cosmology and evaluates the efficacy of the technique by estimating the uncertainties in the recovered cosmological parameters.

为爱因斯坦望远镜生成了一个模拟引力波事件目录，并提出了一种简单、有效且快速的技术，利用黑洞双星的固有啁啾质量谱来推断$H_0$或$\Omega_{\rm m}$。该方法假设了标准宇宙模型，并通过估计恢复的宇宙学参数的不确定性来评估技术的有效性。

Result: The results show that at least one year of observation with the Einstein Telescope is required to constrain $H_0$ to within 1% uncertainty and $\Omega_{\rm m}$ to within 4% uncertainty. This indicates that the Einstein Telescope, operating as a standalone instrument, can effectively use GW spectral sirens to constrain the Hubble constant and the matter density parameter.

结果表明，至少需要一年的爱因斯坦望远镜观测才能将$H_0$约束在1%的不确定度内，将$\Omega_{\rm m}$约束在4%的不确定度内。这表明作为独立仪器运行的爱因斯坦望远镜可以有效地使用引力波频谱警报来约束哈勃常数和物质密度参数。

Conclusion: The Einstein Telescope has the potential to significantly improve our understanding of cosmological parameters through the detection and analysis of gravitational waves from binary black hole mergers. By employing the intrinsic chirp mass spectrum of these events, the ET can provide robust constraints on $H_0$ and $\Omega_{\rm m}$, contributing to the field of cosmography.

爱因斯坦望远镜通过检测和分析双黑洞合并产生的引力波，有望显著提高我们对宇宙学参数的理解。通过利用这些事件的固有啁啾质量谱，ET 可以对$H_0$和$\Omega_{\rm m}$提供可靠的约束，从而为宇宙绘图领域做出贡献。

Abstract: Einstein Telescope (ET) is a third-generation gravitational wave (GW) detector with tenfold better sensitivity compared to the advanced LIGO detectors. It will be capable of observing copious stellar mass binary black hole mergers upto a redshift of 10 which will make it especially useful for cosmography. We generate a mock gravitational wave event catalog for the Einstein Telescope and show the recoverability of either the Hubble constant ($H_0$) or the matter density parameter ($Ω_{\rm m}$). We present a simple, effective and fast technique for inferring $H_0$ (or $Ω_{\rm m}$) using the intrinsic chirp mass spectrum of black hole binaries, and investigate the efficacy of the method assuming the standard model of cosmology. If only $H_0$ has to be constrained, we find that at least one year of ET's observation will be required to achieve 1% uncertainty. With the same amount of observation, $Ω_{\rm m}$ can be constrained to within 4\% uncertainty. With ET operating as a standalone instrument, we show that the GW spectral sirens detected by it can constrain the Hubble constant.

### [86] [Generalizing the CPL Parametrization through Dark Sector Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25373)
*Mikel Artola,Ruth Lazkoz,Vincenzo Salzano*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper investigates interacting dark energy (IDE) models with a non-gravitational coupling between dark matter and dark energy, using the CPL parametrization for the dark energy equation of state. Analytical expressions for the energy densities are derived, and observational constraints are obtained using DESI DR2 BAO, Pantheon+ SNe Ia, and Planck+ACT CMB data. The results show that while constant coupling models have some deviations from $\Lambda$CDM, no IDE model is statistically preferred over $\Lambda$CDM. Bayesian evidence is emphasized for robust cosmological claims.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore the possibility of a non-gravitational interaction between dark matter and dark energy, which could provide insights into the nature of dark energy and its evolution. The study aims to derive analytical expressions for the energy densities and to constrain these models using recent observational data. The goal is to determine if any of the IDE models are statistically preferred over the standard $\Lambda$CDM model. [动机是探索暗物质和暗能量之间可能存在非引力相互作用，这可能为暗能量的本质及其演化提供见解。研究旨在推导能量密度的解析表达式，并使用最新的观测数据对这些模型进行约束。目标是确定任何IDE模型是否在统计上优于标准的$\Lambda$CDM模型。]

Method: The method involves the use of the CPL parametrization for the dark energy equation of state, $w_\mathrm{de} = w_0 + w_a(1-a)$, and the background interaction kernel, $Q = 3H(\delta + \eta a)\rho_\mathrm{de}$, to derive closed analytical expressions for the energy densities of dark matter and dark energy. Observational constraints are then obtained using joint combinations of DESI DR2 baryon acoustic oscillations, Pantheon+ Type Ia supernovae, and Planck+ACT compressed cosmic microwave background likelihoods. [方法涉及使用CPL参数化来描述暗能量的状态方程，$w_\mathrm{de} = w_0 + w_a(1-a)$，以及背景相互作用核$Q = 3H(\delta + \eta a)\rho_\mathrm{de}$，推导出暗物质和暗能量能量密度的封闭解析表达式。然后，通过联合使用DESI DR2重子声波振荡、Pantheon+ Ia型超新星和Planck+ACT压缩宇宙微波背景似然性来获得观测约束。]

Result: For constant coupling models, the deviations from the $\Lambda$CDM model range from $2.7\sigma$ to $2.9\sigma$. For dynamical coupling models, the significance of these deviations is reduced to $1.3\sigma$--$1.5\sigma$. Bayesian model comparison shows that no IDE scenario is statistically preferred over the concordance $\Lambda$CDM model. [对于常数耦合模型，与$\Lambda$CDM模型的偏差范围从$2.7\sigma$到$2.9\sigma$。对于动态耦合模型，这些偏差的显著性降低到$1.3\sigma$--$1.5\sigma$。贝叶斯模型比较表明，没有IDE场景在统计上优于一致的$\Lambda$CDM模型。]

Conclusion: The conclusion is that while some IDE models exhibit deviations from the $\Lambda$CDM model, none of them are statistically preferred. The importance of reporting Bayesian evidence in addition to frequentist maximum-likelihood analyses is highlighted for robust cosmological claims. [结论是，尽管某些IDE模型表现出与$\Lambda$CDM模型的偏差，但它们在统计上都不优于$\Lambda$CDM模型。为了确保宇宙学声明的稳健性，除了频率主义最大似然分析外，报告贝叶斯证据的重要性被强调。]

Abstract: We investigate a hierarchy of interacting dark energy (IDE) models featuring a non-gravitational coupling between dark matter and dark energy. Specifically, we examine scenarios where the background interaction kernel, $Q = 3H(δ+ ηa)ρ_\mathrm{de}$, allows for both constant and dynamical coupling parameters. Adopting the CPL parametrization for the dark energy equation of state, $w_\mathrm{de} = w_0 + w_a(1-a)$, we derive closed analytical expressions for the energy densities of dark matter and dark energy. Afterwards, we obtain observational constraints using joint combinations of DESI DR2 baryon acoustic oscillations, Pantheon$+$ Type Ia supernovae, and Planck$+$ACT compressed cosmic microwave background likelihoods. For constant coupling models, we find parametric deviations from $Λ$ ranging from $2.7σ$ to $2.9σ$; however, for interactions with dynamical couplings, these significances are reduced to $1.3σ$--$1.5σ$. Ultimately, our Bayesian model comparison reveals that no investigated IDE scenario is statistically preferred over the concordance $Λ$CDM model. These results highlight the necessity of reporting Bayesian evidence alongside conventional frequentist maximum-likelihood analyses to ensure robust cosmological claims concerning dark energy evolution and interaction.

### [87] [On the Relation Between Field-Level Posteriors, Correlators, and their Likelihoods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25385)
*Massimo Pietroni,Fabian Schmidt*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper develops a field-level posterior for cosmological data, marginalizing over initial conditions and noise. It generalizes to any weakly non-Gaussian observable and is applicable to perturbative calculations, simulation-based predictions, and effective descriptions. The Fisher matrix is derived, and the information from the evolved field is organized into contributions from connected correlators. The study shows how cross-covariances among summaries reconstruct more of the full field-level information and applies this to BAO scale reconstruction.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to develop a comprehensive and non-perturbative framework for cosmological data analysis that can handle both Gaussian and weakly non-Gaussian observables. This framework aims to provide a unified approach to compare field-level and correlator-based inference, quantify information loss due to compression, and explore the role of stochasticity in large-scale structure data.

Method: The method involves developing a field-level posterior (FLP) by marginalizing over initial conditions and noise. The FLP is expanded around its Gaussian limit to derive a general expression for the Fisher matrix. The field-level information is then reorganized into contributions associated with the connected correlators of the evolved field. The study also includes an application to the BAO scale, demonstrating how the field contains all the information required for optimal reconstruction in the presence of noise.

Result: The results show that the standard Gaussian-covariance result for the power spectrum is recovered, and the Gaussian bispectrum likelihood reproduces the corresponding field-level contribution. Cross-covariances among summary statistics progressively reconstruct more of the full field-level information. For the BAO scale, the field-level posterior provides the necessary information for optimal reconstruction, and the initial field reconstruction arises naturally as a byproduct, yielding the optimal estimate of the initial conditions given the data and noise.

Conclusion: The conclusions are that the developed field-level posterior provides a unified framework to compare field-level and correlator-based inference, quantify the information loss induced by compression, and explore the role of stochasticity. The framework is applicable to a wide range of cosmological data and can be used to optimize the reconstruction of the initial field and the BAO scale in the presence of noise.

Abstract: We develop a field-level posterior for cosmological data by marginalizing over initial conditions and noise in a general forward model. While our focus is on large-scale structure data, the results generalize to any weakly non-Gaussian observable. Moreover, the construction is non-perturbative with respect to the forward model and applies equally well to perturbative calculations, simulation-based predictions, and more general effective descriptions. Expanding the FLP around its Gaussian limit, we derive a general expression for the Fisher matrix and reorganize the field-level information into contributions associated with the connected correlators of the evolved field. This makes explicit which terms are captured by likelihood analyses based on the power spectrum, the bispectrum, or finite sets of summary statistics, and which are lost under compression. We recover the standard Gaussian-covariance result for the power spectrum, show that the Gaussian bispectrum likelihood reproduces the corresponding field-level contribution, and show how cross-covariances among summaries progressively reconstruct more of the full field-level information. As an application to the BAO scale, we show how the field contains all the information required for its optimal reconstruction in the presence of noise, and identify the contributions in the FLP needed to attain this limit. We also show that the reconstruction of the initial field arises naturally as a byproduct of our approach, yielding the optimal estimate of the initial conditions given the data and the noise. Our results provide a unified framework to compare field-level and correlator-based inference, to quantify the information loss induced by compression, and to explore the role of stochasticity.

</details>


### [88] [Microlensing of fast and slow compact objects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25434)
*Manish Tamta,Nirmal Raj,Himanshu Verma*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper explores the constraints on non-standard compact objects using gravitational microlensing, considering a wide range of velocities and different velocity and spatial distributions. It derives mass-dependent constraints for these objects and examines the effects of varying observation cadences and source-lens-observer motion.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to extend the conventional approach of deriving gravitational microlensing constraints, which assumes lenses follow a Maxwell-Boltzmann distribution, to include a broader range of theoretical scenarios where compact objects have velocities that significantly deviate from those in virialized dark matter halos. This includes ultrarelativistic primordial black holes, mirror neutron stars, and other exotic objects.

动机是扩展传统的引力微透镜约束方法，该方法假设透镜遵循麦克斯韦-玻尔兹曼分布，以包括更广泛的理论场景，其中致密天体的速度显著偏离了在维里化暗物质晕中的速度。这包括超相对论原初黑洞、镜像中子星和其他奇异天体。

Method: The method involves deriving model-independent upper limits on the microlensing event rate and then obtaining mass-dependent constraints on the density of lens populations with speeds spanning $10^{-4}c$ to $10^{-1}c$. The analysis is performed for two benchmark velocity distributions (Maxwell-Boltzmann and Dirac delta) and two spatial distributions (uniform and NFW). The effect of the transverse motion of the source and observer relative to the lensing tube is also examined.

该方法涉及推导出模型无关的微透镜事件率上限，然后获得速度范围从$10^{-4}c$到$10^{-1}c$的透镜群体密度的质量依赖性约束。分析针对两种基准速度分布（麦克斯韦-玻尔兹曼和狄拉克δ函数）和两种空间分布（均匀和NFW）进行。还研究了相对于透镜管的源和观察者的横向运动的影响。

Result: The results show that the constraints on the density and masses of lens populations differ significantly from those derived under the assumption of standard dark matter. The study also demonstrates that increasing the cadence of observations can probe smaller masses for fast lenses without suppressing event rates due to finite source and wave optics effects. For slow lenses, the transverse motion of the source and observer becomes significant.

结果表明，对透镜群体密度和质量的约束与在标准暗物质假设下得出的约束有显著差异。研究还表明，增加观测频率可以探测到快速透镜的小质量，而不会由于有限源和波动光学效应抑制事件率。对于慢速透镜，源和观察者的横向运动变得显著。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that considering a wider range of velocities and spatial distributions for compact objects in gravitational microlensing studies opens up new regions of parameter space, leading to qualitatively different constraints compared to the standard dark matter scenario. The findings suggest that varying observation cadences and accounting for the relative motion of the source and observer are crucial for accurately constraining the properties of non-standard compact objects.

论文总结道，在引力微透镜研究中考虑致密天体更广泛的速度和空间分布，开辟了新的参数空间区域，导致与标准暗物质情景相比定性不同的约束。研究结果表明，改变观测频率和考虑源和观察者之间的相对运动对于准确限制非标准致密天体的性质至关重要。

Abstract: Gravitational microlensing constraints on non-standard compact objects are conventionally derived assuming lenses trace the dark matter halo with velocities following a Maxwell-Boltzmann distribution. However, a variety of theoretical scenarios predict populations of compact objects whose velocities deviate dramatically from those of virialized halo dark matter -- ultrarelativistic primordial black holes from cosmic string collapse, mirror neutron stars, gravitationally kicked black hole merger remnants, dark matter nuggets, free floaters ejected from gravitationally bound systems, disk-formed compact objects, and so on. For a given Einstein crossing time, the speed-mass degeneracy inherent in it means that fast (slow) lenses produce events at larger (smaller) masses than spanned by standard windows, opening qualitatively new regions of parameter space. After deriving model-independent upper limits on the microlensing event rate, we obtain mass-dependent constraints on the density of lens populations with speeds spanning $10^{-4}c-10^{-1}c$ from surveys of M31 by Subaru-HSC and the LMC by OGLE with different observing cadences. We do this for two benchmark velocity distributions -- Maxwell-Boltzmann and Dirac delta -- and two spatial distributions -- uniform and NFW, and exclude lens densities and masses that differ from dark matter constraints by orders of magnitude. We examine the effect of the transverse motion of the source and observer relative to the lensing tube, which becomes significant for our slow lenses. We also show that, unlike in dark matter searches, for our fast lenses an increase in the cadence of observations would probe smaller masses without suppression of event rates from the finite source and wave optics effects.
